## Page 8

Preface

I have great pleasure in presenting herewith Book II of Deva Keralam.

The encouragement given by the readers following appearance of Book I hereof is
thankfully acknowledged.

Although the original is popularly attributed to Achyuta, in actuality Venkatesa’s
name also appears as author at one stage. This Venkatesa need not be confused with
Sarvartha Chintamani’s author, vide notes given under sloka 1 infra. The original
authorship is actually divided as under:

Sloka No. 1 to 3407 by Achyuta in the first phase.

Sloka No. 1 to 4775 by Venkatesa in the later phase.

Thus there is a total of 8102 original slokas for which our arrangement of presentation
is as under:

Sloka 1 to sloka 2718 of Achyuta in Book I.

Sloka 2719 to sloka 3407 of Achyuta, and sloka 1 to sloka 1997 of Venkatesa in Book
I.

Rest of the work from slokas from No. 1998 to 4775 of Venkatesa is being brought
out as Book III.

In the present volumealso, there are many general principles applicable to the various
ascendants, apart from Nadiamsa discussions confined to given signs. The reader will be
able to understand the same as he progresses with the study of the text, remembering at the
same time the general outlines given in the preface for Book I.

Ihave every hope that the kind reader will forgive me for my shortcomings if any and
accord a favourable reception to my present efforts.

R. Santhanam

(Editor,

The Times Of Astrology)
9/1040 Govindpuri
Kalkaji

New Delhi 110 019
(India)

Tel 6462777

2719 - 27201/2. Trailokys Nadiamsa -
Capricorn Ascendant (Up to sloka 2769): (a) The

native of former half of Trailokya Nadiamsa in
Capricorn ascendant, in Mercury’s Trimsamsa, will

be the third issue of the family. His birth will be in the’

region of a great river, in a north-south spread street.
The house concerned will be in the eastern part (of the
town) and will be a north-facing one

(b) Find out in which Navamsa the 4th lord is
placed. The house of birth may (also) correspond to
the indications given by the said Rasi or one of its
trines.

Notes: (a) In Capricorn, Trailokya Nadiamsa
extends from 14° 48’ to 15° 0.

Ignore Mercury’s Trimsamsa condition and fol-
low only the relevant Nadiamsa stipulation.

(b) This is a general rule and can be applied to all
ascendants irrespective of the Nadiamsa, and is one
of the conditions stipulated for determining the home
of birth.

2721 - 27211/2. Prosperity: If the lord of the
ascendant is in the 2nd house as the 11th lord (Mars)
is inthe 4th house (in Aries), he will attain prosperity
after the thirtieth year of his age. This yoga will also
give him a physique which is free from diseases and
is strong,

Notes: The effects given apply to the whole of
Capricorn ascendant irrespective of the Nadiamsa as
could be seen below.

Prosperity: Saturnin the 2nd house in Aquarius,
while Mars is in the 4th house will assure prosperity

Deva Keralam 1

right from youth. The influence of Saturn onthe 10th
house, Libra, is passed on through Mars. By himself,
Mars is a functional benefic for Capricorn. When he
is related to Saturn and the 10th house, the native of
Capricorn ascendant is sure to rise without obstacles.

Healthy Body: As the lord of the 11th house, 6th
from the 6th house, Mars has a definite say on health,
like Mercury the 6th lord. The association of Mars
with ascendant lord, Saturn, the latter placed in
Moolatrikona in the 2nd, is a plus point. Such a
person will be free from illness and will attain
prosperity.

Mercury in Aries, while Saturn is in the 2nd, will
also give similar effects for Capricorn natives. But
prosperity, though certain, will be through certain
odds caused by inimical activities as Mercury is,also
the 6th lord, and gets his placement in a bitter
enemy’s sign. Certainty in prosperity is because
Mercury is the lord of the 9th for Capricorn and
bosom friend of Saturn.

2722 - 2723. Saturn in Pisces: Should Saturn be
found in Pisces, witha dual Navamsa, the subject will
be in the grip of penury during his childhood. He will
enjoy sound health and prosperity in his youth. After
25 years of age, goddess Lakshmi will bless his
family.

Notes : Yugmamsaka inthis case is dual navamsa,
and not specifically Gemini, as Pisces Rasiis referred
to. Saturn in Pisces will get one of the other three dual
Navamsa, viz. Virgo, Sagittarius and Pisces.

The hints given hereof apply to Capricorn as-
cendant, in general. By his placement in the 3rd
house, Saturn will aspect the 9th house, denoting
father. Wealth or poverty in childhood depends on
father (or mother). Saturn in Pisces with Virgo
Navamsa will be in the 9th from natal ascendant. In
Sagittarius Navamsa, he will be in the 12th from natal
ascendant and in Pisces Navamsa, he will be in the
3rd in Vargottama. Saturn’s placement in Jupiter’s
sign or Navamsa will produce some adverse effects
about father, as Mercury, the lord of the 9th, does. got
## Page 19

2 Chandra Kala Nadi

go well with Jupiter. Saturn in relation to the 9th from
a sign of Jupiter, for Capricorn, may in the initial
stage not give money through father, but is bound to
give good effects in the long run by virtue of his good
position and good rulership. For Saturn is a slow
planet in revealing good effects. As the lord of the
ascendant, he assumes the onus of protecting the 9th
house.

In my view, we should add Leo Navamsa as well
in which case father’s poverty will be intense.

In analysing a bhava vis a vis a planet’s place-
ment we better take into note two important factors:
The occupant’s relationship with the significator of
that bhava, on the one hand. On the other hand, the
relationship of the Rasi dispositor and Navamsa
dispositor of the occupant with a given significator.

Generally, Saturn related to the 9th is notso good
as he is quite allergic to the Sun, the significator of
father.

2725 - 27311/2. Capricorn Ascendant: (a) One
born in this ascendant, in the former halfof Trailokya
Nadiamsa, will be good-looking. intelligent, elo-
quent, be endowed with charming face and eyes, be
fortunate, religious and will enjoy effects of Raja
Yoga. He will be fond of superior ascetics and will
worship gods and Brahmins. he will eat limited food,
will speak within a limit and will sleep for limited
hours. He will conquer his Senses, and will be skillful
in understanding others’ thoughts. He will beautify
himself with ornaments and also be fond of orna-
ments. He will be an evil person to the evil and will
be unkind to unkind people. He will be bereft of
paternal fortunes (or happiness) and will have self-
earned wealth.

(b) If the 4th lord (noted in Rasi diagram) is inthe
9th place in Navamsa (i.e 9th counted from Navamsa
ascendant), he will be skillful inlaw and philosophy.
The native of the former halfof the subject Nadiamsa
(without reference to 4th lord above) will be helpful
to all, will be endowed with valour, adventure and
fame, be fond of listening to mythological stories, be
ever wealthy, well-disposed to the poor, will worship
Lord Siva by vows and fasts, and be devoted to Lords
Vishnu and Siva. He will ever take to virtuous path
and will have excellent religious attainments. He will
gain through agriculture, quadrupeds etc. He will
lord over villages and lands.

Notes: (a) Applicable only to the subject
Nadiamsa.

(b) Skill in law and philosophy applies to the 4th
lord’s position as specified in the text while the rest
applies to first half of Trailokya Nadiamsa with the
above mentioned placement of the lord of the 4th,
Mars.

For any ascendant, the 4th lord placed in the 9th
from the natal ascendant or from the Navamsa as-
cendant, will be good for legal and philosophical
attainments.

2732-27331/2. Co-born: (a) If the 3rd lord Jupi-
ter is in the 6th house from the ascendant Capricorn,
ora trine thereof (i.c. 2nd/10th), the subject will have
neither an older co-born, nor a younger one.

(b) If the 2nd (Aquarius) is occupied by Saturn,
he will have a sister endowed with longevity, and
anotherasynonymof difficulties, butliving ina good
abode, and yet another endowed withsons and daugh-
ter.

Notes: (a) For Capricorn ascendant, if Jupiter is
placed in Aquarius, Gemini, or Libra, one will be the
lonely child of the family.

(b) Obviously this position of Satuin “enotes
three sisters, while Jupiter in 3rd altogether ceprives
one of co-born. We have no hints as to what Saturn
will do in this regard if he is placed in Gemini/Libra.
However, my suggestion is that Saturn as exalted
ascendant lord will normally not make the native a
lonely issue, nor wil] he do so while in Gemini, being
in direct aspect to the 3rd.

2734 - 2735. Mars: Should the 4th lord Mars be
conjunct Saturn or be in aspect to Saturn, the native
of the subject Nadiamsa will lose his mother in his
very childhood. If Mars be with the Sun in Aries, the
latter in his sign of exaltation, the native will be
wealthy with elephants.

Notes: Mars in the 4th with Saturn’s connection
is bad for mother’s life-span, only when the ascend-
ing degree in Capricorn is Trailokya Nadiamsa.
Otherwise in general for this ascendant, Mars placed
in the 4th with Saturn’s connection cannot cause
short-life for the mother of the native.

Mars and the Sunin Aries isa yoga forwealth and

prosperity for Capricorn natives in general.

2736. Mars-Saturn-Moon: If these three plan-
ets conjoin in the 9th or 10th house, the native will be
a skillful person. He will gainconveyances, bea poet,
will hold the assemblage of men in charm and be
endowed with four kinds of traditional conveyances
(viz. chariots, horses, elephants and men-borne
palanquins).

Notes: The conjunction referred to here should
occur in Virgo/Libra, and is of three angular lords. It
will be far superior for a Capricom native occurring
in the 10th, the best of the angles for that matter,
where Saturn’s exaltation will add further weightage.
Asa result, the subject will receive the above effects
in an increased manner.

This yoga is also applicable to Capricorn ascend-
ant in general as it is conjunction of lords of the Ist,
4th and the 7th in the 9th or the 10th. But for the
Nadiamsa, poetic skills may not be so evident in the
10th house, Libra. Inthe 9th house, apart from giving
the results mentioned in the original, poetic skills
may be abundant as the Moon, signifying imagina-
tion, occupies Virgo, a fertile sign of intellect, and the
3 planets aspect the 3rd house, ruled by Jupiter.

"Poetic skills" denoted need not necessarily
confine to poetry. The 3rd house denotes one’s
ability as a writer and even as a singer.

Jupiter in Pushkaramsa will enjoy riches right from

2738 - 2739. Marriage: During the rulership of
the 2nd dasa, when Jupiter transits a trine counted
from the sign occupied by 10th lord (Venus), the
native’s marriage will take place with a girl hailing
from the southern or south-eastern part of his birth
place. These results have elaborately been narrated in
Sukra Nadi in the chapter devoted to the Bhava
concerned, i.e. 7th house.

Notes: Although the text qualifies Venus by his
10th lordship, he is al!-importnat in marriage as he is
the significator in principle. For any ascendant,
Jupiter’s trina] transit is essential with reference to
the following:

a) Venus. b) 7th lord from ascendant. c) the
Moon. d) the 7th Jord from the Moon.

If Jupiter transit trinally with reference to more
than one of the above four, marriage will be expe-
dited.

There are other factors like Navamsa ascendant
involving Jupiter’s transit. But the above is the
beginning point of the probe.

The girl hailing froma givendirection is peculiar
to the Nadiamsa in question.

2740. Single Marriage: If the 7th lord Moon is
ina fixed sign with a fixed Navamsa (not necessarily
Vargothama), while the significator (Venus) is also
in a fixed sign, it is said, there will be only one
marriage to the native of the subject Nadiamsa.

Notes: This clue about the native remaining with
one marriage nullifying other combinations for a
remarriage can be applied in respect of any ascend-
ant. Venus, the Moon, 7th lord and ascendant lord
being in fixed sign and fixed Navamsa disallow a
remarriage. This however does not define the quality
and length of first marriage.

2741 - 27431/2. Other Effects: (a) If the 7th lord
Moon (counted from natal ascendant) is in the 8th
house in Navamsa (i.e. inthe 8th place from Navamsa
ascendant), he will be sinful by joining others’
women.

(b) One bom in the former half of Trailokya
Nadiamsa in Capricorn ascendant, having Venus in
Somavathi Nadiamsa will have secretive lust for
sexual pleasures. He will be so sexually excited as to
join his spouse.even on prohibited days.

(c) If Venus is in Kanthaa Nadiamsa, he will be
full of merry during sexual union.

(d) Ifthe 10th lord (Venus) is in the 4th (Aries).
the subject of the said Kanthaa Nadiamsa will per-
form good deeds and will have good conduct.

Notes: (a) The 7th lord fromany natal ascendant
occupying the 8th place from Navamsa ascendant
will show want of morality, more on the art of the
spouse. The text takes specifically the Moon into
account as she is the 7th lord fro Capricorn.

(b) Prohibited days for sexual union, by Satsras
in gencral are: 1. Ekadasi (11th lunar day) in cither
fortnight.

2. Amavasya (30th lunar day).

3. Four days from the commencement of a
woman’s periods.

There are many more stipulations. The above is
a brief account.

(c) Kanthaa Nadiamsa occurs as under:

Movable signs 06° 00' to 06° 12'
Fixed signs 23° 48 to 24° 00!
Common signs 21° 00' to 21° 12’

2750 - 2752. Trailokya Nadiamsa - Capricorn
Ascendant: The subject will beget a daughter when
Jupiter transits the 8th house (Leo). After the age of
35, his prosperity will be onthe rise and will cause the
mercy of goddess Lakshmi. Either his 39 year, or 38th
year, will endanger his wife but she will recover
health early. The subject will obtain rulership, bap-
piness to his men and increase of wealth and grains.
Sages say, the dasa of Venus, who is in aspect to a
benefic, will beget him the mercy of goddess Lakshmi
and royal kind of comforts.

Notes: The dasa of Venus related to a natural
benefic being able to confer good effects can apply to
Capricorn in general. Such dasa will cause wealth,
including properties, comforts, honour, name, fame
etc.

to Venus dasa.

2753 - 2757. Capricorn ascendant - Dasa Ef-
fects: (a) The second half 10th lord’s dasa will cause

great happiness, enmity with army chief, and destruc-
tion of relatives of the native.
## Page 23

(b) The concluding part of the fourth dasa will
cause distress. In the dasa which is the fifth in order,
the subject will be fond of listening to mythological
stories, will win the king’s heart and acquire wealth.

(c) Inthe Moon’s sub period during Sun’s major
period, the king will be involved in quarrel. When the
Sun is in his southerly course, great quarrels will
strike in the western part of the country. There will be
fear to the kings of Chola, Konkana, Kashmir and
Mlechcha. Fierce battle, untimely death, and loss of
army will come to pass, after which calm will exist.

Notes: (a) For Capricorn ascendant, the dasa of
Venus will cause increased happiness in the second
half but adverse effects like enmity with army chief
(i.e. men in administration) apart from death of near
and dear.

(b) The 4th dasa will inflict miseries before it
comes to an end. The dasa which is the fifth in
sequence will cause interest in mythology, (denotes
spiritual progress), governmental favours and wealth.

(c) These are irrelevant and interpolated.

2761 - 2762. The Sun in an Angle: (a) Ifthe Sun
occupies an angle counted from Capricorn ascendant
which has Trailokya Nadiamsa, the dasa which is the
fifth in sequence will cause a great deal of fortunes.
The first half of the said dasa will produce much
happiness. The subject in the dasa will acquire power
backed by royal authority. He will establish a colony
for Brahmins. (b) When Jupiter transits the 8th,
religious attainments will be excellent.

Notes: (a) The 8th lord in an angle from the
ascendant (i.e. 1st, 4th, 7th or 10th) or fromthe Moon
as the case may be will help the 5th dasa to give
beneficial effects for any ascendant in general. It is
quite difficult to explain the logic behind such an
experience. But I have seen specifically some horo-
scopes where this position gave specified effects.

(b) For Capricorn ascendant, the transit of Jupi-
ter in the 8th in Leo is supposed to give beneficial
effects as could be observed. However ifthe Moonbe
in Capricorn, this may not exactly apply.

2764. In the region of Mahodadhi, there will be
## Page 24

strife (?) If the 8th lord is exalted and be in the

2765. Raja Yoga: The 9th lord exalted and
joining the significator (Jupiter - the significator for
Dharma ruled by the 9th house, as the reference to
here is Dharma) along with a friendly planet. The
sign in question should not be an evil house, nor
inimical (to companions). He could be also conjunct
oraspected by another benefic or his dispositor. Then
the subject will construct many villages, tanks, tem-
ple-towers, towns and parks. He will be in the com-
pany of virtuous men and will win the hearts of
superior kings.

Notes: The sloka has two expressions which are
not relevant and which affect the continuity of the
relevantand stipulated conditions. These are: Mitrasya
cha uchche stithe = posited in a sign that exalts the
friend of, here, Venus or the sign Aries which exalts
the Sun (Mitra). Swaamina means the lord. These are
omitted in translation.

The essence of the yoga thus is, for Capricorn
ascendant, the conjunction of Venus with Jupiter
supported by another benefic viz. Mercury or a
friendly planet in a good house is a powerful Raja
yoga as a result of which the native will construct
villages & C. That is, he will render social services,
will be inthe company of good menand bea recipient
of royal or governmental favours.

ant, will have his timely death. Ifatall he survives due

the three signs commencing from Taurus, or with the
Sun in Capricorn. The final moment will be in the
early hours of Friday.

Vaidik Brahmin’s family. He will attain emancipa-
tion after the next birth if Jupiter aspects the 12th (for
the Trailokya Nadiamsa native being discussed).

Notes: The following two lines out of tke above
four lines have not been provided with translation as
a part of the text.

Randradhipa dasa kaale gadaamse viprakaalage
which means “For native of Gada Nadiamsa, first
quarter, in the dasa of the 8th lord”.

Viprakaale phalam sathyam prathyaksham Deva
Keralam which means: The results stated for Vipra
Kaala (i.e. first quarter of a given Nadiamsa) in Deva
Keralam will be experienced in actuality.

These two lines are an interpolation and not
connected with the present Nadiamsa in any manner
and hence secluded.

oldest nor the youngest issue. That is he will have
both older and younger co-born. This rule can be
applied to any ascendant.

Angles to the 11th house are: the 2nd, 5th, 8th
and 11th.

2791 - 2794 1/2. Father: Should the 5th lord
Moon be in Capricorn in the company of Venus, the
native of Suprabha Nadiamsa will have a long living
father. (Independent of this yoga) the native of
former half will see his father in danger in the
concluding phase of 3rd dasa or in the first sub period
of 4th dasa. The subject of second half of this
Nadiamsa will incur danger to father in the second
dasa.

Notes: The text dealing with father in respect of
second half of Suprabha Nadiamsa repeats twice but
with slight changes. Thus the translation is confined
to mere second dasa, leaving aside reference to first/
second half of the second dasa.

From these three slokas we understand that the
native of first half of this Nadiamsa will have his
father alive as long as to the end of 3rd dasa or
beginning of 4th dasa while the subject of second half
of this Nadiamsa will lose his father in the very
second dasa. This much we can differentiate.

2796 - 27971/2. Deformity: (a) For a native of
former half of this Nadiamsa, Venus in the 7th will
cause acquisition of a spouse with physical deform-
ity.

(b) The native will be deaf if Ketu joins the 7th
lord Mercury.

(c) To overcome these ills, propitiations as pre-
scribed be done.

Notes: (a) Physical deformity to spouse may
specially apply to Venus placed in the 7th for Pisces

ascendant, Nadiamsa cited. Even otherwise, Venus
in the 7th in debility cannot be of an asset in respect
of marriage. Such yoga will cause some notable
blemish for the spouse apart from delay in marriage.

(b) If Ketu and Mercury are in close orbs, this
conjunction - of Ketu and Mercury - will cause
deafness in case of a Pisces subject.

(c) The remedies are not mentioned clearly.
However, for blemish at “a”, the planet Venus, and
for blemish at “b” ihe planet Ketu should be propiti-
ated by suitable Mantras and prayers.

2798 -2803. (a) One born in the second half will
beget a wicked spouse, who will however be free
from diseases, with a strong physique.

(b) His counterpart, i.e. the native of first
half of the subject Nadiamsa, Pisces ascendant, will
have two wives.

(c) Mercury in the Aroodha of the Sth, in
the company of Ketu and in Aries Navamsa will
cause obstacles in acquisition of progeny. (Some
texts read Putrabhave while some use the expression
Putraarodhe. Sth Aroodha is correct expression, as
Mercury in 5th in Cancer does not obtain Aries
Navamsa.) The same effect will come to pass if the
ascendant Pisces begets the aspect of Saturn and falls
in Scorpio Navamsa. To remedy this ill, donation of
an image of the zodiac be done. The image of the
zodiacand the planets be worshipped as prescribed in
the Sastras. The names of the vowels, including the
## Page 28

Deva Keralam 11

name of Abhijit Nakshatra be written on the image of
zodiac and be given away to an astrologer. Then the
blemish in respect of progeny will be warded off.

Notes: “a” and “b” are clear.

(c) For Pisces ascendant, the 5th Aroodha will be
so many signs away as the Moonis from Cancer (with
exceptions mentioned by me in my notes in Brihat
Parasara Hora, Part 1, English translation). Mercu-
ry’s position should be in such place along with Ketu.
Unless Mercury in the yoga obtains Aries navamsa,
obstacles in acquiring progeny should not be ex-
pected. Alternatively Saturn should aspect Pisces
which should ascend between 13° 20' and 16° 40!
getting Scorpio Navamsa. Remedy suggested is do-
nation of a zodiac’s image to an astrologer. The
image should contain inscription of the 28 Nakshatras
including Abhijit.

2804 - 2806. Dasa Effects: (a) In the sub period
of an obstructive (or adversc) planet during the major
rulership of the 8th lord, the subject will lose relatives
of his age group.

(b) The 2nd half of the 4th dasa will cause
him great happiness.

(c) For birth in the former half of the
subject Nadiamsa, see if the 8th lord’s dasa is in
operation. If so, when Jupiter comes to Taurus in
transit, death of mother be declared. So also in the
intervals of Venus and Rahu (without reference to
Jupiter’s transit).

Notes: (a) Obstructive planets for Pisces ascend-
ant are Venus, Mercury and Saturn. The sub period of
one of these planets, or that of occupants thereof will
cause danger to relatives in the main period of Venus.
The Nadiamsa need not be a considerationas the dasa
of 8th lord for any ascendant is capable of causing

grief.

(b) This axiom is a broad clue to this Nadiamsa.

(c) Linking death of mother in 8th lord’s dasa to
the transit of Jupiter applies only to the subject
Nadiamsa.

2807. Lord of the 8th: (a) Should the 8th lord
be inthe 1 1th (ie. Venus in Capricorn) the native will
be very fortunate. In the end of such 8th lord’s dasa,
his son will fall sick.

(b) The 8th loid Venus obtaining the 4th
place in Navamsa will also give financial acquisition
apart from causing a second marriage.

‘Notes: Two combinations involving Venus are
discussed. (a) By being inthe 1 1th house, he will give
fortunes to the native in general, and sickness in the
concluding part of Venus Dasa. Venus in the 11th
house for any ascendant except Scorpio is generally
a contributory factor for fortunes. The degree of
fortunes will depend on the circumstances prevailing
in a given case. Sickness to a son is applicable only
to the subject Nadiamsa.

(b) Without reference to Venus in Capri-
corn, his occupying the 4th house from Navamsa
ascendant will give financial gains and second mar-
riage to the native. Venus being a Yoga Karaka, his
occupation of the 4th from Navamsa ascendant will
cause financial acquisition. The issue of second
marriage will get confirmed if the Navamsa ascend-
ant is particularly a dual sign - one of Virgo, Sagitta-
rius and Pisces. Here again, the Nadiamsa may many
times be not relevant.

2812 - 28141/2, Venus - Mars: The conjunction
of Venus and Mars for ¢ Suprabha Nadiamsa native
will cause misfortunes, like enmity, in the dasa which

is fourth from birth. To overcome such misfortunes,
donation ofan image of goddess Lakshmi be resorted
to. Asa result, long-lasting progress will be obtained.
In the abseace of this, the person’s household will be
wholly deprived of the mercy of goddess Lakshmi.
The said remedy wiil bring auspicious effects in royal
service and cause destruction of enemies. Later on
due to mercy of King’s minister, the subject will
obtain progeny (?).

Notes: The conjunction of Venus - Mars for the
subject native will be destruciive in the 4th dasa, if
remedy as prescribed is not done. That is, this
conjunction will prove devastating in this context.

Obtainment of progeny after the remedy should
be read without “mercy of king’s minister”.

placed in Sundari Nadiamsa in aspect to or associa-

-tion with Jupiter, one born in Vipra Kala (of Kalusha

2820 through 2887. When the Moon feztures in the
discussion generally it is prescribed to be Sundari
Nadiamsa (of any sign), unless and until specified.
The text’s authority is Chandra Nadi.

pio and Aquarius. In these signs, Kalusha Nad‘amsa
rules from 24° 12' to 24° 28’. Its first half is from 24°
12' to 24° 18' and second half is from 24° 18' to 24°
24! of arc in immovable signs.

The Moon is required to be in Sundari Nadiamsa
of any sign for which please refer to sloka 1584, Book
1 (page 143).

2826 - 2827. Leo/Virgo Navamsa: Birth in an

cable.

2830 - 2831. Jupiter in an Angle: For birth in
an immovable ascendant with immovable Navamsa,
see if Jupiter occupies an angle with Cancer Nav-
amsa. If so, the native’s father will be wealthy,
sickly, and will have a dark and emaciated body. He
will experience poverty in childhood and be devoid
of older coborn.

Notes: The Nadiamsa is not relevant. The as-
cendantshould be inanimmovable sign with immov-

Jupiter is in an angle from the natal ascendant, with
exaltation Navamsa. Needless to mention, the posi-
tion of Jupiter in the sign Aquarius will not grant him
exaltation in Navamsa. So he should be in any other
immovable sign as an angle.

Many good effects about father are discussed
involving Jupiter, who is the 8th lord for Taurus/Leo.
ForScorpio and Aquarius he is the 2nd lord, ruling the
opposite sign of the 8th. His retrogression is specially
discussed again about father in the ensuing verses but
with the use of subject Nadiamsa.

tion, fever and will be much grieved. The first dasa
will prove dangerous for him. Only after the third
year, happiness will prevail.

2844 - 2846. Mercury occupying his own sign

alnng with the Sun, Saturn in Ascendant, Jupiter and
the Moon Leo, Ketu and Venus inthe 3rd, Rahu inthe
9th - this type of planetary array will give great
happiness to the native. But his childhood will be
marked by difficulties. He will have limited progeny.
This is according to Bhargava school of thought. His
brother will also beget similar effects. He will be
equal to a king, wealthy, and prosperous either after
20 or after 32 years of age. For 10 or 16 years (half
of 200132) from the birth of the native, his father will
see prosperity. After a similar number of years, bis
prosperity will decline. Happiness will revive two
years later.

Notes: By a careful study, we can understand
that this horoscope should contain Taurus ascendant
with Saturn therein, Mercury and the Sun in Gemini,
Venus Ketu in Cancer, Jupiter and the Moon in Leo
while Rahu is in Capricorn.

Rabu in the 9th for any ascendant is found to
cause childhood with want of financial comforts in
the family.

2851 - 2854. Birth in Kalusha Nadiamsa while
the Moon is in Sundari Nadiamsa will cause the

the native will become exceedingly wealthy. During

Cancer, his mother will be endangered. She will have
seen brothers. The subject will have a step-mother.

2855. Jupiter in Sundari Nadiamsa: For a
birth in the second half of Kalusha Nadiamsa (of an
immovable ascendant), if Jupiter occupies Sundari
Nadiamsa, predict marriage in the very first dasa.

Notes: The question of marriage in the very first
should be wisely made depending upon the balance
at birth. Alternatively, the next dasa should be
chosen. The text simply implies an early marriage.

2856 - 2858. Obstacles to Marriage: Venus
should be ina dual sign with Libra Navamsa. The
ascendant should be an immovable one with immov-
able Navamsa for birth in Kalusha Nadiamsa. Then
the native’s marriage will face obstacles. For birth in
the same Nadiamsa, Saturn aspecting the 3rd house
will also cause similar obstacles. Marriage will
however occur after two or three weeks of trial. The
bride will have no father at the time of the marriage
of the said native.

avoided for one year (obviously one time fasting is

2867 - 2869. Father: For one born in the latter
part of Kalusha Nadiamsa (in an immovable sign)
father’s death will occur within one-and-a-half year
of birth of the native. His ninth yearwill cause mental
distress while the eighth year grief. Father will be
endangered in the native’s eighth year in case of first
half of the subject Nadiamsa. The native’s father will
take to ascetism following a calamity in the end of
first dasa or in the first sub period of the second dasa
of the native of first half of this Nadiamsa.

system of numerical.

2873 - 2874. Paternal Uncle: Jupiter ruling the
11th house (ascendant being Taurus or Aquarius, an
immovable sign) if aspected by Saturn and begets
Cancer Navamsa denotes that the native will have
only one paternal uncle. The uncle in question will
be extremely intelligent, will have two wives, will
husband women given to anger, and be skillful in
differentiating between the just and unjust. He will
suffer penury during his childhood and will enjoy
happiness in the second half of his life.

2878 - 2880. One born in the second half of
Kalusha Nadiamsa will be somewhat attached to his
coborn. In his fourth dasa, he will incur enmity with
his brother. In the 3rd dasa he will be greatly happy.
If the Sth lord joins the Sun while the 7th lord is with
the aspect of Saturn, the third dasa will cause of
children out of which (only) two or three will survive.

Notes: The two lines relating to sloka 2879 are
not included in the above translation as they are
irrelevant. The first line means: In the second dasa’s
last one-third part there will be family division. This
line is a repetition of sloka 2875. The second line of
sloka 2879 relates to Pisces ascendant, a dual sign,
and that too is partial. The meaning is “The Moon in
the 12th in Aquarius, with Aries Navamsa” and is
incomplete.

2881 - 2887. In the sub period of Jupiter in the
second dasa the ruler of the native’s country will be
destroyed (?) The dasa of 9th lord will give good
effects. For immovable Navamsa, results should be
known through other sources. In the dasa of 8th lord
and in the sub period of 12th lord, for birth in former
half, near Mahodadhi region ..... The king will be
involved in quarrel when Saturn transits the Rasi or
trine, identical with the Navamsa occupied by as-
cendant lord or 8th lord. The country will reel under
drought and lack of rains. One born in Kalusha
Nadiamsa in Pisces ascendant, will die in the 4th
dasa. In his 58th year he will obtain name and fame.
According to Amsayu method he will live upto 61,
with the Sun moving in his southerly course, in
Cancer, Scorpio, Pisces (?) or Virgo. The conjunc-
tion of Venus-Saturn will cause death of the native of
Kalusha Nadiamsa. These effects culled out from
Chandra Nadi, produced in Deva Keralam will bear
truth.

Note: Most of the above seven slokas are either
defective, or meaningless, or wrongly appended.

The intelligent reader will take only applicable views
ignoring other parts of these slokas.

2888 - 2892. Kanthaa Nadiamsa - Pisces As-
cendant: (a) One bom in this part of the zodiac with
Saturn in Scorpio (in the 9th house) will lose his
father in childhood and will be bereft of after- born.
He will incur grief due to loss of elder brother in the
middle of his life. He will have two sisters, out of
whom one will be long-lived, endowed with sons and
happiness. He will obtain happiness in early days by
serving a king. Afterwards he will go to forests (or
will migrate) and will serve a mean king. He will
have two wives and good (male) children.

(b) Due to Amala Yoga (caused by a benefic
being placed in the 10th in Sagittarius), he will obtain
men-borne conveyances by performing rituals as
prescribed in the Vedas.

(c) In the 4th dasa, he will be greatly happy. In
the middle part thereof, he will earn wealth. In the
second half of the said dasa, he will beget convey-
ance and villages (i.e. some properties or position of
eminence). (Dhaatamse is a wrong addition in sloka
2892. Dhaatamsa is cited as Ghaatamsa in some
parts of the text.)

Notes: (a) The above results for Satum’s posi-
tion in Scorpio should apply only when Kanthaa
Nadiamsa rises in Pisces. Otherwise Satum in the 9th
for Pisces will just give troubles to father, and a
second marriage to the native (11th lord aspecting the
11th house, is a slow moving planet.

(b) Amala yoga giving conveyance can be ap-
plied to any part of Pisces, and also to other ascend-
ants,

(c) The effects cited here should be read de-

linking Saturn in the 9th, and also Amala Yoga.
These just relate to Kanthaa nadiamsa, Pisces as-
cendant. Additional effects are cited in slokas 2897-
98.

Kanthaa Nadiamsa occurs twice in each sign.

Movable sign: once from 6° to 6° 12', and again
from 10° to 10° 12’.

Immovable sign: once from 23° 48' to 24° 0'", and
again from 19° 48' to 20° 0’.

Common sign: once from 25° to 25° 12', and
again from 21° to 21° 12'.

2897 - 2898. Pisces Ascendant - Kanthaa
Nadiamsa (Effects continued from sloka 2892):
The subject in his fifth dasa will lose his spouse. His
eldestson will be long-lived and his spouse will suffer
from abdominal diseases. He will beget many dead
children, and will have two full sisters apart from
(unspecified number of) half sisters. He will be
devoted to his father and be honourable.

2899. Maala Nadiamsa: The native of Maala

2900 - 29001/2. Movable ascendant: Fora birth

in Kantha Nadiamsa in movable ascendant (specifi-

‘cally Cancer), if Mercury occupies Somavathi

Nadiamsa in Virgo in the company of the Sun, the

subject will be devoid of an elder coborn. His birth
will be near a great river in a town.

Notes: From sloka 2900 to 2912, the text deals
with Kanthaa Nadiamsa, Cancer ascendant, in con-
tradiction to the chapter’s caption. This will be clear
from sloka 2907 and 2911 infra. In given cases, these
hints apply to other movable ascendants also.

For Kantha Nadiamsa, see notes given under
sloka 2888 supra.

And the next chapter from sloka 2913 also deals
with Cancerascendant, but witha different Nadiamsa.

“Somasuthamse” should read as “Somalatamse”

meaning: "in Somalatha Nadiamsa” the same as
Somavathi Nadiamsa which in Virgo rules from 3° 0'
to 3° 12’. The planet Mercury should be in this space
in the company of the Sun (whose degree is unspeci-
fied) while the ascendant is in Cancer in Kanthaa
nadiamsa. As a result, the subject will be the first
issue without an older coborn.

2907 - 2908. The native of second half of this
Nadiamsa will prosper in the third dasa. One belong-
ing to the former half will have a long living mother,
if Venus ruling the 4th house occupies Libra itself,
with Aries Navamsa. But if the birth be in the 2nd
half, death of mother will occur in the very childhood
of the native.

Notes: For Cancer ascendant Venus in the 4th in
Libra is a contributing factor for mother’s longevity.
His position simultaneously in Aries Navamsa will
give longevity to mother in case of birth in the first
half of Kanthaa Nadiamsa, in Cancer ascendant,
while the same position will cause loss of mother in
childhood in case of birth in second half of the
Nadiamsa in Cancer ascendant.

Thus Venus in Aries navamsa, being in the sign
Libra, implies some danger to mother in general.

2909 -29091/2. Mars in 5th: For Cancerascend-

is in a fixed sign which gives him Sagittarius Nav-
amsa position, the subject will be greatly endangered

in the Sth year. Additional effects thereof will be:
danger to mother, and acquisition of a step-mother
(i.e. another marriage for father).

Notes: For Cancer ascendant, Mars in the 2nd
(Leo), Sth (Scorpio) or 8th (Aquarius), getting Sag-
ittarius Navamsa is discussed above. Thus Mars
should be in one of the following spaces for a native
of Cancer:

1. Leo 26° 40' to 30° 00'

2. Sco 16° 40' to 20° 00'

3. Aqu 06° 40' to 10° 00'

2910 - 2912. Father & Paternal Uncle: (a)
Jupiter ruling the 9th and related to Saturn by aspect
or conjunction will cause destruction of father in the
22nd or 23rd year of age.

(b) The 11th lord Venus, denoting paternal un-
cle, placed in Libra with Aries Navamsa will cause
five paternal uncles. Out of themtwo will be famous.
(This rule involving Venus applies to second half of
Kanthaa Nadiamsa, Cancer ascendant.)

(c) Incase of birth informerhalf of this Nadiamsa,
there will be no paternal uncles at all, i.e. the father
will be the lonely male issue of his family.

Notes: (a) The 9th lord Jupiteraspected by, orin
the company of Saturn will cause early death of
father.

(b) and (c) - Applicable only to the subject
Nadiamsa.

2920 - 2923. Dasa Effects: (a) The native (of Sri
Pankaja Nadiamsa in Cancer ascendant) will obtain
great happiness inthe 2nd halfof 2nd dasa. He as well
as his relatives will become famous. He will acquire
wealth.

(b) One born in the first half will have increase
of wealthand grains. He will have religious advance-
ments in the 4th dasa and become famous in royal
service.

(c) The third dasa will bestow prosperity on the
native of the second half of this Nadiamsa.

(d) Fora native of Cancer ascendant with Pisces
Navamsa the 8th lord (Saturn) placed in the 11th will
give Raja Yoga effects in the third dasa, apart from
men-borne conveyances. He will befriend ministers
involved in royal service.

Notes: (a) Generally, irrespective of first or
second half, the native of Pankaja nadiamsa, Cancer
will be wealthy et cetera.

(b) The subject of the first half of the said
Nadiamsa will have indestructible wealth (as against
the native of 2nd half) and will enjoy religious
advancements in his fourth dasa. These are peculiar
to first half of Pankaja Nadiamsa birth.
## Page 40

Deva Keralam 23

(c) As forthe second half of native, his speciality
will be general progress in the third dasa.

(d) Ignoring the Nadiamsa condition, one be-
longing to Cancer ascendant with Pisces Navamsa
and having Saturn in Taurus will have advancement
in the third dasa & C.

2924. Eighth Lord in 11th: For a native of Sri
Pankaja Nadiamsa in Cancer, the 8th lord Saturn in
the 11th will give abundant fortunes. Inthe end of the
(third) dasa, the native will see his progeny in sick-
ness, But he will gain wealth. There will be second
marriage for the native (during the third dasa).

Notes: In my opinion, here the Nadiamsa condi-
tion is an interruption and the effects cited should be
read in continuity of sloka 2923 above. Thus, when
the navamsa ascendant is Pisces fora Cancer nativity,
fortunes will be galore. Else, Saturn in the 11th, as
the 8th lord, will not be so helpful for gains (fortunes).
The key is Pisces Navamsa rising.

Further, the subject will have two marriages as
the 7th lord is in the 11th house in Taurus. And his

children will be diseased. Both these effects will
occur in the third dasa.

dasa when Mars is in Aries in a Cancer nativity.

2926 - 2929. Cancer Ascendant - Pisces Nav-
amsa: Birth should be in Cancer ascendant with
Pisces navamsa. Then the subject will cause happi-
ness to his relatives, be devoted to Lords Vishnu and
Siva, will eat limited food, will have secretive sexual
lust, be afraid of committing sinful acts, be very
intelligent, will be quite happy in old age and be inthe
grip of difficulties and poverty in childhood. He will
be happy after marriage and will first beget a female
issue. He will have self-earned wealth, and will enjoy
a powerful position in the employ of the king. His
third dasa will bestow on him abundant prosperity.
He will enjoy men-borne conveyances (read only
conveyances) and will be ever happy (in this dasa).

Notes: The words “Kujatrimsamsa sansthithe”
insloka 2926 is a wrong appendage. It means “placed
in the Trimsamsa of Mars”. The position of the
ascendant is already fixed to be Pisces Navamsa.

“Jyeshtaputriyutho” reads as “Seemantha
putrimaan” in another text which correctly means
that the native’s first issue will be a daughter.

2932 - 2937. Mercury in Cancer Navamsa:
Cancer Ascendant with Pisces Navamsa will lead to
following effects if Mercury obtains Cancer Nav-
amsa simultaneously. The native will lord over many
women, be wealthy and be intent upon joining pros-
titutes. He will be everdevoted to pleasing his mother
but will have half-brothers (i.e. father will have
another marriage). These effects will materialise in
the dasa of the 9th lord. He will obtain conveyances
and be happy after the age of 27. Inthe dasa of 8th lord
he will befriend in royal circles and beget a chief
position. He will enjoy the mercy of Goddess Lakshmi.
In Moon’s dasa, during the sub periods of Jupiter and
Saturn, he will incur fear from enemies and destruc-
tion of peace. Further he will acquire the wrath of his
paternal uncle, urinary disorders (diabetes etc.) and
ulcer. To overcome the evils, suitable propitiations
be done.

Notes: The Rasi ascendant should be Cancer

while in Navamsa diagram, the ascendant should be
Pisces having Mercury in the 5th therefrom. As a
result, ina nutshell certain things are brought to light:
The native’s father will have a second marriage. The
subject will himself be related to many women and
will be of loose morals. He will be devoted to his
mother. The dasa of Moon will give him urinary
disorders and disputes with paternal uncle during the
sub period rulership of Jupiter and Saturn. His Mars
dasa will give him fortunes. 8th lord Saturn’s dasa
will introduce him in high circles. Remedies to
overcome urinary disorders and misunderstandings
are suggested in the following slokas.

2938 - 29391/2. Remedies: Donation ofanaxe be
given away to overcome this evils following which
the dangerous urinary disorder and enmity with
paternal uncle will be warded off. The following
Mantra should be recited (before the image of a deity,
in Sanskrit): Mama Satrukshayaarthaaya thava
Poojaam karomyaham. Satruvamsa kshayaarthaaya
sarvaabhishtaartha siddhaye. Bhayaapa mrityu
naasaaya kuthaaram pradamamyaham.

Notes: “Kuthaara” and “Parasu” mean one and
the same thing, i.e. the axe of a wood-cutter. To
overcome urinary disorders and enmity with paternal
uncle, donation ofan axe is suggested with recitation
of the Mantra given with Sanskrit transliteration in
the text above. The meaning of the Mantra is: To
obtain destruction of enemies, i.e. enmity with pater-
nal uncle, I worship you (O Lord). Also fulfill all my
desires and save me from the danger of untimely
death (that could be caused due to diabetes).

2946. Movable Ascendant: One will enjoy for-

tunes throughout life if his ascendant being a mov-
able one has the 9th lord in exaltation while the 4th
from ascendant is occupied by Venus.

Notes: This rule relates to Aries, Cancer, Libra
and Capricorn ascendants. Yet the following may be
noted as to how the condition forms:

1. Aries ascendant with Venus and Jupiter in
Cancer.

2. Cancer ascendant with exalted Jupiter while
Venus is in the 4th in Libra.

3. Libra ascendant with Venus in the 4th in
Capricorn while Mercury the 9th lord is required to
be in Virgo in exaltation.

4. Capricorn ascendant with Venus in the 4th in
Aries while the 9th lord Mercury is required to be in
Virgo itself, in exaltation.

Due to elongational impossibilities between
Venus and Mercury, combinations at 3 and 4 above
are not practical. Apparently the text implies only
Aries and Cancer ascendants.

2947, Lord of Sun Sign: In case of a movable
ascendant, ifthe lord of Sunsignis in exaltation while
the planet Mercury is endowed with full strength, the
dasa of Mercury, particularly its first half will cause
advent of great fortunes.

Notes: "Taddasayam" can also mean the dasa of
the Sun’s dispositor. For all the four movable ascend-
ants, Mercury owns a certain evil house. Although, in
the process, he may be endowed with strength, he
would need the help of the Sun’s dispositor to give
fortunes. Why the Sun’s dispositor comes in the
picture is difficult to be explained. However, this
principle applying to a movable ascendant deserves
special consideration.

. Jupiter (or the first sub period, as it could be alterna-

death.

- 2962 -29631/2. Mother: One born in Champaka
Nadiamsa, having the 4th lord Saturn in relation to
the Sun either by aspect or by conjunction will lose
his mother in his childhood. (Alternatively), loss of
mother will occur in the sub period of the 2nd lord
(Mars) in the major period of the 10th lord (Moon)
and the native will beget a step-mother. However if
birth be in the second half of the concerned Nadiamsa,
the mother will be long-lived.

Notes: Leaving aside Nadiamsa, a clue emerges
to the effect that the sub period of Mars in the major
period of the Moon will prove adverse for mother in
case of Libra ascendant.

2981-2985. Dasa Effects - Libra Ascendant:
(a) Should the dasa lord be devoid of strength, one
will be deprived of splendour (i.e. he will turn pale,
without much blood). Through a benefic planet, only
benefic effects will come to pass; how come there
will be no happiness through it?

(b) If the dasa lord is conjunct the Navamsa
dispositor of a Yoga Karaka planet, the subject will
gain housing properties and the like. He will further
acquire spouse, progeny and friends and royal recog-
nition.

(c) If the dasa lord is placed ina Navamsa of an
inimical planet, then in his dasa, in the sub period of
(another) malefic, there will be fear from thieves and
enemies, loss of position or displacement, enmity
with elders in the family and obstacles in performing
royal duties.

(d) If the dasa lord is weak, is placed in the 8th
and is related to 8th lord by aspect or association, one
will incur damage to his calling and money apart
from developing enmity with coborn. The lord of a
dasa placed at birth ina Rasi/Navamsa ofan inimical
planet will in the sub period of his relevant dispositor
promote expenditure on account of enemies.

_ 2986 - 2988. Libra Ascendant - Jupiter: (a) If
Jupiter is in Pisces at birth, the subject of Libra
ascendant will be dear to his king, be religious,

learned in meanings of Sastras, passionate and eve
peaceful in disposition.

(b) One will be dear to king if Jupiter occupies
the 10th in Navamsa, or be in a friendly Navamsa
(while in the sign Pisces).

(c) IfJupiter, placed in Scorpio, begets Mercurian
or Venusian Navamsa (Virgo/Libra), he will do acts
that will displease the king.

(d) Jupiter in the 10th (in Cancer) with a Nav-
amsa of Saturn will cause foolishness and the native
will be a liar. He will be unorthodox.

(e) If the Navamsa for Jupiter in Cancer is
specifically Capricorn, one will commit many sinful
acts, will have enmity with people equal to the king,
but will show immediate friendly gestures.

(f) Jupiter in the 10th with Libra Navamsa will
make one jealous, and give him secretly held destruc-
tive thoughts.

2998 - 3004. Ashtaka Varga: (a) The sub period
of a planet in whose signs there are 1,2 or3 Ashtaka
Varga dots (rectified) will be futile and the person
will experience much difficulties in his undertakings
apart from loss of money, grains and quadrupeds.

(b) Auspicious effects will occur in the sub
period ofa planet that has five Bindus in his Ashtaka
Varga.

(c) Ifboth the signs owned by a planet (excepting
the Sun and the Moon) has excess Bindus in his
Ashtaka Varga, then his sub period will produce
exceedingly beneficial effects.

(d) The sub period ofa planet in whose sign there
are no Ashtaka Varga Bindus at all will be futile.

(e) From Mars etc. (i.e. Mars to Saturn) good
results will be obtained in their dasa periods ifthe two
signs owned by them are rich with Ashtaka Varga
Bindus (i.e. with more Bindus). If the dots are equal,
(i.e. neither less nor more - containing four Bindus)
effects will be even (i.e. neither good nor bad).
## Page 48

Deva Keralam 31

(f) The sign owned by the Sun (i.e. Leo) being
bereft of Bindus will make his sub period unproduc-
tive (of good). So also regarding the sign owned by
the Moon (i.e. Cancer).

(g) At the time of commencement of the dasa of
the 5th lord, in the signs that contain more Bindus....
the Moon’s Ashtaka Varga... The Bhinnashtaka Varga
of the planets from the Sun onwards should be studied
separately. The effects of the Moon (i.e. the Moon’s
transit) should be studied with the help of
Prastarashtaka Varga.

Notes: Instructions contained in “a” to “f” are
quite clear and are in line with generally available
information. These can be applied as a common
yard-stick.

Instructions in “g” are not clear. Apparently the
text wants to specify something about 5th lord’s dasa.
What all we could gather is that Bhinna and Prastara
Ashtaka Vargas should be used (as per rules laid
down in general).

3005. The importance of the Moon & Ascend-
ant: The Moon is the body while the ascendant (i.e.
ascending degree) is its breath (or spirit or vitality).
After an examination of both these elements, effects
of all the Nadiamsas be declared.

3006. The Ashtaka Vargas of the Moon and the
lord of ascendant be examined while analysing the
effects of those dasas.

Notes: The words “Taddasaayaam” may other-
wise mean the dasas of the Moon and the lord of
ascendant. Yet itis more logical to depend on these
Ashtaka Vargas universally in respect of all dasas
generally in view of sloka 3005 above.

3007. Libra ascendant - Pisces Navamsa: One
born in this part with Mudgara Nadiamsa will be

prosperous and happy in the dasa represented by the
Nakshatra denoted by processing the Ashtaka Varga
of the Moon.

Notes: In the first instance, Mudgara Nadiamsa,
be ignored for itis a corrupt addition. We should take
only Pisces Navamsa to be valid as ascending as part
of Libra ascendant.

Secondly the clue given for analysing the dasa
with the help of Moon’s Ashtaka Varga can be
applied to any ascendant, not just to Libra with Pisces
Navamsa. The meaning is explained below:

The use of the Moon’s Ashtaka Varga is ex-
plained ina brief manner by the text without referring
to a specific house. The word “Avasisiia” meaning
remainder tells us of the involvement some process
of division. With the help of know instructions, we
can understand the same thus:

There will be Bindus in the various signs, even
as low as zero, in the Moon’s Ashtaka Varga. Since
prosperity is referred to, we can take the Bindus in the
pre-rectified Ashtaka Varga chart prepared for the
Moon. Her Sodya Pinda be multiplied by the said
numberof Bindusand dividend by27. The remainder
will represent a Nakshatra counted from Aswini
which will yield a certain planet’s Vimsottari dasa.
This dasa will bring prosperity.

For example there are five bindus in the 9th
(counted from natal ascendant) inthe Moon’s Ashtaka
Varga, and her Sodya Pinda is, say, 80. Thus 5
multiplied by 80 and divided by 27 leaves a remain-
der of 25, which represents Poorvabhadrapada
Nakshatra. Thus, Jupiter’s dasa in this case will give
prosperity.

3011. Irrelevant: Satum’s movement in Revathi,
Hasta, Arudya, Bharani and Svathi will usher condi-
tions of famine in the country.

3042--3017. The Moon’s Ashtaka Varga for
Libra ascendant: Should the Moon bein Vargothama
in Libra and secure 3 (ormore) rectified Bindus in her
Ashtaka Varga, the third dasa will bring prosperity.
("Padadhikabale”" denotes more than two dots.) In
this case when Saturn transits Libra, the native will

enjoy great prosperity. Simultaneously he will have
fear from enemies, but later on he will be happy
overcoming this fear. When Saturn transits in Swathi
Nakshatra, destruction of relatives and fear (from
elsewhere) will occur. During this time, coinciding
with the Sun’s transit in Capricorn through Pisces, the
native will have his enemies converted into friends.
During the next three months with the Sun in Aries
through Gemini, his enemies will be destroyed. In
Gemini however the Sun’s transit will bring forth
some worries but will cause fruition of one’s efforts.
In Cancer, the Sun’s transit will cause happiness and
distress (simultaneously). Saturn moving in Visakha
will bring the enemies into the fold of the native and
will cause great happiness except in the months
denoted by the adverse solar movements. Further,
one will beget success in the attempts he then makes
with Saturn in Visakha.

3018 - 3028. Transit in Nakshatras - General:
(a) When Saturn transits the third Nakshatra fromthe
birth Nakshatra, the native will overpower his en-
emics.

(b) When he moves in the second star, he will
cause great fear, danger in general and danger to life.

(c) In his movement in the fourth star, he will
give distress, quarrels and grief.

(c) In the fifth star, the planet Saturn in transit
will give mental agony and enmity with Pandya king
(i.e.problems through government) and destruction.
When Satummis in transit in the 2nd/4th stars, the king
of the country will dic and the native will undergo
much grief.

(d) If the birth star or the tenth therefrom is
occupied by a malefic at birth, Saturn’s transit in this
segment will create quarrels with king and conse-
quent distress. In the absence of these effects,
physical illness to self, and nuisance from his own
men will come to pass. When a benefic transits in the
first or tenth Nakshatra, auspicious effects will occur
and malefics according to their natural disposition
will cause mental distress.

(e) Results should be understood according to
the caste etc. (or the circumstances of the native).

(f) Should malefics occupy birth star, second,
third or eighth from it, evil transits of Jupiter and the
Sun (Kroorabde, Kroora Masage) will produce abun-
dant difficulties.

(g) If natural benefics occupy one of these three
Nakshatras, as at “f”, these transits will cause great
happiness, proximity to king, advent of wealth, suc-
cess in efforts and progress in profession.

(bh) If malefics occupy first, third or seventh
Nakshatra, the above referred transits will bring
abundant difficulties. These should be deduced with
the help of Ashtaka Varga.

(i) Auspicious effects and acquisition of wealth
will take place if benefics occupy favourable
Nakshatras. Advent of wealth will occurinthe month

of 11th lord (i.e. the Sun’s transit in any Rasi occur-
ring on the week day ruled by the 11th lord from
ascendant) or when the Sun transits the sign repre-
sented by the ascendant’s decanate. With the Sun’s
auspicious transits, acquisition of wealth will have to
be foretold.

Notes: Results of Saturn’s transit ina certain star
Should be applied to the 10th and 19th stars froma
givenstaras well. Forexample Janma Nakshatra (i.e.
the star occupied by the Moon, the first Nakshatra)
includes the 10th and 19th therefrom. 2nd Nakshatra
includes 11th and 20th also. So on and so forth.

These apply to any given in nativity in general.

3029 - 3031. Results of Weekdays: If the birth star
(containing the Moon) coincides with a week day
ruled by a benefic planet, the native will enjoy
various kinds of wealthand happiness. Birthona day
ruled by a malefic will cause physical illness, royal
wrath and financial instability. Ifit be ona Tuesday,
one will wander (aimlessly) and will incur danger
through royal anger. Monday birth will grant happi-
ness, possession of wonderful flowers, sexual
enjoyments filled with love, and enjoyment of qual-
ity food. (Additional effects for) Tuesday birth will
be grief, self-destruction, and quarrels. Mercury’s
day, viz. Wednesday as the day of birth will cause
happiness, acquisition of (or enjoyment) intoxicant
drinks, and ghee apart from leaming and wealth,
Thursday birth will cause acquisition of robes, wealth
and physical happiness. One will enjoy oraments,
sexual pleasures, scents and a variety of clothes if the
## Page 51

34 Chandra Kala Nadi

birth be ona Friday - ruled by Venus. Saturday being
the day of birth will give grief, difficulties, fear,
troubles from servants and diseases.

Notes: In the first instance, week days are divided
between benefic and malefic planets, thus: Monday,
Wednesday, Thursday and Friday are benefic days
ruled in order by the Moon (irrespective of Paksha or
lunar half), Mercury (irrespective of his association),
Jupiter and Venus. Malefic week days are Sunday,
Tuesday and Saturday and are ruled by the Sun, Mars
and Saturn in that order. Now see the following
clarificatory notes.

Benefic week days will give wealth and happiness
in combination with other horoscopic influences.
“Birth star coinciding with week day ruled by.......”
is an unintelligible clause.

When the day of birth is ruled by a malefic it will
make one prone to illness depending on the other
yogas in the horoscope.

The following classical quotations may be of inter-
est.

One born on Sunday will be endangered in either
the first month or the 6th month,or in the 22nd/23rd
year. His life span will be 60 years.

Monday-born will face danger in the 11th month or
in the 26th/27th year. His life span will be 84 years.

Tuesday-born will be in trouble in the 2nd or 22n
year. He will be always sick and will live upto 74
years.

Wednesday-born will incur danger inthe 8th month
or in the 8th year. He will die after his 64th year.

Thursday-born will be in danger in 7th month,
16th/13th year. He will live upto 84th year.

Friday-born will never fall sick. He will die in the
60th year.

Saturday-born will incurdangerin the 1st month or
in the 13th year. His life will end in 100th year.

3032 - 3033. Illness: (a) Should the day of birth
be ruled by one of the lords of 6th and 8th, the native

will fall sick in the sub period of the said planet and
in its major period.

(b) The month will correspond to the evil transit of
the Sun.

(c) Astrologers predict illness, (in the above case)
to be materialising on the week days ruled by the lord
of the major and sub periods.

Notes: The following table will show the lords of
the 6th and 8th for the 12 ascendants.

Ascendant 6th Lord 8th Lord
Aries Mercury Mars
Taums Venus Jupiter
Gemini Mars Saturn
Cancer Jupiter Satum
Leo Saturn Jupiter
Virgo Saturn Mars
Libra Jupiter Venus
Scorpio Mars Mercury
Sagit. Venus Moon
Capri Mercury Sun
Aqua Moon Mercury
Pisces Sun Venus

As an example if a person of Aries ascendant is
bom either ona Wednesday (ruled by Mercury) oron
a Tuesday (ruled be Mars) he will acquire illness in
the major period of Mars and sub period of Mercury,
or Vice versa.

Similarly for other ascendants, one should make
suitable evaluation.

(b) The Sun’s evil transit with reference to the
Moon, ascendant, or other natal positions should be
properly linked. Insuch months during the rulership
of suggested dasa periods, the illness will be more
likely.

(c) The commencing week day will either be of the
lord of the 6th or of the 8th from the ascendant.

3034. Should the ascending degree be aspected or
## Page 52

Deva Keralam 35

occupied by a malefic planet, or by a planet that has
lost in a war with another, or be occupied by an
inimical planet, then in its periods the subject will be
involved in disputes provided the said yoga is
unaspected by a benefic planet.

Notes: “Occupation” of a malefic is not in our text,
but is adopted from another version and added to the.
translation.

“Aroodha Bhaga” is ascending degree, that is the
sign ascending at birth.

Planetary war: When two planets (except the
luminaries) are on the same degree there is sa J to be
a war between them. The one in the north is declared
victorious.

Amore clear picture is givenby C.G. Rajan. When
two planets out of the five, viz. Mars to Satur, are in
one and the same sign with longitudes of identical
degree, minute and second, a planetary war occurs.
The victor will have higher latitude.

I give below an example.

On23rd August 23, 1992, Venus and Jupiter in Leo
attained the same degree, minute and second while
the latitude of Venus was 1° 17' North, and that of
Jupiter 1° 4’. Hence Venus, with a higher latitude
should be treated as winner.

Another planet that could be connected with the
ascendant by aspect of association is one inimical to
the lord of the ascendant. Example: Capricom as-
cendant related to the Sun, dead enemy of ascendant
lord Saturn.

In each of these cases, the result is involvement in
quarrels, in the dasa periods of the concerned planet.
In case of the example of Capricorn, the dasa of the
Sun will give the said result.

Protection from the said adversity is a helpful
association of the ascendant with a benefic.

3035 - 3037. Dasa Effects: During the first Dasa
the native will have eating comforts, will beget
auspicious effects and various kinds of wealth apart
from grief. The second dasa will cause wealth,
happiness and apparels. Destruction of quadrupeds,
landed properties and money, and grief to one’s near
and dear will be produced by the third dasa. Addi-
tionally sickness, enmity with relatives, quarrels and
sudden outbursts of anger will follow. Inthe 4thdasa,
effects to occurare well-being, happiness, wealthand
worship. The fifth dasa will cause grief due to loss of
wealth following royal wrath. One will acquire inthe
sixth dasa happiness, wealth, success, lands, garlands
and robes. The seventh dasa will produce many a
kind of grief, difficulties and ailments due to vitiation
of three bodily temperaments viz. bile, wind and
phlegm. Acquisition of royal honours, ornaments,
conveyances, involvement in divine undertakings
and bed comforts will take place in the eighth dasa.
The last of all, the ninth dasa will cause friendliness
with the king and virtuous men, fondness for learn-
ing, obeying royal orders, arrival of sons, friends and
relatives and skill. These apart, one will be worried
on account of unwed progeny, will incur fever,
phlegmatic fevers and troubles to sitand to sleep, and
wander aimlessly. (The word “Subham” is a corrupt
addition at the end of the sloka No. 3037.)

Notes: The above slokas give general hints about
the nine dasas commencing from the first dasa. The
relevant terms are not however exactly used. For
example, “Janmarkshe” means Moon sign and not
literally first dasa. But subsequent references are to
Sampath, Vipath etc, upto Parama Maitra. Thus
these refer only to Dasa sequences.

The summary of the effects of nine dasas given by
## Page 53

36 Chandra Kala Nadi

the text can be arranged as under ignoring certain
over-stated hints:

ist dasa: Happiness and grief.

2nd dasa: Financial progress

3rd dasa: Losses, grief, sickness, enmity and loss
of temper.

4th dasa: Wealth and happiness.

5th dasa: Grief, loss and troubles from govern-
ment (or professional debacles) and other related
sources.

6th dasa: Properties, wealth and general happi-
ness

7th dasa: Various ailments and grief.

8th dasa: Royal honours, conveyances and spir-
itual progress.

9th dasa: Worry about progeny, illness, royal
association etc.

Refer also to Phala Deepika etc.

3038 - 3039. (a) Saturn transiting in the 10th house
(read “Karmarkshe” instead of “Janmarkshe”) will
grant curd, sauce or vessels (i.e. eating comforts),
quadrupeds, agriculture (or professional gains), cour-
age and ornaments. In Adhana ascendant, it will
bring royal wrath apart from causing mental infirmity
and destruction of conveyances, wealth and food. In
the 8th, there will be fear from enemies and troubles
relating to progeny, friends, spouse and king. In the
7th there will be troubles from king, enemies and odd
or unsuitable placements, apart from troubles from
servants.

(b) The astrologer should get up in the early hours
of the day and worship his family deity and then
calculate the planetary positions following which

only all (related to horoscope study) should be under-
taken.

(c) The Bhava that has strength (or more dots) in the
Moon’s Ashtaka Varga will reveal its effects (posi-
tively).

Notes: In “a”, there is no clear mention as to the
fact that these results relate to Saturn’s transit. Buta
reference to sloka 486 infra which almost has
semblence to the present slokas will convince the
reader of my suggestions. Thus missing links are
supplied in the translation.

3040. Saturn’s Transit: The signs that are weak,
when transited by Saturn, will be a cause of a great
deal of difficulties. The specific evil months (should
be traced with the help of adverse solar movements).

Notes: "Tarabala Viheenarksha" has been trans-
lated as weak sign so as to be practical in interpreta-
tion. Otherwise, this term means: the signs that have
weak (of afflicted) constellations.

Weak signs referred to here are those Bhavas
which fall short of Shadbala (or six source strength,
viz. Kala Bala etc.) and those that are deprived of
minimum Ashtaka Varga dots, and the effects of
relevant transits of Saturn will be only adverse. The
minute period of adversity will be specifically trace-
able with unfavourable transits of the Sun, narrowing
down to a month.

Prastharashtaka Varga is another method.

The Sun is adverse when he transits the following
places with reference to concerned natal positions,
according to Sphuji Dhwaja:

From ascendant: 3rd, Sth, 6th, 9th, and 12th.

From Saturn: 3rd, and 12th.

From Jupiter: 1st, 3rd, 7th, 8th, and 12th.

From Venus: Ist, 3rd, 4th, Sth, 8th, 9th, and 10th.

From Mars: 3rd, Sth, 6th, and 12th.

From Mercury: 1st, 2nd, 4th, 7th, and 8th.

From the Moon: ist, 2nd, 4th, 5th, 7th, 8th, 9th, and
12th.

3041. Rahu’s Transits; When the planet Rahu

3042 - 3043. According to another source, fear of
theft and loss of village articles [ignoie the word
"village"] and difficulties are denote’ . Rahu Dasa,
Mars bhukti. Debts, theft, ulcer and diseases will
follow. These effects can be expected also inthe dasa

birth).

is replaced by “Rahu’s transits” in another version.

We have a very useful clue about Saturn’s natal

constellation, which in turn will relate toa Dasa. For
example, Saturn in Aswini will mean that Ketu Dasa
will be adverse, in Bharani Venus Dasa will bx
adverse, so on and so forth.

3044, The said Dasa (ref. sloka 3043) related to

3045. Untimely Death: The sub period of the
strongest planet in the Dasa of a malefic will bring
about untimely death and grief on account of evils to
one’s own men.

Notes: Untimely death means some danger to the
person’s life.

“Strongest planet” to cause the said evils should be
carefully identified. For practical purposes it is one
with potential Shadbala (6-source strength), and
placed inanadverse house at birth, i.e. 6th, 8th or 12th
from the ascendant, the Moon or the Dasa Jord, whe
is a natural malefic. Then only these adversities will
be born.

3046 - 3048. Navarasa Dispacitors ete. (a) Note
the Navamsa dispositorof Saturn. cf Mandiand of the
Rast disp ositor of 8th tard. The wcakest of the three
will dssta5, the happiness of the pairve.

(b) When Saturn transits the 8th kouse, ore will be
foolish (read Moodhatmamurthy instead of
Maudhyaanias per other version), will have destruc-
tonof physique. appearance, virtues, gold (i.e wealth,
properties and the like), eye-sight and family happi-

and chest apart from abdominal disorders caused by
## Page 55

38 Chandra Kala Nadi

excessive eating. He will be deprived of happiness
relating to residence and conveyance. Hard flesh will

(c) Saturn’s association with the 8th house (at

Three planets play a leading role in destroying
one’s happiness.

1) The Navamsa dispositor of Saturn.

2) The Navamsa dispositor of Mandi. [ Mandi and
Gulika are one and the same.]

3) The Navamsa dispositor of the planet in whose
sign the 8th lord is places. Example - Pisces ascend-
ant gives the 8th lordship to Venus, who is, say, in
Leo. The dispositor of Venus is the Sun. The Sun is
in the Navamsa say of Mercury. Hence it is Mercury
that can spoil happiness in this case.

For exact calculation of Mandi, see sloka 70, ch.3
of Brihat Parasara Hora, part 1, English translation
by R. Santhanam. The position of Mandi is to be
calculated for the beginning Muburia of Saturn, and
not ending Muhurta, as further justified in the exam-
ple given in the notes for slokas 25 - 30, chapter 4,
ibid.

3050. Jupiter in Retrogression: The effects due
to Jupiter (mentioned above) will come to pass if he
is endowed with strength, or even if he is retrograde
without beingin debility. Results relating to a Bhava
be deduced according to the association it has.

Notes: The results noted in “d” above (slokas 3046
- 49) will not come to pass, in spite of the fact that
Jupiter may be related to Venus if Jupiter is retro-

grade in Capricorn, or if he is short of minimum
strength.

If a weak or debilitated Jupiter in retrogression is
related to Venus, it will only spoil the good role of
Venus. This verse disproves the theory of Uttara
Kalamrita that a debilitated planet in retrogression is
eaual to an exalted one.

3051 - 3053 1/2. Immovable Ascendants -
Kuntala Nadiamsa: Jupiter in Aquarius with
Vargottama Navamsa while the Moon is in Kuntala
Nadiamsa (in another version it is Kunda Nadiamsa)
will give the under-mentioned effects. The native
will have anelder brother. His sister will havea long-
living husband. The Moon in Kunda Nadiamsa
(without reference Jupiter above) will bring abun-

* oains through relatives. The subject will be rich,
i ', given to sexual pleasures, will have limited
educauun and be an expert in matters relating to
material prosperity. In his childhood, he will be
mean. Later he will have worries about progeny and
be emaciated. His brother will be initiated with
Pranava Mantra (the sacred syllable "Om" - taught
to Lord Siva by His Son, Kartikeya), be bold, splen-
dorous, be a pleased soul, (one time) a sinner, given
to anger and credited with valorous acts.

Notes: Kuntala Nadiamsa is Kunda Nadiamsa which
rules from 26° 24' to 26° 36' in movable signs, from
3° 24' to 3° 36' in immovable signs, and from 11° 24'
to 11° 36’ of common signs.

common signs.

3073-3075. Nara Yoga: If Saturn in the 7th house
without the aspect of a benefic planct joins an exalted
planet, a yoga called Nara Yoga is produced. The
native will be, as a result, a great sinner, will torture
and cheat others, will do base acts and kill (or trouble)
Brahmins. On account of these sins, be will incur
diseases and loss of sons and be emaciated.

Notes: This yoga does not apply to Aquarius
ascendant although it appears in this part. No planet
is exalted in Leo. This is a yoga generally applicable
to all ascendants but Aquarius, Taurus, Leo, Gemini
and Sagittarius. No planet is exalted in the 7th in
these cases.

“Uchcha Yoge” is a corrupt addition in sloka 3074
referring the source to be another authority.

will do sinful acts.

(b) The conjunction of Jupiter and Rahu produces
Guru Chandala Yoga which denotes that the person
will commit a hundred sins.

3080. Jupiter in Aquarius: Should Jupiter be in
Aquarius with watery Navamsa, his older brother
will incur grief and separation ina foreign place. His
father will die at home (means, in birth place). Later
the person will face destruction of sons.

of children to the native. Scorpio should not be
treated as a watery sign. It is the only insect or
centiped sign in the zodiac. Canceris another watery
Navamsa which Jupiter in Aquarius shal] not obtain.

3082 - 3083. Benefic Places - General: The Sun
is auspicious in the 6th, 3rd and 10th houses. The
Moon is favourable in ascendant, 3rd, 6th and 7th
houses. The 4th, 3rd and 6th houses are beneficial for
Mercury. Jupiter is favourable in the 9th and 7th
houses. All the planets are favourable in the 11th
house. These apply to transits.

Notes: As for the Sun, the Sanskrit word “Dik” is
translated as the 10th instead of 8th. Actually the
directions are ten including skyward and earthward.
Otherwise these are only eight.

“Agni” means three, denoting three sacrificial
fires.

“Adri” means seven denoting seven hills. Other
terms are simple enough.

The hints given here apply in general to transits of
planets.

The generally favourable positions for planets in
transit with reference to the Moon could be found in
transit-chapters of standard textbooks.

3084. Saturn - Mars Conjunction: When Saturn
and Mars join inthe sign Cancer inthe 8th, the native
will see his spouse and sons in sickness and physical
decay according to sages.

Notes: This particular piece of instruction should
apply to Sagittarius ascendant. However there may
be such effects when these two joinin the 8th forother
ascendants, but not just in Cancer notwithstanding
the ascendant.

illness in general); Sth - great fear; 6th - destruction
of enemies; 7th - greatly miserable; 8th - death; 9th
- physical emaciation; 10th - distress; 11th - gains;

3086 - 3089. Saturn’s Effects According to Oth-
ers: If Saturn transits the natal ascendant, one will be
involved in quarrels and will incur grief. In the 2nd,
it will cause fear from enemies and destruction
wealth. One will enjoy food comforts, and happiness
of progeny and relatives with Saturn moving in the
3rd. Further, success in war (litigations etc.) and
various kinds of comforts and fulfillment of desires
will also materialise. The transit of Saturn in the 4th
will destroy friends, progeny and those that are dear

to the native. Loss of quadrupeds, lands, calling and
honour will follow. The 5th house having Saturn in
transit will cause wavering mind, and entanglement
in many (impracticable) thoughts (or plans). Destruc-
tion of enemies and great comforts will result 6th
house Saturn in transit. This planet moving in the 7th
will harm the native’s spouse, progeny and servants.
In the 8th destruction, enmity and vices will result.
Attachment to sinful deeds and destruction of for-
tunes and auspiciousness will be revealed by transit
Saturn in the 9th house. Obstructions to financial
gains and destruction of purpose will be brought
about by Saturn in the 10th. An intelligent astrologer
should declare such results for Saturn’s transit in
ascendant etc.

Notes: The concermed lines dealing with Saturn’s
transit in 11th and 12th from ascendant are missing,
as attributed to another source consulted by the
author. The deficit can be made up by sloka 3084
supra.

The following information on effects of Saturn’s
transit with reference to concerned natal positions
may be of use to the reader:

On natal Saturn - wounds and diseases; 2nd
thereof - loss of honour; 3rd - cure from illness and
trouble from enemies, gain of status; 4th - destruction
of virtues and friendly contacts; 5th - acquisition of
son and wealth; 6th - acquisition of position and
wealth; 7th - unfruitful movements, destruction of
spouse; 8th - diseases, destruction and enmity; 9th -
destruction of livelihood; 10th - no professional
gains; 11th - pleasures and wealth; 12th - wandering
and fear.

On natal Sun - happiness, wealth, joy and pleas-
ure, 2nd thereof - wealth; 3rd - loss of honour, vigour
and physical beauty; 4th - increase of happiness from
kinsfolk; 5th - sickness to self, and anxiety about
children; 6th - difficulties; 7th - happiness from
spouse; 8th - destruction of diseases and confusion;
9th - evils; 10th - professional success; 11th - wealth
and good effects; 12th - loss of work.

On natal Jupiter - delusion; 2nd thereof - destruc-
tion of good effects; 3rd - conflict and quarrels; 4th
- anxiety and loss of relatives; Sth- gives progeny,
honour, acquisition and glory; 6th - fame; 7th -
agitation and loss of wife; 8th - death; 9th - distress

from mean and low people; 10th - destroys beauty;
1ith - easy money; 12th - increase of physical
strength.

On natal Venus: destroy beauty and spouse; 2nd

and hatred; 4th - strife; 5th - imprisonment; 6th -
honour, lordship and wealth; 7th - anxiety and de-

3090 - 3091. (a) Father: When Saturn transits the
9th from the Moon sign, predict loss of father. This
will apply to his aspect on the said 9th house as well,
or to the time of his conjunction with natal Sun. (In
coincidence with one of the above conditions), de-
struction of father will take place when Saturnattains
the decanate, Navamsa or Dwadasamsa ruled by the
Sun. Further transit Sun will also be in adverse
placements.

(b) When Saturn transits the sign represented by
the Navamsa position of the 12th lord counted from
the ascendant, quarrels and destruction of suns (prog-
eny) will come to pass.

Notes: In the first instance, three clues regarding
the transit of Saturn in connection with fatality to
father are discussed. Saturn should move in oraspect
the 9th counted from the Moon (or ascendant), or he
should come to the sign occupied by the natal Sun
(representing father). This is not enough. Saturn
should simultaneously be in Leo’s decanate or Nav-
amsa or Dwadasamsa. Leo Dwadasamsa is available
ineachsign. Leo decanate applies to the signs Aries,
Leo or Sagittarius. Leo Navamsa does not occur for
## Page 61

44 Chandra Kala Nadi

the signs Gemini, Libra and Aquarius.

The third condition is the Sun in undesirable
houses.

Only then death of father be predicted.

(b) See in which Navamsa the lord of the 12th is
placed at birth. The transit of Saturn in the sign
denoted by the said Navamsa will promote quarrels
and will endanger one’s progeny.
