3092 - 3093. (a) When transit Saturn attains the
sign represented by the Navamsa position of the 4th
lord from natal ascendant, the person will have
quarrels with the king (or employer), and also diffi-
culties.

(b) The Bhava concerned will incur destruction
when Saturn transits (1) the sign equal to the Nav-
amsa position of the ruler of the 8th from the bhava
under consideration; (2) the sign that is in aspect to
the lord of the 8th from a given bhava.

(c) See if a Bhava lord attains more and more
divisions of the planet ruling the 8th therefrom. In
that case destruction of the original Bhava in question
will occur in the dasa of the (lord of) original Bhava.

Notes: (a) Difficulties and professional problems
will surface with Saturn’s movement in the sign
denoted by the Navamsa occupied by the lord of the
4th at birth.

(b) Three clues are given in respect of transit
Saturn’s ability to destroy the indications ofa house.
Firstly, in the sign denoted by the Navamsa position
of such a planet which rules the 8th from a given
house, Example - the 9th lord rules the 8th from the
2nd. Hence the sign denoted by the Navamsa position
of the 9th lord will be the target of Saturn’s transit.
This will affect family happiness, financial progress,
eyes, education etc.

Secondly Saturn should transit such a sign that is
aspected by the loid of the 8th from a given Bhava.
Example: The 2nd rules the 8th from the 7th. Hence
Saturn moving in the sign denoted by the Navamsa

position of 2nd lord will affect spouse, partnership
etc.

(c) This part is translated after supplying certain
missing jinks. The ideas the lord ofa bhava should not
beget many divisions of the planet ruling the 8th
therefrom. Then the dasa of the original bhava lord
yield adverse effects. For example in case of Aries,
the 6th is ruled by Mercury. Mars rules the 8th from
Virgo. Mercury remaining in many of Martian
divisions will in Mercury dasa cause ill-health, loss
in litigations, enmity etc. - adverse effects concern-
ing the 6th house.

3095 -3097. Libra Ascendant -Saturn’s Transit,
Venus dasa etc.: (a) When Saturn comes to the sign
represented by the Navamsa position of the lord of the
ascendant or of 11th, ora trine to one of these two
Navamsas, difficulties to mother be foretold. (b) The
ascendant lord’s dasa will bring in mental agony to
maternal relatives, during the sub period of 12th lord
of 10th lord.

(c) The dasa of 1 0th lord will cause great prosperity
for maternal uncles.

(d) So also the dasas of the lords of 2nd as well as
3rd.

Notes: (a) For Libra, the ascendant lord is Venus,
the 11th lord is the Sun. Hence the sign denoted by
the Navamsa occupied by Venus orthe Sun, ora trine
## Page 62

Deva Keralam 45

thereof, transited by the Sun will trouble the mother.
Thus this points to a certain month which should be
read only with a relevant sub period.

(b) The second clue is for Libra ascendant, Venus
dasa causing grief to maternal relatives in the sub
period of the 10th lord Moon or the 12th lord Mer-
cury.

In the following example, the maternal aunt of the
native had lost a growing daughter (about 15 years of
age) due to snake bite. This is in the native’s Venus
dasa, Moon’s sub period.

Native born on 17th February 1984, at 2235 hrs in
Delhi. Balance of Venus dasa at birth: 18 years 4
months and 22 days. Moon’s sub period in this dasa
ruled from November 1986 through July 1988.

Rasi positions: Taurus - Rahu; Leo - Moon; Libra
- ascendant, Mars, Saturn; Scorpio - Ketu; Sagittarius
- Jupiter; Capricorn - Mercury, Venus; Aquarius -
Sun.

Navamsa: Aries - Saturn; Taurus - Mars; Gemini
- Mercury, Rahu; Cancer- Jupiter; Leo - Moon; Libra
-ascendant; Scorpio - Sun; Sagittarius - Ketu; Aquarius
- Venus.

Further, from the clues given in the original vide
“a”, “c” and “d” above, we learn that the major
periods of the Moon, Mars and Jupiter are meant for
prosperity of the maternal relatives of a Libra native.

3098 - 3099. Libra Ascendant - Mother: The
person’s mother will be troubled in the sub period of
the lord of the 4th during the dasa of the 11th lord.
When Saturn in transit comes to the sign represented
by the Navamsa position of the 11th lord, predict
evils to the progeny of maternal uncles. These effects
are retold based on Sarva Nadi.

3100 - 3101. Jupiter in Navamsa: (a) For Libra
ascendant, should Jupiter in Pisces occupy the 9th
sign in Navamsa, (ora benefic’s Navamsa), one will
be dear to the king of his motherland. The dasa of
Jupiter as a consequence of above placement will
cause great happiness, just disposition and auspi-
cious effects.

(b) Jupiter in Pisces with Libra Navamsa will make
the native broad-faced and grant him pleasures in
general and an affectionate wife.

Notes: (a) Jupiter being the 6th lord for Libra
ascendant can prove auspicious in his dasa if he is at
birth placed in Pisces with specified Navamsa posi-
tion.

(b) Jupiter’s position in the 6th in Pisces (13° 20' to
16° 40') with Libra Navamsa grants a happy marriage
to the Libra native. “Lakshmi Shashtiamsa" is a
redundant conditions, not incorporated in the render-

3102 - 3108 1/2. Gemini Ascendant - Mudgara
Nadiamsa: He will be dark-bodied, will have praise-
worthy virtues. endowed with skills and will suffer
from stomachial disorders. His maternal aunt’s fam-
## Page 63

46 Chandra Kala Nadi

ily will be prosperous and herson will be affectionate
to the subject. The subject will live ina town betwixt
forests, will have a windy body, be fond of secretive
missions, be a miser and calm in disposition. He will
be skillful in religion, meritorious in acts, will have
knowledge of tastes (a branch of medical science),
will be well-educated, and fond of jokes. Tanks and
gardens will be constructed by him. He will honour
gods and Brahmins, be attached to his relatives,
devoted to Lords Vishnu and Siva, will eat limited
food, will have secretive lust for sexual pleasures, be
timid but majestic in disposition. In the middle of his
life, he will attain great prosperity while his child-
hood will be in the grip of poverty and troubles. He
will have no younger brother, and be fond of maternal
relatives. His maternal grand father will be endowed
with longevity. The person will do acts that will
please his mother. His eldest issue will be a female.
The native will be passionate, and be happy after
marriage. He will have self-earned wealth and will
serve the king. The sub period of the 9th lord in the
third dasa will cause great prosperity. The sub period
of lord of ascendant in the third dasa will cause
acquisition of a daughter.

Libra ascendant having Jupiter in Pisces. Actually
these relate to Geminiascendant, Mudgara Nadiamsa

Hence the present slokas are separated with suitable
identity. Also see slokas from 3165 to 3210 for
Mudgara Nadiamsa, Gemini ascendant which occurs
from 19° 36' to 19° 48' of arc.

3111 - 3114. Mudgara Nadiamsa: One born in
this Nadiamsa with the 7th lord in Lakshmi
Shashtiamsa will marry in his birth region. His
spouse will be fatherless (at the time of marriage).
The number of brothers-in-law will be in correspond-
ence with the Bindus (after reduction) in the Ashtaka
varga of Venus, or those in the 7th counted from the
Moon-occupied sign. Outof such numberof co-born,
two or three will be long-lived. The native’s father
will have seven brothers. Alternatively it will be 2 or
3 only. Two paternal uncles will be long-lived but be
disposed to cheat their brother (i.e. the native’s
father). The native’s maternal grand-mother will
face (early) destruction. He will incur poverty in the
second dasa.

3116 - 31191/2. Jupiter in 10th: If Jupiter is in the
Sth from 6th, i.e. 10th (denoting progeny of maternal
aunt), endowed with strength, the personal maternal
aunt’s son will have longevity, will have huge wealth
including elephants, bea ruler of the land (i.e. be very
powerful), will lead over many a woman, rich and
endowed with sons and daughters. The said relative
will be devoted to his mother. When the native will
be in the dasa of the 10th Jord, the said relative will
acquire a step-brother (i.e. the native’s maternal aunt
will get a co-wife). The native will in the dasa of the
10th lord obtain a rich conveyance, be happy after 26
years of age. He will constructa new house, will have
financial gains and auspicious effects. In the sub
period of the lord of ascendant during the dasa of the
10th lord, he will join royal men and acquire a
position of wide presidentship (or headship). God-
dess Lakshmi will shower Her blessings on him.
sub periods of the lords of the 6th, 8th or 12th in the
dasa of the Moon will also give same effects - enmity,
distress and quarrels.

(d) Saturn’s transit in the Moon sign, or in the sign
equal to Moon’s Navamsa at birth, will produce
danger from an inimical king (or powerful people).
Remedies as prescribed be sought. (Then) due to the
pleasure of kinsfolk (i.e. favourably disposed kins-
folk) enemies will turn into friends, and great happi-
ness will come to pass.

(e) The native of Mudgara Nadiamsa, Gemini
ascendant, should donate an axe (as a remedy vide
“d” above) as a result of which the band of enemies
will be destroyed.

Notes: (a) Mars, the 6th lord, denotes thefts for
Gemini ascendant. His occupation of exaltation
Navamsa will lead to such losses.

(b) Royal enmity could be interpreted as enmity
with powerful people in connection with marriage.
Thus there will be stiff opposition to marriage if

Saturn and Jupiter are in Libra in the Sth, with
identical longitudes.

The original instructions contained in “c” to “e” are
also applicable to Gemini. These are clear and need
no further clarifications.

3128 - 3129. The native will be fickle-minded
(i.e. will lose mental stability) due to enmity with the
king of his land during the dasa of the lord of the 10th
and in the sub period of an obstructive planet. Resort-
ing to donation and reciting the Mantra earlier sug-
gested, he will overcome such enmity and beget
auspicious effects.

Obstructive planet is the one that is not favour-
ably disposed to Mercury, the lord of Gemini ascend-
ant. Mainly these are Mars and Jupiter.

Planets not well-placed could also be obstructive
irrespective of their favourable relations with Mer-
cury.

3134 - 31351/2. (a) When Satum transits the sign
Scorpio, the native of Libra ascendant will develop
physical ineptitude or laziness.

(b) Should the lord of the ascendant be in the 6th
house while its lord is in the Sth in association with
the 8th lord, one will have diseased stomach.

(c) Should Venus be in the 7th from the ascend-
ant with Saturn’s aspect or association, one will incur
phliegmatic disorders and illness caused duc to exces-
sive heat. Further he will be troubled by impure
excretion and urinary disorders.

Notes: (a) This rule applies to Libra ascendant,
a sudden shift by the text from Gemini ascendant.
Satum moving in the 2nd from Libra ascendant is said
to cause bodily inability.

(b) This is a general rule, not for Libra ascendant
alone. With the lord of the ascendant in the 6th while
the lords of 6th and 8th are in the 5th house, abdomi-
nal disorders are to be foretold.

(c) Phlegmatic disorders relate to lungs and
heart. Rectal and urinary disorders are also part of
Venus in the 7th linked to Saturn by aspect or
conjunction. This axiomis more effectively applica-
ble to Libra ascendant, because of Saturn’s rulership
of 3rd (lungs) and 4th (heart). Venus rules the 8th
house in this case, and is the natural ruler of kidneys
## Page 66

Deva Keralam 49

(urine etc.) whose placement in Aries is bound to
create problems generated by excessive heat.

3136 - 3139. As a remedy, religious vows on
Sundays be observed. Every week (on Sunday), the
twelve Sun Gods be worshipped and or: should
spend Sundays without consuming fooe. Then the
sins of the previous birth be destroyed and incurable
disorders of urine, bile and wind will vanish. Before
commencing the vows, the astrologer should be
worshipped. Health will be recovered following do-
nation of red clothes. The Sun God’s image should be
obtained made of gold according to one’s means (for
the worship). Meditation, Posture. etc. suitable to the
worship and donation be also done.

Notes: The remedy suggested applies to blem-
ishes cited at “b” and “c” in slokas 3134-351;2.

3143 ~ 31481/2. Jupiter Dasa - Libra Ascend-
ant: The sub period of the Sun in the major period of
Jupiter will cause worries onaccount of royal sources.
Happiness will be restored later on. The sub period
of the Moon (in Jupiter dasa) will give a mix of good
and bad effects. Indigestion, dysentery, difference of
opinion with relatives, and distress to maternal kins-
folk will corne to pass. In the sub period of Venus. his
relatives will be in trouble while the king’s family (?)
will be in distress. His friends will be destroyed. In the
sub period of Mars, the native’s son will incur
troubles while his daughter will beget married. There
will be troubles to the person’s wife in Rahu’s sub
period of Jupiter dasa. The sub period of the Moon in
Jupiter’s dasa will endanger his maternal uncle in
(dangerous) cold fever during the Sun’s transit in evil
signs. His mother will also be in great distress. The
person will himselfenjoy great happiness. (Jeevamsa
Nadiyogena is not of proper composition, not amena-
ble for translation.) Acquisition of a child in the
family, ornaments and marriage function will also
materialise during the Moon’s sub period.
(Paschadvyakulakaryena does not fit the context. It
means, later due to performing distressful jobs.) He
will make good fortunes in royal association.

Notes: The sub periods of Venus, the Sun, the
Moon, Mars and Rabu in the main period of Jupiter
are discussed here in respect of Libra ascendant,
without involving the Nadiamsa. A rough overview
## Page 67

50 Chandra Kala Nadi

is depicted below.

Venus' sub period - troubles to relatives.

Sun’s sub period - initial troubles from govern-
ment which will soon be sorted out.

Moon’s sub period - indigestion, dysentery, en-
mity with relatives, danger to maternal relatives, and
distress to relatives in general. The subject will
receive a mix of good and bad, but be generally
happy.

Mars' sub period - troubles to son, wedding of a
daughter (if of marriageable age).

Rahu’s sub period - troubles to wife.

3149 - 31521/2, (a) The Major Period of 10th
Lord: During the sub period of the 2nd lord ix the
dasa of the lord of the 10th the native will have his
first issue. ("Seemantha" is a Vedic function related
to birth of the first issue.) The sub period of the 12th
lord, in the dasa of the 10th lord will in the initial part
cause mental distress and happiness in the middle
part. ("Swaraja gnatinasanam" is irrelevant denoting
destruction of royal relatives.) The sub period of the
3rd lord will cause distress in performing royal
duties. Happiness will come to pass in the sub period
of the 9th lord while there will be yoga (prosperity)
in the sub period of the ascendant lord.

(b) Remarriage: Destruction of wife will occur
in the junction of 7th lord’s dasa. Immediately,
happiness will be restored due to remarriage, and the
subject will have more prosperity.

Notes: (a) The Moon’s dasa, Mars sub period
will be favourable for obfaining progeny. Mercury;s
Sub period in this dasa will give mixed effect. Jupi-
ter’s sub period will lead to professional failures.

The sub period of Venus will grant prosperity.

The results of sub periods noted above are in the
Moon’s dasa, and for a person born in Libra ascend-
ant.

(b) Junction of the 7th lord’s dasa is end of the
dasa of the Moon and the beginning phase of Mars’
dasa. Mars should be specially well-placed to give a
second marriage and more progress.

3173 - 3176. (a) Jupiter in strength placed in the

12th, or in aspect thereto, denotes that the native of
Mudgara Nadiamsa will attain Heavens after quitting
his mortal coil.

(b) The lord of the 12th being related to Jupiter
by aspect orconjunction and occupying the Navamsa
of the 7th lord’s dispositor, will also cause attainment
of Heavens due to the mercy of Lord Siva. Due to the
merits of present birth, he will next time have an
excellent rebirth. Later he will be freed from rebirths.

(c) Only those planets that are in Upachaya
houses will have full strength and can bestow health
and longevity.

Notes: Instructions noted in “a” and “b” are
clear.

(c) This is a general rule applicable to any
ascendant. Planets with strength in 3rd, 6th, 10th or
11th can promote one’s health and life span.

However based on my experience, a strong
planet in the 6th house is found to be a source of
misery for physical well-being.

3177 - 3180. According to Rudra Yamala: If
the Sun is in the Sth house in aspect to his son (i.c.
Saturn), donation of gingili cakes will cause relief
from abdominal disorders. The image should be
obtained made of gingili cakes, with two diamond-
studded hands, three eyes and covered with red robes.
The Sun God should be worshipped as prescribed by
Sastras, before donating gingili cakes. This secret is

mentioned in Rudra Yamala. This will increase the
years of life span and will grant health and give good
## Page 70

Deva Keralam 53

fortunes.

Notes: There is some confusion in composition
of the relevant part of the text about the image. The
God concerned is not mentioned. Three eyes do not
denote the Sun-God. Could it be of Lord Siva?

The essence of the other portion is: The Sun in
the 5th associated with Satur is capable of causing
dangerous abdominal disorders to the extent of cur-
tailing life-span. This can be overcome by suitable
worship of the Sun God, and donation of gingili
cakes. Gingili comes under Saturn’s domain.

3184 - 3186. According to Manu: The image of
one white-footed zodiac will please the Nava Grahas.
By donation of such image longevity. health and
happiness will result, and fear of untimely death will

be destroyed. A decorated pot filled with sacred
water should be kept on the heap of fresh grains and
the zodiacal image should be placed there. At the end
of Homa (worship of sacred fire), the donation sug-
gested should be made.

3187 - 3188. Jupiter Dasa - Venus sub period:
For one born in Mudgara Nadiamsa, predict the
following effects in the sub period of Venus during
the dasa of Jupiter. His enemies will turn into friends.
He will acquire wealth. His undertakings will bear
fruits. Some distress will occur due to disaster. He
will consume sweet food and drinks, and acquire
costly robes and jewelry. He will gain wealth and
lands and be very happy. His valour, enthusiasm and
prowess will be on the increase and alas, he will ever
be close to Fire God (i.e. he will perform Homas etc.
ona regular basis).

Notes: These two slokas, and sloka 3192 de-
scribe effects of Jupiter’s dasa, Venus sub period.
Generally favourable description is made except an
abortion to wife.

3200 - 3206. Jupiter’s 3rd Round of Transit:
Fora native of Mudgara Nadiamsa, during the third
## Page 72

Deva Keralam 55

round of transit, Jupiter will give followingeffects: In
the Ist and 9th, he will give wealth. Inthe 11th - there
will be fear from enemies. Happiness, comforts and
auspiciousness will prevail during his transit in the
twelfth. When in the 8th he will cause birth of a son,
acquisition of jewels and loss of a boy for one of his

kinsfolk. Due to an afflicted Satum in transit in.

Scorpio, royal enmity will come to pass. Later hap-
piness, royal favour and wealth will be acquired.
When Jupiter comes to-the sign represented by the
Navamsa occupied by the 11th lord, the subject will
obtain invaluable articles, conveyances etc. When
Jupiter is in the 3rd house in transit, he will acquire
cows and clothes. Inthe 11th and 12th, the planet will
give more gains. In the 7th it will bestow rulership of
a region apart from a high degree of scholarship.
Again in the 3rd there will be some distress in general,
but auspicious results wil] mature during the Sun’s
transit in evil signs. Jupiter ina trine to 3rd will cause
unhappiness among relatives. In the 4th, he will give
happiness and birth of a son. Transiting in Sth, the
planet will cause great distress and involvement in
blameworthy deeds. Later happiness will prevail.

Notes: Jupiter in the 3rd round giving favourable
effects while in transit on the Moon sign is notewor-
thy. So also bad effects while transiting the 11th from
the natal Moon.

When Jupiter transits the 8th from the Moon, as
Saturn transits the 6th from the ascendant, will cause
professional debacles.

While movinginthe 11th fromthe Moon, Jupiter
is adverse in the third round; he will be auspicious
when he moves in the sign represented by the natal
Navamsa of the 11th lord from the ascendant, that is
Mars.

Even in the 12th from the Moon, transit Jupiter
will give gains.

In the 3rd from the Moon, the planet Jupiter will
give gains apart from distress. But he will prove
favourable during the adverse movements of Saturn.

Transiting in the 7th/11th, he will cause troubles
to relatives.

While Jupiter is in the Sth from the Moon, one
should protect himself from questionable deeds.

3207. Jupiter’s 4th Round of Transit: For a
native of Mudgara Nadiamsa, the 4th round of transit
Jupiter will cause following results. In the sign Pisces
and in the initial portion of Aries, he will cause
mental agony, and in Taurus distress of a great
magnitude.

Notes: In this round, the whole of Pisces will be
adverse for Jupiter’s transit. As for Aries, with his
advancing movements, he will become mild. But
again with transit Jupiter in Taurus in the 12th, the
person will be highly troubled.

3217 - 3218. Jupiter in Virgo Navamsa: [he
ascendant should be Leo, with Leo Navamsa. Jupiter
Rabu should be in the rising sign while Jupitershould
be specifically in Virgo Navamsa. As a result of this
yoga, the person will prosper in royal service. His
father would be famous during the native’s child-
hood. The native will possess an attractive body, be
fond of women, be always libidinous, be regarded by
his kinsfolk, be not righteous, be skillful in perform-
ing valorous deeds and will have the fortunes of
acquiring education in many places.

Notes: The first line of sloka 3217 is rectified in
order to get proper concept of the yoga. Further the
words “Rahu Samsthithe” should read as “Rahu
Samyuthe”,

Three simultaneous conditions should exist as
under:

1. Leo ascendant (13° 20' to 16° 40') giving the
same Leo Navamsa for the ascendant.

2. Jupiter and Rabu in Leo.

3. Jupiter in Virgo Navamsa (i.e. in Leo 16° 40'
to 20° 0’).

Then the person will reap the prescribed effects.

3227 - 32291/2. Moon in Mohana Nadiamsa:
(a) The Moon in Mohana Nadiamsa and conjunct
Saturn will produce the following effects for a Leo
native. His parents will be long-lived. His father
would have two marriages. The person will gain great
fortunes in his old age and will enjoy comforts like a
king.

Mohana Nadiamsa may be referred to in the
notes under sloka 1599, Book I.

(b) The Moon in Mohana Nadiamsa (without
reference to Saturn) will give the undermentioned
results for one born in Leo ascendant. The person will
be devoted to serve Lord Siva. He will have three
paternal uncles endowed with long lives. According
to some it will be four. His maternal aunt’s daughter
will be endowed with sons, limited fortunes and
auspiciousness. After some interval she will lose her

brother, and will predecease her husband.
Also see sloka 3235.

donating "Naga Pasa” (Varuna’s weapon), auspi-

3271. Venus Sub Period: In any dasa, the sub

3272. General Clue: Take a Bhava. The dasa of
the lord of the 8th therefrom will adversely affect that
bhava in his very sub period.

Notes: This is a general rule. It is not restricted
to Leo alone.

The major period of the 8th lord from a given
Bhava will adversely affect the Bhava concerned.
While in some cases, this holds good in some it does
not. Sufficient skill is needed to apply this aphorism.

In case of Aries, the 3rd is Gemini. The 8th lord
therefrom is Saturn whose dasa can cause troubles to
one’s brother. For this ascendant, 5th house is Leo.
Jupiter is the 8th lord from Leo. His dasa affecting
progeny may not be that simple.

Similarly the reader can work out details for
other ascendants.

3277 - 3278. Capricorn Ascendant - Kalikz
Nadiamsa: The native of first half of this Nadiamsa
will be a Soodra, 2nd or 3rd issue of the family and
will be destructive for his older brother. His fathe1
will be present at the time of his birth. During birth,
the child will be entangled in umbilical cord.

Notes: The subject belonging to Kalika
Nadiamsa’s first half in Capricorn ascendant cannot
be the first issue of the family. He will be either the
2nd or 3rd issue only.

His older brother/s will die prematurely.

His birth will be with some complications. There
will be no such complication if the conditions laid
down in sloka 3285 are available.

Kalika Nadiamsa rules as under: from 14° 24' to
14° 36' in movable signs; from 15° 24' to 15° 36' in
fixed signs; and from 29° 24' to 29° 36’ in common
signs.

3289 - 32921/2. Infantile Mortality & Rem-
edies: For birth in the first half of Kalika Nadiamsa,
the 8th lord in the ascendant in a benefic’s Navamsa
and in the company ofa benefic will cause Balarishta
or infantile mortality. For two or three weeks in the
first dasa, orin the first sub period of the 2nd dasa, this
fearwill exist. To overcome this, worship of animage
of the Moon god made of silver placed ona bell-metal
vessel and the image of Sun-God made of gold robed
with red apparels be done. Donations after worship
should be given away. Following these measures,
health and longevity will improve.

3297 - 3299. Second Half: (a) For a native of
second half of Kalika Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascend-
ant, childhood will commence with happiness (with-
out Balarishta). He will be endowed with brothers
and sisters and will have a difficult calling.

(b) If the dispositor of the 8th lord is exalted and
strong while Jupiter occupies ascendant with a ben-
efic Navamsa, the subject will enjoy longevity.

(c) If the said Jupiter placed in the ascendant is
in a malefic’s Navamsa, life-span will be limited.

Notes: (a) Professional upheavals are indicated
in this case.

(b) The Sun’s dispositor should be exalted. Ju-
piter though in debility in the ascendant should be in
a benefic’s Navamsa. With these two conditions life-
span will be long.

(c) Short life will come to pass if Jupiter in
Capricorn ascendant is in a Navamsa of a malefic
planet.

3300 - 33011/2. Infantile Mortality: (a) If the
Moon is in extremis and be in Scorpio Navamsa,
without a benefic’s aspect, infantile mortality will
exist in case of birth in the 2nd half of the said
Nadiamsa. ;

(b) The Moon begetting the company of Jupiter
and being with another benefic or if Jupiter is in the
7th, this blemish will not exist.

Notes: (a) A planet is said to be in extremis or in
adead state if itis inthe last six degrees ofan odd sign,
or in the first six degrees of an even sign. To get
Scorpio Navamsa, remaining in extremis, the Moon
should be in Gemini, Libra or Aquarius only.

(b) The Moon joining two benefics - repeat two
## Page 81

64 Chandra Kala Nadi

benefics - including Jupiter will give longevity to a
Capricorn native; alternatively, Jupiter alone in
Cancer will be sufficient.

3302 - 33041/2. Paralysis & Breathing Disor-
ders: Note if birth is in the former half of Kalika
Nadiamsa in Capricorn ascendant. In that case Jupi-
ter should be in the ascendant aspecting the Juminar-
ies (the Sun and the Moon). The Sun should be in
Halaahala Shashtiamsa. This yoga will cause the
following effects. The person will possess a blood-
red and symmetric body, broad eyes and a charming
nose. During childhood, he will suffer from breathing
disorders and paralysis. In the 2nd year he will be
greatly in danger. After 3rd or Sth year he will be
happy with a strong physique with sound health.

Notes: There is no Shashtiamsa as Halaahala
(great destructive poison emerged at the time of
churning Milk Ocean by gods and demons, and
swallowed by Lord Siva). There is however Garala
(poison) Shashtiamsa which extends from 4 deg ()' to
4 deg 30' of odd signs, and from 25 deg 30' to 26 deg
0' of even signs. Perhaps our author used this syno-
nym.

3305 - 3309. Saturn & Mars: Saturn in own
sign, own Navamsa or in exaltation in aspect to Mars
will cause a happy childhood. The person will be
happy after eight, in particular. He will eat limited
food, will be given to enjoyment of pleasures, be
charitable, famous, devoted to Lord Siva, be skillful
in writing and learning, be fond of Panchakshari
Mantra, be disposed to sing the praise of the Lord, and
be honourable. He will be attached to Lord Siva, be
charitable, be helpful to others, be passionate and will
be more intelligent than his father. He will have two
maternal uncles and two paternal uncles and be
attached to latter two. He will have a paternal aunt
who will have a long-living husband and be auspi-
cious for the family.

achiever.

3333 - 3339. Family Lineage: One born in the
second half of Kalika Nadiamsa will not have his
lineage grow (i.e. will be childless). The Sun in
Halahala Shashtiamsa will help the paternal uncle of
the native of former half Kalika Nadiamsa grow his
family. Further the native will enjoy many pleasures
after 22 years ofage. The king of his country will live
long(?) The native through his paternal uncle will
enjoy comforts of many women and children(?) His
prosperity will increase after 27 and he will be much
happy. He will be learned, will be ingenious, knowl-
edgeable about Siva Purana. His marriage will occur
in the 25th year. His 16th year will endanger his
father. The sub period of a malefic in the dasa of 8th
lord from the Moon could (also) endanger the father.
(Or) When Saturn arrives at the sign represented by
the Navamsa occupied by the 4th lord, father will be
destroyed. Saturn moving in the 8th sign will cause
sickness to the native’s paternal uncle. In the absence
of this effect, the native will incur royal enmity in his
first dasa. Later he will recover health and be happy.
In the junction period of first and second major
periods, he will be distressed.

Notes: Certain irrelevant hints relating to the
king etc. are found in the text above which may be
expunged.

For Halaahala Shashtiamsa. see notes under
sloka 3302 - 3304 supra.

3366 - 33671/2. Sun - Mercury Conjunction:
For birth in Sama Nadiamsa, if the Sun is in the 10th
house, joining at the same time Mercury in a dual
Navamsa, the person will be given to anger and be
pleased instantly; he will have two wives and be
passionate. Instead of dual Navamsa, if the Sun so
placed joins Mercury in Taurus Navamsa, there will
be two long-living sisters and a long-living older
brother. The two sisters will enjoy abundant prosper-
ity.

Notes: The Sun in this case in a dual Navamsa
denotes two wives to the native, while in Taurus
Navamsa two sisters are indicated, instead of two
wives. Thus the Sun in Taurus eliminates the possi-
bility of a second marriage. A shrewd astrologer can
profitably understand different uses of Navamsa.

Also see sloka 3371 infra.

of second half of Sama Nadiamsa in Leo ascendant is
described thus. He will be skilled in the interpretation
of internal sentiments by external gestures, be charm-
ing faced, skillful, timid, learned and famous.

(b) The Native: Now the native’s qualities are
explained. He will be black-bodied, intelligent,
helpful to others, learned in two languages, a believer
in God, learned in all religions, liberal (or eloquent)
and will have firm happiness.

Deva Keralam
(Chandra Kala Nadi)

Part Two

by Venkatesa

Sa ageMse we TMT PTA We I

1. I, Venkatesa, belonging to Kasyapa Gotra,
respectfully salute Lord Venkateswara, the Glori-
ous, and narrate effects (of astrological combina-
tions) for the (pleasure of the) king.

Notes: For the part from sloka 1 above till the
end, i.e. sloka No.4775 appearing hereafter, the
author's name is givenas Venkatesa. The name of the
author in the earlier portion is noted as Achyuta. We
do not know whether it is the same author with a
different name, or an entirely different author. But
the language used in the original seems to be from one
and the same person.

In the present context, the Goira of the author is
given as Kasyapa and hence he was a descendant of
sage Kasyapa.

[Kasyapa was a mythical sage, husband of Aditi
and twelve other daughters of Daksha. By Aditi, he
was father of Adityas and of Maha Vishnu. By his
other twelve wives, he was father of demons, Nagas,
reptiles, birds and all kinds of living things. He was
one of the seven Great Rishis (Sapta Rishis) and priest
of Parasu Rama and Lord Sri Rama Chandra.]

The author Venkatesa was apparently enthused
by some royal patronage to compile the present work.
He should not be confuséd with Sarvartha
Chintamani's author, Venkatesa Daivagna, who in
fact belonged to Bharadwaja Gotra.

Lord Venkatesa invoked by our author is an
incarnation of Lord Vishnu and resides on Spata gins,
the Seven Hills, in Tirupati.

Suet 7 amet yodat farsrya: |

Se yefrears AT STAT I? I

4 tasferfrae affrser sete: |
deat fafsamte: WeraATaa: I2

2-3. This science should never be told to wicked
souls, particularly who are rulers. Nor should itever
be passed on to wicked students, nor to those that are
childless or fickle-minded. The astrologershould be
one who has won anger, is truthful and is rid of
jealousy.

to others (i.e. one should remain immune to distur-
bances), and silently pray the lord of his heart, i.e. his
family deity. Aftera study of the Bhavas, everything
(relevant) should be declared (in respect of a given
horoscope).

5 - 91/2. Note: The concept given here is not full
and thus not clear. Unless relevant sutras are sup-
plied, the meaning is difficult to grasp. The author
quite briefly introduces Jaimini's school.

From Sri]. Rangacharya's Jaimini Sutramritam
necessary quotations and clarifications for this part of
slokas help our job.

Firstly the relevant original portion is fully re-

produced below as our author's Sutras are incom-
plete.

"Chakram Chaturvidham gneyam aadyam
audayikam smritham |

Dwiteeyam thu
vikruthaakhyam truteeyakam |

Graha chakramchaturthakhyam evam chakrasya
nirnayah |

Bhaavaa dwaadasa lagnaadyaah krama
maudayikam bhaveth |

Yatra krama vyutkramaabhyaam gananam
thvojha yugmayoh |

Prakrutyaakhyam hitachchakram yatra
yugmaujha yosthathaah |

Gananam tadvikruthaakhyam — graha
chakramathochyate |

Lagnaadheesam samaarabhya choththar-
oththarathah sthithaan |

Gnaatwa grahaan chara vasaadraaseen chakra
kramenavai |

Grahaa evam hi bhaavaah syuh lagna vittadi
sangnitaah |

Evam navasu bhageshu vinyasya navasah
grahaan /

karma sthaane api lagnesa nyasya laabhe dhana
sthitham |

Vyayethu shahsta rasistham vinyasyokta
vidhaanatah |

Grahachakramitham proktham phala gnanaaya
surtbhih |/ "

prakrithaakhyam

This relates to computation of Jaimini Dasa and
is a general yardstick for the various kinds of special
Dasas enunciated by the sage. For odd signs, viz.
Aries, Gemini, Leo, Libra, Sagittarius and Aquarius
the counting is in the straight ascending order. For
even signs, viz. Taurus, Cancer, Virgo, Scorpio,
Capricorn and Pisces, the counting is to be reversed.
This method of counting, that is in straight order for
odd signs and in reverse order for even signs, is called
Prakruti Chakra.

Sometimes a converse method is to be adopted.
To wit, the counting is in the reverse order in case of
odd signs, and in straight order in case of even signs.
This is called Vikruti Chakra.

Whether odd sign or even sign, the counting is
universally in straight order. This is called Audaytka
Chakra.

The 4th one is Graha Chakra. This is to be
counted, in a straight manner as per the rules pre-
scribed, from the sign occupied by the lord of the
ascendant. The nextplanet in the Rasi chartis the 2nd
Bhava, its next is the 3rd Bhava. This way after
exhausting the 9 Bhavas with 9 planets, the lord of
the ascendant himself becomes the 10th bhava, the
2nd again becomes the 11th bhava, and the sixth
becomes the 12th Bhava.

From the Rasi of the Dasa concerned, the number
of signs counted up to the sign occupied by the lord
of the Dasa Rasi, minus one, will be the number of
years of the dasa. The Dasa years will never exceed
12. If the dasa lord is in the 7th from the dasa Rasi,
consider 10 years. The dasa years divided by twelve
will yield the durations of the various Buktis. Ac-
cording the Rasi being odd or even, the distribution
should be in direct or reverse order.

ael ATsI i Y HbeTAG URS I 10 -22. Longevity Computation: One's longev-
arena: — ity should be found based on:

(a) lords of ascendant and the 8th;

val ae, ‘ : (b) ascendant and the Moon;
fearraary CTT PAATS HAT STS HANA TOY (c) ascendant and Hora ascendant.
## Page 92

76 Chandra Kala Nadi

In case of mutual contradiction, the span given
by the pair of natal ascendant (Janma Lagna) and
Hora ascendant (Hora Lagna) should only be consid-
ered. The duration of day or night, as the case may
be, should be divided by 12 and the resultant number
should be counted from natal ascendant in direct or
reverse manner according to its being odd or even
signto get Hora Lagna. Two ghatikas anda half make
for one Hora Lagna. The ghatikas elapsed from the
time of sun rise orsun set to birth be distributed @2.5
ghatikas per sign from the ascendant in direct or
reverse manner depending on the ascending sign
being odd or even.

Should the lords of the ascendant and the 8th be
in movable signs, the life span will be full. So also
when the ascendant lord is in a fixed sign while the
8th lord is ina common sign, or the 8th lord ina fixed
sign while the lord of the ascendant is in a dual sign.

Life span will be medium if the two are in dual
signs, or one in fixed sign and the other ina movable
sign.
Short life will result if both of them are in
immovable signs, or one in movable sign and the
other in a common sign.

Ifthese (lords of ascendant and 8th) are placed in
the initial portion, life span will be full. In the
conclusive portions of the signs concerned, these
minimise their contributions. If placed in the middle
portions, the contribution should be ascertained by
tule of three process.

One hundred years of life span is full. 66 yrs of
life span is medium. Short life is for 33 years. In
between the classification should suitably be under-
stood.

Another Method: The ascendant is Dharma.
The 2nd is Artha, The 3rd is Kama. And the 4th is
Moksha. Their respective trines are also known by
similar names (and are called Dharma Artha Kama
Moksha Trikonas). If the Ayur Lagna (explained
below) is in Dharma Rasi as Chaturthamsa Rasi is in
a Moksha Rasi, full length of life will be granted.
When the Ayur Lagna is in Dharma Rasi while
Chaturthamsa Rasi is ina Kama Rasi, life span will
be medium. The Ayur Lagna and Chaturthamsa Rasi
falling in Dharma and Artha Rasis in that order will
give short life. That is if Chaturthamsa Rasi is in the

4th from Ayur Lagna , full life will come to pass; in
the 3rd medium life span, and in the 2nd short life be
predicted. Should the Ayur Lagna and Chaturthamsa
Rasi fall.in the same kind of sign of triad, i.e. both
being Dharma, or Artha, or Kama, or Moksha, the
length of the life will be the least.

Ayur Lagna: Note the Navamsa occupied by the
Moon in a horoscope. Commencing from there
distribute five gahtis persign till birth ghatis fromthe
Sunrise are exhausted. The final sign arrived by this

count is called Ayur Lagna.

Chaturthamsa Rasi: 1.25 ghatis make up for for
one Chaturthamsa Rasi. The remainder obtained in
the process of Ayur Lagna evaluation should be
divided by 4, and distributed at the rate of 1.25 ghati
per sign commencing fromthe Navamsa of the Moon
to get the designated Rasi.

The sign occupied by the lord of the 8th is also
called as Hora Lgana and the one occupied by the lord
of the ascendant is Rasi Lagna. If the lord of the
ascendant becomes Karaka for longevity, the compu-
tationwill be specially revealing. Otherwise, the sign
occupied by the lord of the 8th be considered as
instructed earlier.

Counting of 8th House - Fixed Signs: The 8th
house concerned for the four fixed signs are - Gemini
for Taurus; Sagittarius for Scorpio; Virgo for Leo;
and Pisces for Aquarius. That is the 8th house for
birth ina fixed sign is counted from the oppositesign
thereof in a direct manner.

Destruction of A Bhava: If the dispositor of a
Bhava is in the 6th, 8th or 12th counted from the
ascendant, the original Bhava in question is de-
stroyed. .

The Three Khandas: The foursigns commenc-
ing from the ascendant form first Khanda; the next
four the 2nd Khanda, and the last four the 3rd
Khanda. The respective Khandas occupied by ben-
efic or exalted planets will be congenial for the
incarnation of an emperor. For others, the considera-
tion should be according to the horoscope concerned.
Malefics or planets in debility in these Khandas will
cause difficulties.

Aroodha Lagna: Note the number of signs the
lord of a Bhava is away from the Bhava in question.
Count so many signs from the lord concerned to get
## Page 93

Deva Keralam 77

its Aroodha. In case of odd signs the counting is from
that very sign. If even sign is involved, the counting
is from the opposite sign.

Notes: In these slokas, firstly the well-known
principle of life span being long, medium or short is
incompletely conveyed in the first instance. In the
second instance calculation of Savayana Hora Lagna
is prescribed.

(a) Use of lords of ascendant and 8th based on
Jaimini's Sutra "Aayuh pitru dinesaabhyaam": If
both these lords are in movable sign/s, long life is
indicated. If one is ina fixed sign while the other is
in a dual sign, then,again full life span will come to
pass. Medium life span will result if one is in a
movable sign and the other is inan immovable sign.
Short life is denoted by both these planets being in
immovable signs. The same is the case when one of
them is ina movable sign and the otherina dual sign.

(b) Use of ascendant and Moon sign should also
be done with the same guidelines, replacing the pair
of planets at "a".

(c) Again with the help of Janma Lagna (natal
ascendant) and Hora Lagna, similar assessment be
made.

If the indications as per the three methods are
identical, itshould be accepted as final. Should there
be contradictions, the indication given by the pair of
Janma Lagna and Hora Lagna is alone final.

(There is a school of thought that if two pairs
yield identical hints, that alone be considered.)

The method of Hora Lagna calculation given by
our text is used to find out what is called Saavayava
Hora Lagna.

Other matters discussed in the slokas are clear.

23 - 24. Matta Matanga Yoga: The lords of

angles and trines should be in their own signs, or in -

a sign that exalts the lord of the ascendant, or should
be in angles/trines (ie. angular lords in trines and

trina] lords in angles). Then the yoga produced goes
under the name of Matta Matanga Yoga. One bornin

25. The said Matta Maatanga Yoga will be
nullified if the lord of the ascendant occupies an
inimical sign or the sign of his debility. One born in
the said yoga (when in tact) will be wealthy owning
limitless sums.

Breathe aeate ys adhe sat

26. Malaviya Yoga: Venus in strength in an
angle identical with his own sign or sign of exaltation
will cause what is called Malaviya Yoga. The person
born in this yoga will be the lord of a number of
elephants, horses, chariots and palanquins, apart
from lands, forts and the like. He will be an ocean of
numerous virtues, be endowed with an excellent
wife, attached to other women, will win over the lord
of men (i.e. the king) and will enjoy pleasures.

Notes: Malaviya yoga is formed in the following
ways.

Venus in Pisces in case of Gemini, Virgo, Sag-
ittarius and Pisces ascendants (dual signs).

Venus in Libra in case of Aries, Cancer, Libra
and Capricorn ascendants (movable signs).

Venus in Taurus in case of Taurus, Leo, Scorpio
and Aquarius ascendants (immovable signs).

Thus al] the 12 ascendants enjoy this yoga with
Venus in a specified place.

It comes to our notice, in the course of our
studies, that Venus in debilitation Navamsa is greatly
crippled of its possible superior role through Malaviya
Yoga. So is again the case if he joins Mercury closely
in Pisces, oris combust in any of the signs concerned.

Incase of the yoga formed by exalted Venus, his
dispositor, Jupiter, should not be in the company of
Saturn. If that be the case, the person will be in the
receiving end, instead of enjoying Maha Purusha
Yoga effects. (Refer to sloka 27 infra.)
## Page 94

78 Chandra Kala Nadi

When Venus in Libra or Taurus forms this yoga,
the question of dispositor does not arise. Here
Saturn’s influence onJupiterdoes notspoil the Yoga.

_ As per our text, Malaviya Yoga gives rich con-
veyances, landed and housing properties, association
with royal (or powerful) men and enjoyment of
pleasures.

Other effects stated elsewhere are as under. The
person with this yoga will have thin lips. He will have
wheatish complexion, thin waist, and will shine like
the moon in appearance. His voice in respect of
majesty will be comparable to an elephant’s voice.
His teeth will be white. He will obtain rulership of
certain kingdoms. His life span will be 70 and death
will be in a shrine.

His earnings will be by his own efforts.

ate wige ee aresdtarragar |
qed ae refs FE: 2 I

27. Cancellation: In the process of the above
yoga being present, Jupiter joining Saturn will nullify
the yoga whereupon the exaltation (note the term
“exaltation”) effects of Venus will go in vain. And
the person will be troubled due to planetary blemish-
es.

Notes: It is to be noted that Malaviya yoga
caused by Venus being in Pisces in an angle will be
nullified by Jupiter’s association with Saturn. Thus
the underlying concept is Malaviya yoga caused by
Venus in Libra or Taurus, being angular, will remain
unaffected by Jupiter-Saturn conjunction.

31. Three planets in their respective own signs
will produce pleasures. Their being in the Navamsas
owned by Yogakarakas (significators of prosperity)
will give a comfortable life. Their weakness and
occupation of Navamsas owned by Avayoga Karakas
(obstructors to prosperity, contrary to Yoga Karaka)
will make living difficult. Two planets in own signs
will (also) give pleasures; in the Navamsas of Yoga
Karakas, one will be blessed with Raja Yoga. Four
planets in exaltation signs will usher abject poverty.

32. (a) Ifa planet is debilitated in Rasi but begets
his exaltation Navamsa, the person will be rich and
will enjoy many pleasures. If the said debilitated
planet is in the Navamsa of a Yoga Karaka, birth in
a prosperous family is denoted.

(b) Loss of honour, difficulties, courageous dis-
position, miserliness and prominently proneness to
diseases are the effects (for four planets in exalta-
tion).
## Page 95

Deva Keralam 79

Notes: (a) Richness and pleasures will follow a
planet that occupies its exaltation Navamsa though
debilitated in Rasi. Example: Venus inthe sign Virgo
with Pisces Navamsa.

Again, being in debility, ifthe planet occupies a
Navamsa owned by a favourable planet with refer-
ence to a given ascendant, one’s birth will be ina
prosperous family. Example: Cancer ascendant, the
Moon in debility in Scorpio, but with a Jupiterian
Navamsa. Advanced students will well realise,
Scorpio Navamsa, though ruled by Mars, the best
planet for Leo, is not a welcome position in this case.

(b) Results given at “b” should strictly be in-
cluded to the planet in debilitation sign, with Yoga
Karaka Navamsa. But that is not a sensible thing to
do. These are part of results of four planets in
simultaneous exaltation, vide 4th line in the original
sloka 31 above. It is clear that these lines have
wrongly been appended in the present place. Hence
we can put the results as under in one place for easy
understanding.

Four planets simultancously exalted cause ab-
ject poverty, loss of honour, difficulties, miserliness,
and proneness to diseases apart from the only good
effect, viz. courageous disposition.

33 - 34, Adhi Yoga: In the formation of
Chandradhi Yoga, should the Moon be endowed with
full rays, the person concerned will be the ruler of the
earth, be strong, will enjoy pleasures, will own
wealth, elephants etc. With benefics in the 7th, 6th
or(and) 8th from the Moon (orascendant, as “Tasmin”
reads as “Lagnam” in another version), Adhi Yoga is
formed. As a result one will be an army chief,

minister or king and be endowed with wealth, com-
forts, might and vanquished enemies. He will be
long-lived and will be free from fear of illness.

Notes: The text refers only to Chandradhi Yoga.
Lagnadhiyoga being equally important and similar,
suitable addition in brackets is made by me.

Normally, commentators interpreted that
benefics (that is the three natural ones) in the 7th
produce an army chief, in the 6th - a minister, and in
the 8th - a king. One way they may be right. Then
the inference is that the 8th having the three benefics
produces the best Adhi yoga followed by 6th and 7th,
in that order.

Whether itis Lagnadhiyoga or Chandradhiyoga,
the Moonshould have undiminished rays. In the first
line of sloka 33, we find the term “Poornamsabhaage”.
Thave not tried to enrich the interpretation with some
new meanings. Removing redundant possibilities, I
have given a practical interpretation.

Also see sloka 36 and others infra.

("Antarbhava" reads as "Antarbhaye" in another

elephants.

against the Sth house by Deva Keralam.

43. If all the planets occupy variously their own
signs, own Navamsas, friendly divisions, or be in
Deeptamsa (i.e. Deeptavastha), own decanates, an-
gles, or be in Muditavastha, Moolatrikona positions,
or endowed with temporary strength (strength at the
time of birth), or be in Vargottama Navamsa, they
will cause auspiciousness and happiness in their
(dasas and) sub periods.

Notes: Deeptavastha: A planet in his exaltation
sign attains this Avastha or state. (Deeptha = blaz-
ing.)

Muditavastha: Being in a close friend’s sign.
Mudita denotes happiness; also known as Pramudita.

These two Avasthas or states are among nine
suchstates relating to the positions of various planets.
## Page 97

Deva Keralam 8]

Temporary strength = Strong in Shadbala or six
sources of strength. These are Sthaana bala (positional
strength), Digbala (directional strength), Kaala Bala
(temporal strength inclusive of Ayana Bala), Cheshta
Bala (motional strength), Naisargika Bala (natural
strength) and Drikbala (aspectual strength), For
details consult relevant standard text books describ-
ing this aspect.

48 - 51. Chaamara Yoga: (a) The lord of the 9th
in the company of the lord of the 4th and being in
exaltation while Venus is in the 5th from the ascend-
ant, will cause Chaamara Yoga. The native of Aries
ascendant with this Yoga will enjoy prosperity (in
general) (and more so) after the age of sixteen. He
will be a king, or be rich and happy.

(b) In case of Chaamara Yoga occurring to
Cancer or Aries ascendant, with Venus in an angle or
a trine, there will be a “Raja Yoga”. The person
belonging to Chaamara Yoga willenjoy Yoga effects
fromthe age of 12. Butthe twelfth yearwillusher fear
from untimely death. If he survives this danger, long
life is assured.

Notes: (a) According to our text, the 9th lord
should be exalted and be with the lord of the 4th.
Venus should also be in the 5th from ascendant. Then
the yoga in question forms.

Two more kinds of yoga with this name is
explained by Parasara thus.

First, the ascendant lord should be exalted in an
angle and be in aspect to Jupiter. Saturn, Mars, and
Mercury can be exalted this way; that is the ascend-
ants concerned, according to this axiom, could be
Aries, Gemini, Virgo and Capricorn.

Parasara’s second type of yoga is two benefics
jointly should be in the ascendant, 7th, 9th or 10th.
The effects for either kind of Chaamara Yoga are:
royal status, royal honour, long life, scholarship,
eloquence and high rate of knowledge in all arts.

Mantreswara gives yet another situation for this
yoga. The ascendant should contain a benefic while
its lord beina good house (Bhava) or in his exaltation
sign. The effects are long life, increasing prosperity,
fame, virtues and leadership.

Thus the Chaamara yoga is described in four
different ways by different authorities.
## Page 98

82 Chandra Kala Nadi

"Chaamara" is chowrie, a royal insignia.

(b) It is not known why our authorall ofa sudden
adds angular position for Venus which is not speci-
fied in “a” above in the original. Then he calls it a
(mere) Raja Yoga relating to Cancer or Aries ascend-
ing.

Anyway the clues given hereof will serve the
reader to suitably assess this yoga. At best one can
ignore the name and look upto effects laid down.
After all a rose is a rose, call it with any name.

55 - 59, Lakshmi Yoga: The Moon in her
exaltation sign with radiant and multiple rays, Mer-
cury in the 7th, the Sun in the 6th, Venus in the Sth,
Jupiter in the ascendant, and Saturn with Mars in the
3rd - the native with this planetary array will enjoy
Rajya Lakshmi Yoga and will be the lord of the earth.
Further he will be a learned person, owning lands, be
dear to the daughters of the king, and will be ever
blessed with the mercy of Goddess Lakshmi. After
the age of 25, his prosperity will be on the rise;
particularly after 30. He will acquire huge wealth in
the 16th year which will also be a year of fear of
untimely death and his body will be grounded to the
earth in a war. If he survives he will live happily
without diseases and with a strong physique. In his
71st year or in 61st year, he will incur death without
fail.

Notes: Minus the position of the nodes, this
seems to be a specific horoscope taken by the author
froma Nadi work. Calling the entire yoga as Lakshmi
Yoga or Rajya Lakshmi yoga is just not that impor-
tant.

60. Akhanda Samrajya Yoga: Out of the lords
## Page 99

Deva Keralam 83

of 11th, 10th and 2nd houses counted from the
ascendant, even if one is in an angle to the Moon, the
native will be the ruler of an undivided kingdom (i.e.
will be an emperor of large area). Simultaneously,
Jupitershould be the ruler of one of 2nd, 5th and 11th
houses counted from the ascendant.

Notes: Akhanda Samrajya Yoga giving rulership
of a vast united land is applicable to all the four
immovable ascendants (not tc Scorpio and Aquarius
alone as commonly taught by many writers, ancient
as wellas modern) if we carefully study the rulership
required for Jupiter. He can rule one of the three
houses, viz. 2nd, 5th and 11th for Taurus, Leo,
Scorpio and Aquarius. For Taurus, he is the 1 1thlord.
For Leo he rules the Sth. For Scorpio he rules two
houses, viz. 2nd and Sth. For Aquarius, he is the lord
of 2nd and 11th.

Now, this yoga can form in one of the following
four manners.

(a) For Taurus ascendant, one among the three
planets, Mercury, Saturn and Jupiter should be in an
angle to the Moon.

(b) For Leo, one of the two planets, Mercury or
Venus should be in an angle to the Moon.

(c) For Scorpio, one of the three planets Jupiter,
Sun and Mercury should be in an angle to the Moon.

(d) For Aquarius, one of the two planets, Jupiter
and Mars should be in an angle to the Moon.

Akhanda Samrajya Yoga thus applies to neither
a movable ascendant nor a dual ascendant. That is,
Aries, Gemini, Cancer, Virgo, Libra, Sagittarius,
Capricomand Pisces do not obtain Akhanda Samrajya
Yoga.

are Sra OY Peerage |

61 - 62. Cancellation of Akhanda Samrajya
Yoga: This yoga wil] stand nullified, if a malefic is
in the 8th or 12th from the immovable ascendant
(concerned). In that event (apart from not getting the
good effects) the native will live a grief-ridden life
and will have somewhat defective a physique. The

formation of a (true) Samrajya Yoga will nullify
other yogas causing penury.

Notes: When the said yoga is formed as persloka
60, there should be no malefic planet (Saturn, Mars,
Rabu, Ketu, weak Moon, ill-associated Mercury) in
the 8th or 12th from the said immovable ascendant.
The prohibition ofa malefic in 8th or 12th should be
applied to only that immovable ascendant which
forms the basis of this Yoga. Looking fora maleficin
8th/12th from all the four immovable ascendants will
be too much.

The Moon being weak if placed in the 12th or 8th
from the ascendant, while the other condition of this
yoga remains fulfilled, will nullify this yoga.

Samrajya Yoga is a short-term for Akhanda
Samrajya Yoga. As a result of this yoga, the person
will be wealthy and highly prosperous, ifnot literally
an emperor. This is a good yoga for occupying
prominent positions of national importance, political
or apolitical.

63 - 68. (a) Yogas With Reference to Moon:
Four different yogas named Uttama (excellent),

Madhyama (moderate), Adhama (mean) and
## Page 100

84 Chandra Kala Nadi

Adhamaadhama (the meanest) are produced (when
planets are in the 10th, 7th, 4th and the 1st with
reference to) the Moon. With the last mentioned
yoga, (other) yogas in the horoscope become weak;
ineffectiveness thereof should be understood with the
help of directional influences.

(b) Uttama Yoga: One born in this yoga will be
a Satvika, be intelligent, honourable, will have wealth
earned by fair means, will take to good path and be
orthodox.

(c) Madhyama Yoga: This native will serve a
king, be predominantly passionate, will indulge in
both good and bad acts, be educated and intelligent.

(d) Adhama Yoga: One born in this yoga will
ever besickly, be attached to performing unrighteous
deeds, libidinous, unprincipled and wil] live a
wretched life.

(e) Adhamaadhama Yoga: He will be inflicted
by grief, libidinous, mean, be given to severe anger,
fond of promoting quarrels, ever sinful, attached to
the wicked, will have an eye on others’ food and their
spouses and be given to faulting others.

Notes: In a way it can be said that the original’s
spirit is not fully maintained in these six slokas for it
has been recomposed by a later composer without
having any regard to fullness of the conditions and
without giving heed to proper astrological terms.

First of all there is no clear reference to the four
houses involved. These have been supplied by me in
line with the effects enlisted. Further I have my own
doubts about effects given for Adhamaadhama Yoga.

The reader will do well to consider natural
benefics and malefics that form the yoga and take
only relevant principles.

I do not know how the reader will react to my
suggestion that benefics form the first two mentioned
yogas while malefics form the penultimate and last
yoga.

Phala Deepika’s Uttama, Madhyama and
Adhama Yogas may also profitably be seen in its
sixth chapter.

69. Three Planets: With three planets in exalta-
tion, one will be highly intelligent. If three are inown
signs, he will be a minister. A dull-witted person is
born with three planets indebility. He will have grief-
ridden livelihood if three are exalted but in degrees
causing an adverse yoga. If three planets are in
debility but are in degrees causing a favourable yoga,
one will enjoy prosperity and pleasures.

70-71. Maha Panditha Yoga (Yoga for Great
Scholarship): If the Sun and Mercury join ina sign
which is the ascendant and is the place of exaltation
for one of them, or if Jupiter (alone) is in the
ascendantin exaltation, the yoga called Maha Panditha
Yoga is produced. As a result, the person will be a
scholar, ruler of men and land, wealthy, will be
scientific (ormaintaina scriptural viewpoint), learned,

be a good speaker in the assembly of Brahmins, a
protector of secrets, and be wise and virtuous.

Notes: This yoga forms in three ways.

Firstly, the Sun and Mercury can be in Aries
ascendant, where the Sun is exalted.

Secondly, the Sun and Mercury can be in Virgo
ascendant, where Mercury is exalted.

Thirdly, Jupiter can be alone in Cancer rising.

72-78. Jupiter’s Navamsa Positions: (a)Should

Jupiter be in the 10th or 6th with benefic Navamsa,
-the person will be virtuous and highly intelligent.

(b) Jupiter in Sagittarius with Cancer Navamsa,
or in Capricorn with Leo Navamsa, or in Pisces with
Libra Navamsa will cause grief, and deprive the
native of learning and happiness.

(c) Jupiter in the 2nd house obtaining 8th Nav-
amsa while the Moon is in Scorpio Navamsa will
from the age of sixteen cause the effects of “one
yoga”. (This part in sloka 74 is not clear, and is
defective in composition. The meaning is - it will
give effects of one yoga. Obviously this position of
Jupiter is mixed up with the Moon’s Navamsa. The
text wants apparently to suggest that Jupiter in the 8th
Navamsa, placed in the 2nd is not welcome, which
will be clear from “b” above and “d” below.)

(d) Avoiding the 8th Navamsa, Jupiter placed in
the 2nd will give happiness, cducation, sweetspeech,
modesty and fondness for religious merits.

(e) Jupiter in the 2nd house or in the 8th house
with a benefic’s Navamsa will grant learning, clev-
erness in royal circles, and intelligence.

(f) Jupiter placed in an angle or ina trine, with
Pushkara Navamsa will bestow great prosperity. Ifin
the process the planet is weak, or is in 6th/8th/12th
sign from Navamsa ascendant, he will cause grief on
account of a son (or progeny) following the 21st or
31st year. The trinal signs {rom Aries to Pisces (i.e.
trinal signs counted from the ascendant) should simi-
larly be estimated.

Notes: Here the text describes Jupiter in certain
Navamsas.

(a) Being in the 6th or 1Uth in Rasi, he should
occupy his own Navamsa, or that of Mercury/Venus.
He can also be in exaltation Navamsa if the Moon is
full. As a result, the subject will be endowed with

virtues and a high degree of intelligence.

(b) Jupiter in his Moolatrikona sign - Sagittarius
- (from 10° 0' to 13° 20') with exalted Navamsa is not
welcome for happiness and Icarning. So also his
position in the sign Pisces (13° 20' to 16° 40)’ with
Libra Navamsa, and the sign Capricorn - debilitation
sign - (23 deg 20! to 26 40') with Leo Navamsa.

Interestingly, Jupiter in the sign Cancer (23°20!
to 26° 40") with Aquarius Navamsa (the 8th Nav-
amsa) is excluded. Obviously this does not stand in
the way of one’s learning and happiness unless the
Moon is in debility in Navamsa. Please see notes in
“c” below.

See slokas 546 - 553 for effects of Jupiter in
Pisces with Libra Navamsa.

(c) Jupiterin the 2nd house with eighth Navamsa
(23° 20' to 26° 40’) while the Moon is in debilitation
Navamsa will from the age of 16 till the end cause
such effects as to lead to unhappiness and deprival of
learning. The mention of “one yoga” seems to be
wrong and the above interpretation makes sense
keeping the earlier sloka, No.73, in mind while the
8th Navamsa of Cancer (i.e. Aquarius Navamsa) is
not included. In the present context, the Moon in
specified Navamsa position is an additional require-
ment.

(d) Should Jupiter be in the 2nd (in any sign) he
should not be between 23° 20' and 26° 40'. Then he
will grant the specified results. That is, if Jupiter is
in the 2nd with eighth Navamsa, happiness, educa-
tion, speech etc. will be affected adversely.

(e) If Jupiter in the 2nd/8th house gets his own
Navamsa or that of Mercury or Venus, or Cancer
(while the Moon is full in case of Jupiter in Cancer
Navamsa), the person will be well-educated, intelli-
gent, clever enough to enter into high societies.

(f) For Pushkaramasa, see page 239 of Book 1,
Deva Keralam.

onwards are in Pushkara Navamsas the person will
enjoy the blessings of Goddess Lakshmi (i.e. be
opulent), and will enjoy pleasures, fame and happi-
ness.

80. The Sun’s Navamsa Positions: Short life
will come to pass if the Sun is in:

(a) the sign Gemini with Capricorn Navamsa.

(b) the sign Sagittarius with Cancer Navamsa.

(c) the sign Virgo with Aries Navamsa.

Notes: This is a general rule applicable to any
ascendant meaning the Sun in dual signs, excepting
Pisces, has a certain role to play in respect of one’s
life-span.

(a) The Sun in Gemini 10° 0' to 13° 20' getting
Capricorn Navamsa wil] reduce life-span.

(b) So does he when in Sagittarius 10° 0' to 13°
20' getting Cancer Navamsa.

(c) Again life will be short if the Sunis in Virgo
10° 0' to 13° 20' obtaining Aries Navamsa. Please
note Aries, though the exaltation Navamsa of the
Sun, is prohibited being 8th from Virgo.

In these cases, the Sun’s Navamsa positions will
be 8th counted from his sign positions.

Why the Sun in Pisces - another dual sign - with
Libra Navamsa is not added to the list merits special
attention while Aries Navamsa of Virgo is. Practical
horoscopic studies can give us suitable guidance.

81. Danger to Father e/ cetera: Should the Sun
be in the 12th house, or if Saturn is in Aswini, or in
the 7th or its trine, or in the 10th there will be danger
to father etc. in the childhood of the native.

Notes: Father et cetera includes paternal rela-
tives.

The position of the Sun and Saturn are discussed
in the present case.

The Sun in the 12th will cause danger to father
and others in the form of sickness, not necessarily
death. Bhavartha Ratnakara’s dictum that a
significator in the 12th contributes to the growth of
the indications concerned, thus, gets a limited excep-
tion.

Saturn in Aswini Nakshatra will cause the same
effect.

Again Saturn features inthe 3rd, 7th, 10th or 11th
in respect of sickness to the said relatives. From the
3rd and 7th, he aspects the 9th. The 11this the house
of some paternal relatives. Why the 10th comes into
play could be understood with some examination.
The 10th is the 2nd from the 9th which denotes
father’s original family before his marriage.

Of course the two rules involving the Sun and
Saturn are quite general in nature. In the concerned
places, they should not enjoy strength so as to be
adverse.

Prafte sare TUTE Tey 12? II

$2. Evils to Father: If the Moon is in the 5th
house in aspect to Saturn and Mars, the first dasa of
the native will endanger the father. The relevant sub
period will be that of the Dasamsa dispositor of the
first dasa lord.

Notes: Regarding the sub period concerned, we
should verify the Dasamsa chart and find out the
dispositor of the lord of the first dasa. In case that sub
period had already expired before birth, the sub
period of the Moon, Mars or Saturn may be relevant
in the first dasa.

The importance, inthis yoga, is for father’s death
in the very first dasa itself.

$3 - 85. Amala Yoga: (a) If the 10th from lunar
ascendant, i.e, the Moon sign, is in occupation by a
benefic planet, the yoga going under the name Amala
Yoga is formed, giving indestructible and life-long
wealth to the person. The 2nd, 4th and 6th from the

'
## Page 103

Deva Keralam 87

Moon should be free from malefic occupation in this
yoga. So also the 9th sign in Navamsa.

(b) Jupiter (too) in the 10th house from the Moon
produces Amala Yoga. In the Amala Yoga caused by
Jupiter, if Venus aspects the ascendant, one will beget
abundant wealth, be famous and happy.

Notes: (a) Although it is a questionable practice
to find out Amala Yoga from the natal ascendant,
effective one is doubtlessly the one formed by a
benefic (viz. Jupiter, Mercury or Venus) in the 10th
from the Moon.

Two conditions are stipulated by the text which
are not found inothertexts. These are freedom forthe
2nd, 4th and - please note the word “and” - the 6th
from a malefic occupation, while the 9th from Nav-
amsa ascendant should also be free from a malefic.
(Some may possibly interpret that all these four
places are in Navamsa chart.)

Parasara does not allow any other planet, 1.¢. a
malefic, inthe 10th in the formation of this yoga. His
condition is described by the words “Kevalaischa
Subhairyuthe”, that is only benefic in the 10th, to the
exclusion ofa malefic. Inthe list of acquisitions, the
sage does not include wealth while Phala Deepika
does. Our text further enhances the value of this yoga
by the expression - indestructibleand life-long wealth.

(b) Our text specially takes the Amala Yoga
caused by Jupiter in the 10th from the Moon in which
case the aspect of Venus on the ascendant causes
much wealth apart from fame and happiness.

Increased wealth, fame and happiness are addi-
tions to be caused by Venus in simultaneous aspect to
the ascendant.

86-88. Neecha Bhanga Raja Yoga: If the Rasi
lord, or the planet that will be exalted in the sign
containing a debilitated planet, occupies an angle
with reference to the Moon, the subject will become
a king or munificent emperor. One with a planet that
has cancelled debility will become anemperor and be
greatly happy. His prosperity will be on the rise from
his 33rd or 35th year. In the dasa of such a planet,
other rulers will adore the feet of the native, and he
will be plentiful, and his fortunes will consist of gold
and precious stones.

Notes: Although this yoga is quite popular, some
of the effects mentioned here are noteworthy.

The angular position of the planet concerned is
only from the Moon, to the exclusion of the natal
ascendant, as per our author.

$9 - 91. Chatra Yoga: The Moon in the 2nd
house while Venus is in the 9th, 2nd, 3rd, 12th or 11th
from the ascendant will cause Chatra Yoga. The ©
person concerned will be happy, eloquent in speech,
soft-bodied, rich with royal features, learned, intelli-
gent, will have stirring appeal for women, be radiant
akin tothe Sun, endowed with longevity, will become
skillful in worshipping Lord Siva after the age of
twenty, be well introduced in the study of various
Mantras and Agama Sastras, will obtain a son in the
old age, be wealthy, will attain fame through jour-
neys and be worshipped by the king.

Notes: "Chatra" means umbrella, rather a tradi-
tional royal symbol.

While the Moon and Venus form Chatra yoga as
per our work, this yoga is treated as part of Nabhasa
yogas by Parasara, Varaha Mihira etc. According to
## Page 104

88 | Chandra Kala Nadi

them all the (seven) planets should be in seven
continuous houses commencing the 7th house. The
results thereof are the person will be long-lived, be
happy in the beginning and ending parts of his life,
will help his kinsfolk, be a king and be close to many
kings (i.e. will be opulent etc.) and be intelligent.

94. The 8th lord in the 8th while Mercury is inthe
6th will give the following effects. The subject will
be ever anxious to receive charities, be blessed by the
goddess of beauty, be troubled by penury, will un-

dergo numerous difficulties, will attain prosperity

Notes: This is not a good yoga and gives many

be beautiful and quite famous. He will have belated
prosperity.

95. Evil Lords: The 8th lord in the 6th or 12th,
the 6th lord in the 8th or 12th, and the 12th lord in the
6th or 8th, or these three planets in their above-
specified own houses in mutual aspects only between
them (to the exclusion of other association) - this
yoga will make one a king, endowed with distinct
wealth and be praised by the king of kings.

Notes: The yoga simply requires evil lords in
evil houses.

In this context, Uttara Kalamrita’s much popu-
lar Vipareeta Raja Yoga is to be noted.

Lord of 8th in 6th or 12th, lord of 6th in 8th or
12th, or lord of 12th in 6th or 8th or the said three evil
lords connected in any way by exchange, aspect or
conjunction, and simultaneously having no such
relationship with other planets - produces Vipareeta
Raja Yoga. The formation of this yoga is not that
simple; so also its effects. The person concerned will
be “the king of kings”. He will have fame and wealth.

Mahadeva in his Jataka Tatva lays down a
simple rule to the effect that the 8th lord and the 6th
lord interchanging places, or being angular, produce
a mighty and powerful person. This aphorism of
Mahadeva is somewhat akin to sloka 96 infra.

receive a reduction. Thus thc culprit is the 6th lord.

102 - 103. Rajapooja Yoga: Ifthe 9th lord is in
exaltation with exceeding strength, and in aspect to
the Moon, while an angle or trine from the ascendant
is occupied by Mercury, the yoga called Rajapooja
Yoga is produced. One born in this yoga will have
even limbs, will have wealth exceeding ten thousand
(gold coins), (i.e. be very rich), will have no brothers,
be famous, long-lived and will be endowed withsons.

Notes: The name suggested should be Rajapoojya
Yoga instead of Rajapooja Yoga. However royal
honour - true to the name - is not part of the effects,
which are otherwise quite interesting.

“Exceeding strength” refers to a higher number
of units in Shadbala.

Having no brothers (thus becoming the sole
inheritor of ancestral properties) and begetting male
offspring may be noted with special emphasis.

104. Should the lord of the 1st house be in
exaltation or be in Vargottama Navamsa, and be in
aspect to Venus, the native will have self-realisation
through the school of Non-dualilty, be devoted to

Vedantha doctrines, and be a knower of the Al-
mighty.
## Page 106

90 Chandra Kala Nadi

Notes: Advaita Philosophy = Identity of Brahma
(supreme soul) with Jeevatman (human soul).

Vedantha = complete knowledge of the Vedas,
the second and the most important part of Mimamsa,
or third of the three great divisions of Hindu philoso-
phy.

An average reader not properly initiated into
astrology may run the risk of involving the planet
Venus ina lower level of material enjoyments. The
higher plane of Venus should never be missed, as he
is noted to be the able preceptor of demons knowing
many things that were not known even to Deva Guru
or Jupiter. Venus or Bhrigu is said to be the exclusive
knower of imparting life into the dead, known as
Mrita Sanjivani Mantra. He is an unparalleled expert
in Muburta.

Venus is inanangle ora trine, attaining the 12th sign
counted from Navamsa ascendant, the subject will be
relieved of mundane bonds, i.e. will attain Moksha,
final emancipation.

106. Knower of the Almighty: The lord of the
12th counted from the ascendant or the Moon sign
being in Deva Shashtiamsa, in exaltation or with
strength (of other kinds) should be aspected by
Jupiter and be in a Navamsa of Mercury. Then the
person will be interested in doing good deeds and be
a knower of the Almighty.

Notes: Deva Shashtiamsa extends twice in odd
signs - once from 1° 0' to 1° 30' and again from 12°
0' to 12° 30'. As for even signs, it is from 17° 30' to
18°O' and again from 28° 30' to 29° 0’.

107. Should the Moon be in Vignanamsa, the

native will have knowledge of essence of Vedantha,
will have many pupils who in turn will have pupils,
will ever do such routines as taught by the Vedantha.

Notes: Vignanamsa is not a specific standard
term. Seeing terms like Jeevanmukthamsa denoting
the 12th sign from Navamsa Lagna, the term of
Vignanamsa should denote the 9th sign counted from
Navamsa Lagna. The 9th house denotes Vignana or
scientific temper and achievements of a person. We
may not always be right in taking out such meanings
for such terms, because some times they seem to be
wanting in proper editing in the original.

The following slokas containing such unusual
terms, for which we have no clearclues, will confirm
our doubts.

113. Jupiter & 9th Lord: If the lord of the 9th
and Jupiter occupy friendly signs or their respective
exaltation signs or any other auspicious houses,
avoiding evil houses, and be conjuncta benefic, or be
in aspect to their dispositor/s, the native will con-
struct many villages, tanks, towers, towns and gar-
dens. He will befriend virtuous men and be an
excellent person on the earth.

Notes: The 9th lord and Jupiter should be well-
placed as stipulated. Both of them should be with a
benefic or benefics as the case may be. Orthey should
be in aspect to the owners of the signs they are in. For
example, Leo ascendant, the 9th lord Mars with
Jupiter in Virgo aspected by exalted Venus.

One having this yoga will be a successful profes-
sional builder. Other effects are company of virtuous
men and excellence in many ways.

115. Mars aspecting Jupiter: If the planet
Jupiteris in Cancer in exaltation inaspect to Mars, the
person concerned will be the leader of horses, towns,
elephants and many forts. He will be endowed full
life-span. He will own an array of palanquins deco-
rated with ivory and gold. Under the auspices of a
king he will adore a gem-studded diadem and be
served by subordinate kings.

Notes: The netessence of exalted Jupiteraspected
by Mars is longevity, abundant wealth and fame.

Jupiter in Cancer should be aspected by Mars
either from Sagittarius (owned by Jupiter himself),
from Capricorn (Mars in exaltation) or from Aries
(ownership held by Mars).

116. Kahala Yoga: The subject having Kahala
Yoga will have firm thinking, be valorous, be en-
thused by four kinds of traditional armies and will ’
show great courage in a war.

Notes: Kahala Yoga’s formation is not explained
here and we do not know how the original proposed
this yoga. But the effects are quite akin to Parasara’s
stipulation.

As perthe sage, the yoga in question occurs when
the 4th lord and Jupiter are in mutual angles as the
ascendant lord enjoys strength. An alternative for-
mation according to Parasara is by the 4th lord being
in his own orexaltation sign along with the lord of the
10th. The results thereof are: “The person will be
energetic, adventurous, cunning, endowed with a
complete army consisting of chariots, elephants,
horses and infantry, and will lord over a few vil-
lages.”.

“Foolishness” is also a part of Kahala Yoga
according to some Tamil textbooks.

The reader may further refer to Jatakadesa
Marga, Phala Deepika and Jataka Parijata for fur-
ther information.
