126 - 127. Mani Pravala Yoga: (a) This yoga is
formed in one of the following three manners:

(1) A benefic exalted in the 2nd or the 3rd while
a malefic is in debility.

(2) A benefic exalted in the 4th or in the Sth.

(3) A malefic exalted in the 8th while a benefic
is so placed in the 9th.

Asa result, the person will be wealthy and be a
king.

(b) A contrary situation will produce opposite
effects, that is the subject will be poor.

Notes: (a) Some may prefer to interpret that all
these three conditions should be simultaneously
present to form Mani Pravala Yoga. The condition
“Vipareethe Viparyayah” (vide condition at “b”
above) does not allow that interpretationas a contrary
situation is impossible to exist.

(1) The 2nd house or the 3rd house from the
Ascendant should have an exalted planet while a
malefic planet should be in debility anywhere. Thus,
two planets feature in this condition.

(2) Here only one planet features - that is the 4th
or the 5th should have an exalted planet.

(3) Here two exalted planets feature - benefic
exalted in the 9thand malefic exalted in the 8th house
from the Ascendant.

In any of the above cases, the subject will enjoy
a royal status with wealth and paraphernalia.

(b) Contrary: Now, a contrary situation in each
of the above three individual conditions should be
drawn thus:

(i) Contrary condition for“a1” above is: The 2nd
or the 3rd having a debilitated planet while a malefic
is exalted anywhere. This will deprive one of wealth
and status. In other words, in a horoscope where a
malefic planet is exalted, the 2nd or3rd should be free
from occupation by a debilitated planet.

(ii) Contrary for “a2” above is: the 4th or 5th

from the Ascendant should have a debilitated planet
as a result of which one will be poor, without any
mentionable status.

(iii) Contrary for “a3” above is: 8th house having
a debilitated malefic planet while the 9th house has
a debilitated benefic planet. This native will also be
in the grip of poverty and will have no important
position in life.

WH AW TPT MHA: Ur! Ul

128. Tenth From The Moon Sign: The Sun or
Mars inthe 10th from the Moon will make the person
an achiever and valorous, but of sinful disposition;
Mercury produces a scholar. One equal to the king is
denoted by Jupiter; devotion to pleasures will result
Venus occupying 10th from the Moon. Satur refines
one with grief if he happens to be in the 10th from the
Moon.

Notes: The Sun inthe 10th of the Moon will give
wealth and health. The person will help others, and
will enjoy royal status.

Mars in the 10th from the Moon sign will make
one live in foreign places. He will be intent upon
enjoying sensual pleasures, will have a cruel dispo-
sition and will have a mean conduct.

Should Mercury be in the 10th from the Moon,
the person will be rich, close to highly placed people,
famous, artistic and intelligent.

Jupiter in the 10th from the Moon, will give
success in all undertakings. The subject will be
righteous, wealthy, will have a famous history and
will enjoy ministerial positions. Also see effects of
Amala Yoga in the previous slokas.

Fortunes, beauty, success, riches and royal rec-

" ognition will follow Venus placed in the 10th of the

Moon.

Although evil effects like childlessness,
grief,poverty, sickness and emotional upsets are in-
herent of Saturn’s position inthe 10th from the Moon,
he will be an asset for political success in this
position. He should of course be well-placed.

129 - 130. Good Features, Long Life et cetera:
(a) A strong benefic in the Ascendant while maletics
are devoid of strength, will produce a person com-
plete with pleasingly excellent and auspicious fea-
tures (befitting physiognomically favourable de-
scriptions). Further, be will be long-lived, worshipped
by the king and be happy. In this yoga, the Ascendant
should however be a benefic’s sign.

(b) The Moon in the Ascendant aspected by her
dispositor produces one who will be wealthy, whose
intelligence will be as sharp as the point of Kusa
grass, and who will be of a famous lineage.

Notes: (a) If malefics placed anywhere enjoy
strength, they will prove an obstacle for the benefic
in the ascendant in delivering the results suggested.
Comparatively malefics should be stripped of their
vigour. If malefics are stronger than the benefic in the
ascendant, opposite effects will come to pass. If the
ascendant is ruled by a natural benefic, the advan-
tages will be sure.

Ifthe sign ascending is a malefic, the disqualifi-
cation can be offset by more than one benefic therein,
i.e. two or more benefics placed in the malefic sign
ascending; not that those who are born in Leo, Aries,
Capricom etc. will be backward in these respects.

(b) This is acommonly found yoga and needs no
detailed explanation.

131 - 133. (a) A malefic in the ascendant will
make one sickly, weak and troubled by enemies.

(b) A malefic in the ascendant in aspect to the
lord of the 8th house will cause penury and sickness.

(c) If the aspecting planet in the above case is the
4th lord, instead of 8th lord, one will be happy.

(d) If the aspecting planet in the above case is the
6th lord, poverty will result.

(e) Saturn in the Sth or in the 9th house, with a
Navamsa which denotes barrenness (i.e. Leo Nav-
amsa) will make the native marry a barren woman.
Alternatively, he may beget dead children.

(f) The 7th lord ina Navamsa owned bya eunuch
planet while the 4th house is occupied by Rahu, and
the 2nd by Saturn - this yoga will destroy two orthree
children.

Notes: (a) If the occupant of the ascendant is a
major planet, being malefic, like Satur, Rabu, or
Ketu, sickness and inimical troubles will be peren-
nial, and will not end soon. A benefic highly afflicted
will also give similar effects.

(b) This can affect the length of the life as well.
The person will be in perpetual sorrow.

(c) A malefic in the ascendant in aspect to the
lord of the 4th is said to give happiness. Perhaps it is
because the lord of the 4th holds key to one’s general
happiness. That way Venus will also do thesame job
like the 4th lord.

(d) The aspect of the 6th lord will further trouble
one with litigations, debts (different from poverty)
and incurable diseases.

(e) Classical texts describe Leo as barren. Prac-
tical experiences have generally not proved this
point.

(f) The 7th lord from the natal ascendant should
not be in Gemini, Virgo, Capricorn or Aquarius in
Navamsa. The 2nd from the ascendant denotes
family. But the reader may be wondering why the 4th
house is involved in matters related to birth of
progeny. Although general text books like Jataka
Parijata, Saravali, Parasara Hora, and PhalaDeepika
have not referred to the 4th in respect of acquisition
of progeny, Nadi text books give importance to the
occupation of the 4th as well. Of course they have not
## Page 111

Deva Keralam 95

over-rated the 4th in preference to the 5th, nor did
they state that the 4th rules progeny.

For example see sloka 136 infra where the 4th
house is referred to in respect of children.

134 - 135. Concerning Wife: (a) Should one
have a malefic in the 7th house while the 7th lord is
conjunct another malefic, his wife will incur disor-
ders of stomach and worm-infected womb. In the
absence of these, her conceivability will be in doubt.

(b) Ifthe 9th lord is inthe 7th house identical with
a sign owned by Jupiter, while the dispositor Jupiter
is in the 10th house with a malefic, the native will
marry a physically disabled woman.

Notes: (a) This is a simple yoga easy enough to
be understood. This yoga will cause obstacles in
begetting progeny. Else, the person’s spouse may
have abdominal disorders.

(b) The 7th house is ruled by Jupiter in case of
Gemini or Virgo rising. For Gemini, the 9th lord
Saturn in the 7th house while the 7th lord Jupiter is in
Pisces in the company of a malefic will cause mar-
riage with a physically disabled girl. In case of Virgo,
the 9th lord Venus should be in Pisces, in exaltation
while Jupiter is in Gemini with a malefic to cause
marriage with a woman with physical defect.

There is also a rule that Venus in debility in the
7th will give a physically defective spouse.

136. The 4th House: If the 4th house is hemmed:
between malefics, Jupiter in the 5th will cause lim-
ited number of children. Instead of Sth, if Jupiter be
in the 2nd, he will harm the native’s wife. Lastly if he
be in the 7th, while the 4th is hemmed ‘between

malefic,s the subject will have two or three mar-

nages.

Notes: Three yogas are discussed here involving
the 4th house and Jupiter. In each yoga, the common
feature is that the fourth house should be hemmed
between malefics.

Inthe first place, Jupiter in Sth will cause limited
number of children. In the 2nd house, he will ad-
versely affect the wife, normally will curtail her life-
span. In the 7th house, Jupiter will give two or three
marriages. All these, only when the 4th house has
malefics on both the sides. Otherwise, Jupiter alone
in such position should not be expected to give these
adverse results.

143 - 144. Libra Ascendant: One bor in Libra
Ascendant will be the second issue of the family. In
case of second half, birth will be ina small village on
the bank of a “mean” (or small) river and the native
will be the fourth issue. In case of former half, birth
will be in a city.

Notes: So far the text has been dealing with
general rules applicable to various ascendants, with-
out taking Nadiamsa into consideration.

From now on, some Nadiamsa rules are dis-
cussed,

Here, the text does not mention the Nadiamsa,
but Libra Ascendant. Only first half and second half

Chandra Kala Nadi

are mentioned. This inconsistency continues upto
sloka 164, infra.

From a careful reading, it will be evident that
these belong to Vikrutha Nadiamsa, Libra ascendant
as found from sloka 165 on.

145 - 149. Father: (a) The father of the native
of first half would serve in royal circles and be happy
gaining royal honour (or recognition).

(b) The father of the native of second half would
earn his livelihood in foreign place, and would be
disposed to wandering (or frequently moving from
place to place for living). He would be somewhat
distressful. He would have uterine brothers, be sickly
and be attached to his calling (or agriculture). He
would be rich with quadrupeds and grains.

(c) The father of the native of first half would be
rich in conveyances. In childhood he would incur
poverty. He would be the lonely issue of his family,
be lustful and his kinsmen would be famous. He
would leave his birth place and serve a king in the

southern part. He would become famous in royal
circles, be the chief treasurer and be independent.

160 - 164. Paternal Grand-parents: The na-

grace of Sun God obtain sons.

168 - 170. (4) The 3rd lord’s decanate position
(read “Vikramesa” for “Vikramamsa”, or the Nav-
amsa position or its trine as for Mars, or the 12th sign
from the one occupied by Mats will be the natal sign
of one’s brother.

(b) The Bhavas ruling father (i.c. 9th house etc.)
should be multiplied by two, to which the time of
birth in ghatikas be added, "along with the rays for
movable signs etc." and divided by 27. The resultant
figure when counted from Dhanishta/Aswin) will
indicate the birth Nakshatra of the relative con-
cerned, Alternatively a trine thereof willalso be such
Nakshatra. These views are accordding to Manu.

to Ashtaka Varga. Butthe original suffers from errors
as the term “Charadi Rasmi Samyuktha" is not proper.
The rays (or Rasmis) have nothing to do with a sign
being movable, immovable or dual.

173 - 174. Position and Wealth: If the 5th lord
(Saturn) is exalted and obtains a benefic’s Navamsa,
or debilitated but being in the midst of benefics, will

cluding elephants. His father will be wealthy right

a far superior position.

associated with bencfics on either side (even longitu-
dinally, if not sign-wise) will cause the above-men-
tioned effects. This is called Subhakartari yoga and
is generally quite effective.

180 - 181. Jagathi Nadiamsa - Libra Ascend-
ant: (a) The Sun in Leo (in 11th) with Scorpio
Navamsa will give wealth right from birth, but the
subject will be somewhat sickly.

(b) The Sun joining the Navamsa ruled by the 6th
lord wili cause distress to father; in the sub period
ruled by the 6th lord death through water be foretold.

Notes: (a) Placed in Leo 23° 20' through 26° 40’,
the Sun gets Scorpio Navamsa.

(b) For the Sun’s position in Leo, the Navamsa
referred to here is Sagittarius, not Pisces. The stress
for Sagittarius is that it is owned by the 6th lord
Jupiter. The sub period of 6th lord Jupiter is in the
dasa of 8th lord Venus. Apparently the text cites
some possible Balarishta, not necessarily insurmount-
able end as a remedy is suggested below.

Jagathi Nadiamsa may be found in sloka 2128,
Book I.

199. Deha Rasi & Jeeva Rasi: During the
junction periods of two Kalachakra dasas, Deha Rasi
and Jeeva Rasis being reduced to malefic transits will
cause inauspicious effects.

Note: After rectifying the somewhat ill-con-
structed sloka, the above mcaning emerges. The
sloka suggests that no malefic planet, of major cat-
egory (like Saturn and Rahu) should be in transit in
either the Deha Rasi or the Jeeva Rasi to avoid
inauspicious effects during the time one Rasi dasa
ends and another begins as per KCD.

ruled by Jupiter. However ivory specifically comes
under the domain of Satur just as teeth, animal hom
etc.

Those in “b” and “d” need some more conditions in
the original and hence are unclear.

256 - 257. The Lord of the 7th: Should the lord
of the 7th be in the ascendant, the dasa of 7th lord will
cause happiness to the subject apart from mamiage to
his son. The dasa of 8th lord will inflict death on the
subject - in the 48th or 54th year.

Notes; The clues regarding dasa periods for
Libra ascendant, from sloka 248 to 257 can be
arranged in an easy way as under:

1, Saturn in exaltation at birth will enable Cap-
ricom - Saturn dasa give happiness depending on the
whole set of planets.

2. The ascendant Libra, and the 4th - Capricorn
- both occupied by malefic planets, will produce great
danger in the dasa of Capricorn - Saturn. Note the
## Page 123

Deva Keralam

inclusion of the ascendant.

endanger father and other relatives. (This isto he read
with point 2 above.)

4. For Libra ascendant, the dasa of Capricorn -
Saturn will generally harm the persou’s mother.

5. The dasa and sub periods ruled by Cancer,
Scorpio, Taurus and Capricorn will also barm his
mother. That is two of the said four signs should rule
the major and sub periods.

6. The dasa of Capricorn - Saturn wil! give
prosperity and acquisition. The sub period of a
benefic’s sign will beget royal favours.

7. The dasa of Aquanius - Saturn will give many
sons, and acquisition of wealth provided Saturn is in
Libra at birth. Further the person will be inthe service
of the king and be virtuous.

8. The dasa of Aquarius - Saturn will give
happiness (instead of total effects as at 7 above) if
Saturn is in his own sign orown Navarnasa, as against
his being in Libra.

9. The dasa of Pisces - Jupiter will cause increase
of enemies and minimise one’s wealth. His spouse
and children will incur diseases and difficultics.
(This should equally apply to the native.)

10. [f Mars is in the ascendant Libra, the dasa of
Mars (Vimsottari) will cause marriage to bis son.

11. Venus dasa, will inflict death in certain
circumstances. This should be applied when the dasa
is the first one or when Venus is in the grip ofa killer
planet.

The above instructions at S.No.1 to 9 apply to
Kalachakra Dasa analysis, while 10 and 11 areas per
Vimsottani dasa.

A discerning reader can extend these suitably to
the various other ascendants.

260. The Moon in Kinnara Shashtiamsa in Scor-
pio along with Ketu, while Mars joins Rabu (in
Taurus) and begets Leo Navamsa will lead to going
for an adopted son.

Notes: Kinnara Shashtiamsa in Scorpio extends
from 2° 30' to 3° where the Moon is needed to be in.

Kinnara is a mythical being with a human head
in the form of a horse.

Mars in Taurus should be between 23° 20’ to 26°
40' to beget Leo Navamsa.

Thus for Libra ascendant, the Moon and Mars
should be in the above-mentioned spaces while Rabu
and Ketu are in order in Taurus and Scorpio. As a
result, one will have an adopted issue.

up his religion, be devoid of wealth, be a miser, will
eat limited food and will incur enmity with his bride
(i.e.spouse). One born in Libra Navamsa will be fond
of union out of wedlock.

Notes: The clues given about Leo are of doubtful
origin.

The other aphorism relating to Libra Navamsa
should be applied after a careful study of the 7th
house, Venus and other related elements.

269. The Moon in the company of Ketu denotes
that during childhood the subject will be breast-fed
by another woman (than the mother). He will not
havee just one step-mother (i.e. will have many) out
of whom this subject will be dear to one.

Notes: The conjunction of the Moon with Ketu
in this case denotes many marriages to the native's
father. Out of many step-mothers one in partciular
will like the subject.

Further this conjunction will not allow the native
to be fed with his mother's milk during childhood.

270 -271. Planets in Ascendant; The Sun inthe
ascendant will produce a bilious physique and the
subject will be lustful. His complexion will be like
that of Mercury (?); he willservea king and be liberal.
He will be fond of bitter juices and will have a bad
(questionable) history. He will be given to bad
conduct and will be a good minister. If Venus is in
the ascendant, one will be lustful, be endowed with
progeny and be devoid of coborn.

Notes: Bilious physique, liberal disposition and
serving a king are repeated again in sloka 271.

These clues seem to apply toa specificascendant
which is not clear.

However some hints are generally applicable to
the various ascendants in a certain measure. The Sun
in ascendant will cause association with king (or
government), bilious body, bad history etc. Similarly
Venus in the ascendant will give a lustful disposition.

apply to Kinnara Nadiamsa in Leo ascendant.

314 - 315. Parijatha Yoga for Leo Ascendant:
The lord of the ascendant Sun being in association
with Venus and Mercury in aspect to the 9th lord
(Mars) will cause whatis called Parijatha Yoga. One
born thus will enjoy royal recognition, will deliver
auspicious and lovable words, will cause happiness
to all people, will enjoy abundant pleasures, be
endowed with progeny and grand-children, will pos-
sess eyes that are peculiar to women with eyelashes
resembling an arch, and will have a very beautiful
appearance. If this yoga is aspected by a malefic (than
Mars), questionable birth and sinful disposition will
come to pass.

Notes: The Yoga - Parijatha - applies irrespec-
tive of Nadiamsa. The yoga given hereof apparently
forms when the ascendant !ord joins the lords of 2nd
and 10th in aspect to the lord of the 9th.

There is another kind of Parijatha Yoga given by
Jataka Parijatha of Vaidyanatha which could be
found in its chapter VII, sloka 156.

In our text, it is stated that Parijatha Yoga
aspected by a malefic denotes a questionable birth,
and the native will commit sins. The aspect should
be to the Sun and his associates, viz. Mercury and
Venus.

320-323. The natural and temporal strengths of
lords of the various Bhavas and their significators
should be studied before declaring effects. The
dispositor of the lord of a Bhava becomes its perma-

nent (or chief) signficiator. If the said dispositor is
related to a benefic by aspect, he will be auspicious;
and if to a malefic, he will turn inauspicious. The
house in which the lord of a Bhava is placed becomes
its Anitya (or temporary) Karaka. If this temporary
house is related to malefic planets by aspect or
occupancy, the original Bhava suffers annihiliation.

328 - 330. Importance of Dispositor of Bhava:
He, i.e., the dispositor of a Bhava lord alone is the
giver of effects (concerning the original Bhava). If
the Karaka is in own sign, or in Vargottama, or in
exaltation, or be placed amidst benefics, he will cause
more auspicious effects providedd he is no§ in debil-
ity, combustion, and malefic aspects. The lords of
these Bhavas (?) placed between the lords of the 9th
and the 4th or in debility (weak degrees) will cause
the end of the subject prior to that of his parents
provided he is endowed with prosperity. (That is, if
prosperity is absent, death as above will not occur.)

331. The learned declare birth of many male
issues for one having the Jord of the Sth in deep
exaltation in aspect to a benefic and at the same time

Chandra Kala Nadi

occupying an odd Navamsa. It is however essential
that the 5th house should be free from malefic
aspects.

Notes: Discussions on Leo end here for the time
being.

From here upto sloka 335, the rules are general
and not for a particular sign ascending.

In the present aphorism, the lord of the Sth can
be replaced by Jupiter.

Either of the two in deep exaltation, in aspect to
a benefic (Mercury or Venus, or Jupiter in case of 5th
lord’s deep exaltation) will give many sons. The
important condition is the said exalted planet should
be in odd Navamsa. By extension, if the deeply
exalted planet begets even Navamsa, daughters will
be numerous, instead of sons.

Aspect of a malefic on the 5th house (or the 5th
lord or Jupiter) will vitiate the suggested effects.

332. Vamsa Vichcheda Yoga: There will be no
birth ofa male issue causing Vamsa Vichcheda Yoga
(discontinuity of dynasty) if Saturn is found in the 3rd
while the 8th lord is in Vandhyavastha and the Sth
house is in aspect to or in occupation by a malefic.

Notes: Vandhyavastha is not a standard astro-
logical termlike Deepta, Muditaetc. Apparently, the
text stipulates the 8th lord to be in such a position to
deny progeny like being in a barren sign, Leo.

Vamsa Vicheda Yoga specially denies birth of
male progeny.

335. Remedies: To overcome the blemish of
absence of progeny (vide sloka 332), donation of a
goldenimage of Kalpa Druma or the golden image of
a cobra ora splendorous Linga or the image ofa four-
armed Vishnu be done. This will rid one of sins
relating to absence of progeny.

Notes: Kalpa Druma = the Heavenly Tree grant-
ing fulfillment of all desires.

Cobra = Image of Nagaraja, preferably with
seven hoods.

Linga = Image of Siva Linga.

Four-armed Vishnu = Chaturbhuja with Divine
Disc capable of destroying evils wholly (i.e.Sudarsana
Chakra) and Divine Mace.

One of the above four images, made of gold,
according to one’s resources be given away in dona-
tion.

336 - 337. The 5th lord causing Vandhya Yoga
(i.e. 5th lord involved in a yoga denying progeny)
could be remedied by donating the image of Santhana
Gopala (i.e. Lord Krishna). If the yoga of the 5th lord
denotes acquisition of dead progeny donate the
Sisumara (explained elsewhere in relevant notes)
thrice. Gold weighing 6 units (Pala, a traditional
weight), or half of it, or one fourth of it should be
given in donation. Donating a quantity lesser than
this will not achieve the purpose according to sages.

Notes: Vandhyamsa Yoga and Mritha Prajamsa
yoga are improper terms. They denote childlessness
and dead progeny in order. Itis a different matter that
some may interpret these as relevant degrees to which
interpretation I am not able to subscribe.

338 - 3391/2. Immovable Ascendant: There will
be two surviving (i.e. long-lived) sisters for one born
in an immovable ascendant who has the Moon in
Pisces, with Navamsa position in Cancer or Leo or
Aquarius. One of them will be prosperous endowed
with sons and daughters. The subject will aftersome
interval incur destruction of brothers and sons.

Notes: The last line of sloka 3391/2 above does
not convey proper meaning befitting the context. In
one version, this expression is replaced by: “The
sister will prosper through this native and be auspi-
cious.”

This aphorism applies to Taurus, Leo, Scorpio or
Aquarius. The Moon’s position in Pisces is coudi-
tioned by her occupation of Cancer/Leo/Aquarius
Navamsa.

345 - 347. Scorpio Ascendant: Mars in Leo
Navamsa while the Moonis in the ascendant Scorpio
will lead to the following. The subject will live ina
colony of Brahmins, will face difficulties and pov-
erty during childhood and will attain prosperity after
the age of 27 through a brother-in-law. His mother
will be a virtuous and pure lady.

Note: In sloka 347, certain portions are corrupt
and unclear. These relate to: “Bhratraa
sahagamishyathi” - a brother committing
“Sahagamana” which was done only by females.
They committed iiemselves to pyre when their hus-
bands died. Anotheraspect that is not clear is “danger
to father during the rise of the native and the junction
of a dasa”.

These are better ignored in this part of the text,
as there are clear views in sloka 349 infra.

349. Inthe end of the 2nd dasa or in the beginning

369 - 374, Irrelevant: Rahu should be ina sign
that is trine to the Navamsa occupied Saturn. When
Saturn in transit comes to that sign (occupied by
Rahu), there will be drought in the country. There
will be no rains for ten years commencing from birth
that is in the former half of Kutila Nadiamsa. After
33 years of age also, it will be so. After 42 years of
age, there will be scarcity of rains. When Saturn
transits in Revathi, Sravana, Hastha, Arudra, Bharani
and Svathi (Vayu Deva or wind god is the regent of
Svathi and hence this Nakshatra is known after him),
there will be fearof drought in the country. Thus have
been stated effects for the first and second dasas vis
a vis Saturn’s transit. If Rabu attains the same
longitude as that of Satur and is placed in the 3rd or
the 11th, physical decay and great fear will exist in
the world.

placed. Neither they are of meaningful composition.

379. Grief to Sister; When Satum in transit
attains the (natal) degree of 12th lord (Venus) or the
sign occupied by the 4th lord (Saturn), the native’s
sister will be grieved on account of separation from
husband.

Note: The reference to 4th lord and 12th lord
could at best be put as above in the rendering. The
fourth line is not clear. It seems to me that the
longitudes of (Saturn) 4th lord, and Venus (12th Jord)
should be added. On this degree Saturn’s transit will
cause the same effect - grief to sister.

From the above statement we can conceive the
following instructions.

(a) Saturn’s transit on natal Venus’s degree.

(b) Saturn’s transit on his own degree at birth.

(c) Saturn’s transit on the resultant longitude
arrived at by adding those of Venus and Saturn at
birth.

119

In each case the possibility is sister begetting
grief on account of marital tragedy.

383 - 388. Kutila Nadiamsa - Former Half:
This native of Scorpio will lose his children as they
are born apart from (himself) suffering from phleg-
matic disorders. By donating a specified plant, the
native will be happy obtaining a surviving child. In
the absence of this remedy, evils to progeny will
exist. Other remedies suggested are bathing in the
Sethu and worshipping the golden image of Nageswara
and giving charity to astrologer. These will bless one
with long-lived progeny. Phlegmatic disorders could
be avoided by worshipping the image of the zodiac.
By donating the image (of the zodiac), tuberculosis
(a phlegmatic disorder) will be destroyed. Worship
of Nava Grahas and Rudrabhisheka (rituals pre-
scribed for Rudra, a form of Lord Siva), (untimely)
death will be surmountable.

Notes: Here no planetis involved, butthe degree
of birth alone.

Phlegmatic disorder indicated is to the tune of
killing the person untimely. Remedies for obtaining
long-lived progeny and for overcoming death are
suggested in the above verses.

400 - 401. (a) Navamsa of 9th Lord: It will be
a time of prosperity when Jupiter transits the sign
identical with the Navamsa occupied by the 9th lord
atbirth, ora sign trinal thereof, or the sign(s) aspected
by the 9th lord.

(b) So also in respect of Jupiter’s transits in the

following places:

(1) The Navamsa Rasi denoted by the occupa-
tion of the ascendant lord, or a trine thereof.

(2) the Rasi occupied by the lord of the ascend-
ant.

(3) the Rasiaspected by the lord of the ascendant.

Notes: The combinations given are quite simple.
The planets involved are the Moon (9th lord) and
Mars (ascendant lord). Jupiter is one of the best
planets for the ascendant in question.

Since ten particular signs can be generated for
Jupiter’s transit to be favourable, a liberal approach
is not suggested. One should be quite selective,
keeping directional influences and other relevant
transits in mind.

Also see the following verses, for specific ef-
fects.

408 - 4111/2. Scorpio Ascendant - Kutila
Nadiamsa: Due to blemishes caused by adverse
placements of planets in the zodiac, the native of
Kutila Nadiamsa, Scorpio ascendant will during
Saturn’s movement in Libra, incur evils to his kins-
folk. During Saturn’s journey in Scorpio, his pros-
perity will be checkered and he will be indistress. At
forty-eight he will face (timely) death. However after
forty, he will be in the grip of fear of untimely death
after which time he will survive due to favourable
planetary combinations contributing to life-span
(Yogayu). At the age of forty-eight, evil planets will
overtake him. There will be danger to him ona high
road during his fortieth year. If he survives this
danger, he will be famous, happy and prosperous in
his birth country.

Notes: Froma study of relevant verses of Kutila
Nadiamsa, Scorpio ascendant, we can gather that the
subject will be endangered in his forties. The life will
not be quite long.

412. For Scorpio ascendant, Kutila Nadiamsa,
Saturn placed in Libra at birth will grant long lives to
the person’s progeny.

Notes: As is being seen by us on various occa-
sions inthis work, the 12th denotes death of children.
Saturn, signifying longevity, in the 12th will confer
long-lives to children of the native.

Thus, an adverse or weak planet in the 12th will
cut short progeny’s longevity.

414. Venus in Scorpio: Should Venus be in the
divisions of Aries, while placed in Scorpio, the
subject of Scorpio ascendant will take to ascetismdue
to a family calamity. He will further win his five
senses.

Note: “Meshamsa” is not translated as Aries
Navamsa because Venus in Scorpio cannot get such
Navamsa. Thenitdenotes the other possible division
of Aries.

Winning the senses is essential fora true Sanyasi
with fully severed mundane bonds, Venus is the lord
of the 7th, ruling one’s senses. His occupation of
Aries Vargas or divisions, placed in the ascendant
Scorpio, should allow one’s senses to move toward
self-realisation.

In otherwise an afflicted horoscope, this position
of Venus will only misdirect the subject to enjoying
material pleasures of various kinds, instead of grant-
ing him true ascetism.

418 - 420. Rectified Ashtaka Varga: (a) When
Saturn transits the signs that have 1, 2 or3 Bindus in
- the Ashtaka Varga of the ascendant, intense difficul-
ties will come to pass.

(b) Abundant wealth will be acquired if the sign
containing five Bindus in Ascendant’s Ashtaka Varga
is transited by benefic planets.

(c) During the currency of favourable dasa peri-
ods, if the signs containing five or more bindus are
transited by malefic planets, great prosperity will
occurapart from acquisition of wealth of quadrupeds.

Notes: The authordeals withuse of Lagnashtaka
Varga (rectified with Ekadhipathya and trinal cortec-
tions).

(a) This rule is clear and applies to the various
rectified Ashtaka vargas, the net essence of which is
adversity.

123

(b) Benefic planets in transit on their own accord
canimprove good effects even if the dasa periods are
somewhat adverse.

(c) As for malefics, to give the good effects cited,
the additional requirement is operation of favourable
dasa periods.

The reader will note the difference between
malefic and benefic transits.

423 - 426. Dasa Periods: (a) If however, the dasa
lord be seen with mediocre strength the undertakings
commenced by the person will incur slow effects;
obstacles of strong nature, and (even) destruction.

(b) Ifthe dasa lord be located with Jeast strength,
one’s wealth will be destroyed; he will face loss of
position, calumny from others, loss of quadrupeds
etc., diseases to spouse, progeny and the like and
abundant grief. Further his parents and other kinsfolk
will fall prey to diseases and he himself will be
subjected to great distress.

(c) Should the dasa lord be deprived cf strength
in toto, one’s physical felicity will be completely
void.

(d) The lord of the dasa provided with full
strength, or being with a benefic planet, will increase
the auspicious effects.

Notes: “Kshema Gathi” denoting a certain mo-
tion of the dasa lord (vide sloka 423) is not a clear
term and ultimately unhelpful.

Navamsa, there will be fear and distress on account
of enemies. The sub period concerned will be of that
planet which is inimical to the lord of the dasa, or of
a planet that is in its own sign.

432. Jupiter in Pisces: One having Jupiter in
Pisces will be liked by his king, be righteous, ac-
quainted with higher knowledge, passionate, peace-
ful and virtuous.

Notes: As per Kalyana Varma, Jupiter in Pisces
will give expertise in ancient Sastras. The subject
will be honoured by friends and virtuous men. He will
enjoy a leading position under the king’s employ,
will be wealthy, will not incur defeat, and be skillful
in policy matters. His undertakings will prosper.

433. Jupiter in the 10th House: (a) Ifthe planet
Jupiter is found in he 10th house, one will be a
minister.

(b) Jupiter in the 10th with a friend’s Navamsa
## Page 141

Deva Keralam 125

will make one dear to king.

(c) If the Navamsa in question is ruled by Mer-
cury or Venus, Jupiter in the 10th will involve the
subject in trouble and will make him perform such
acts which will arouse the wrath of the ruler.

Notes: (a) This position of Jupiter in the 10th
refers to-no specific Navamsa. The text tersely
indicates a superior professional position for the
subject.

Jupiter in the 10th will further give wealth,
welfare and happiness in general, conveyances, fa-
vourable kinsfolk and fame. Whatever be the under-
taking, the subject will complete it successfully. He
will be disposed to much eating. His sexual
enjoyments will be limited. He will be short-tem-
pered and his contributions to the society will last
long. He will obtain patronage of influential] men.
Richness is a part of this position of Jupiter. The
subject will be learned in many Sastras including The
Bhagavad Gita.

There are authorities to state that Jupiter in the
10th carries some inberent blemish to cause worries
about progeny.

Also see sloka 436 infra.

(b) If Jupiter in the 10th occupies a Navamsa
owned by the Sun, the Moon or Mars, the person will
be close to high-ups in power.

(c) In this context, Jupiter begetting Gemini,
Virgo, Libra or Taurus Navamsa, will cause profes-
sional difficulties from powerful people.

Also see the following slokas.

436. Jupiter in the 10th House: The person
having Jupiter in the 10th house will be blessed with
much wealth, the nine kinds of precious stones, and
large golden chains (or ornamenis); he will be an
expert teacher in sports, pastime, dance, songs, arts,
business activities ofall kinds and spiritual Initiation.
He will be firm in disposition, be honoured by a
superior king, and be himself an ocean of virtues and
good deeds. However he will incur enmity with his
kinsfolk.

440 - 441. Early Death of Father: The Moon
should join Saturn and Mars and be in the Naksbatra
represented by the remainder in the process of mul-
tiplying the rectified Bindus in the 9th place in Sun’s
Ashtaka varga by the Sun’s Sodhya Pinda and divid-
ing by 27. Furtheras a resultof this yoga, the person’s
mother will be distressed. He will have no after-born.
His prosperity will be of a great order in the dasa of
the Sun, ina foreign land.

Notes: “Suryashtakavarga Samsodhya
Nakshatra” on its own has no specific meaning, as
given above. But such an interpretation is a part of
chapters related to use of Sodhya Pindas, Nakshatras
etc. in the Ashtaka Varga method. There may be
scholars who can give better interpretation to the
above condition.

448 - 449. From Mars (to Saturn), good results in
their periods will be dependent on the number of

they give good results, with two or three bindus
adverse effects, with moderate bindus (i.e. 4 and
above) moderate effects. If the sign Leo gets no
Bindus, the sub period of the Sun will be futile. So
also the sub period of the Moon if Cancer is devoid
of Bindus.

461 - 463. Saturn in Svathi; When Saturn
transits Svathi, there will be destruction of enemies,
and incurring fear. One will befriend enemies from
the time the Sun moves in Capricorn through Pisces
(coinciding with Saturn’s stay in Svathi). Should the
Sun, then, be found in transit in the signs commenc-
ing from Aries, one’s enemics will be destroyed.
However with the Sun in Gemini, there will be some
distress and later on health will prevail. With the
Sun’s change of course in Pisces, one will attain
success in undertakings while happiness will prevail
with the change of Sun’s course in Cancer. In
between there will be distress.

Notes: Sloka 463 has an incompatible term
“Meenayana”, The Sun does not change his course
in Pisces. Hence this is a wrong term. His transit in
Meena or Pisces is part of his northerly course or
Uttarayana. ;

For ready information of the reader, the Sun
changes his course twice ina year. When he enters
Sayana (tropical) Capricom, he commences his north-
erly course, i.e. Uttarayana. When he enters Sayana
Cancer, he commences his southerly course,
Dakshinayana.

For Hindus' religious purposes, these courses are
detected on Nirayana (sidereal) basis.

465 - 470. Saturn’s Transit: When Saturn moves
in the third Nakshatra from the birth Nakshatra, the
person will seize his enemics but he will also have
fear of a great order; if it is the second Nakshatra, he
willbe in the grip of fear. In the fourth Nakshatra, the
transit of Saturn will cause distress and quarrels in
native country, trouble to populace (?), mental wor-
ries and enmity with the king of Pandya country. This
transit will also cause the native’s destruction. The
2nd and 4th Naksbairas being in transit by Saturn will
cause death of the king (?), and trouble to relatives.
When malefics transit natal ascendant, 10th house
and Adhana ascendant, the subject will incur
misunderstanding with royal circles, or physical
illness to self, and troubles to his kinsfolk. If these are
in transit by benctic planets, auspicious results will
come to pass, and if by malefics, mental distress will
be incurred. The wise should deduce the effects
according to caste, community etc.

Notes: Also see slokas 482 - 485 infra.

Inall the cases of transits on a given Nakshatra,
the 10th and 19th thereof will also pass similar
effects. Final effects will depend on the age of the
native concerned.

474 - 475. Only good effects and advent of
wealth should be predicted for the transit of a benefic
in the Nakshatras that are favourable to Janma
Nakshatra. Specially wealth will accrue in the fol-
lowing months: (a) When the Sun transits the sign
occupied by the lord of the 11th. (b) When the Sun
arrives in the Rasiidentical withascendant’s decanate.
(c) “Subha drishti yuthe maase” means the month
that has benefic’s aspect. (The concept behind this
condition is not clear.)

476 - 478. The Janma Nakshatra coinciding with
a week day ruled by a benefic planet will cause
various kinds of wealth and happiness. Physical
distress, royal wrath, and infirm disposition will
follow birth ona week day ruled by a malefic planet.
Sunday birth denotes (aimless) wandering, royal
wrathand (futile) arguments. Happiness, acquisition
of wonderful flowers, affectionate cohabitation, and
good food will result birth on Monday. Grief, self-
destruction, quarrels, physical ailments and endless
wanderings are the effects for birth on Tuesday. One
born on a Wednesday will be happy and derive
pleasures through honey, ghee, learning, and listen-
ing to mythological stories. Jupiter’s day being birth
day will bless one with robes, fruits, honey, wealth (or
articles) and attending to temple festivals. Friday-
born will obtain ornaments, enjoyments from fe-
males, various kinds of clothes and lovely scents.
Grief, difficulties, fear, diseases and servitude will be
the effects for birth on Saturday.

Notes: Reference to Janma Nakshatra on a par-
ticular week day is made in the first line of sloka 476.
Whereas without a reference to Janma nakshatra,
these results could have directly been attributed to
week days. For there is no specific Nakshatra in-
volved with a given day.

482 - 485. (a) Effects of Saturn in Transit in

Various Nakshatras: Saturn transiting the Janma

Nakshatra will produce royal wrath, grief and infirm
finances. If the transit be in the 2nd Nakshatra,

Chandra Kala Nadi

wealth, comforts, ornaments and robes will be ga-
lore. There will be destruction of quadrupeds, lands,
and wealth, grief, diseases, separation from relatives,
quarrels with servants and a temperament to lose
temper instantly, when it is the third Nakshatra. One
will be happy and rich, will enjoy food comforts and
will receive a messenger (with good news) if the 4th
Nakshatra is transited by Saturn. The 5th Nakshatra
in this respect creates royal anger, financial pressure,
obstacles to work and grief. Attainments, acquisition
of progeny, financial success, lands, wealth, gar-
lands, and robes will be produced by Saturn in transit
in the 6th Nakshatra. Much grief, difficulties, and
diseases caused by the co-operative vitiation of the
three humours of the body will be the result of Saturn
transiting the 7th one from Janma Nakshatra. His
transit in the 8th Nakshatra will cause union with
friends, honours from royal circles, ornaments, con-
veyances, devotion to one’s calling and bed com-
forts. If the 9th Nakshatra from Janma Nakshatra is
transited by Saturn, the subject will befriend the king,
will move with virtuous men, be engaged in learning,
will carry out royal orders, will have visits by his
progeny and relatives and be endowed with wellbe-
ing.

(b) Saturn’s Transit in 12th House: If Saturn be
in transit in the 12th house which happens to be his
close friend’s place, the subject will be engaged in
thoughts ofa low caste woman ("Vrishali" apart from
meaning “low caste woman” also means an unmar-
ried girl of 12 years of age whose menstruation has
just commenced, or a woman who is the mother of a
still-born child). He will think also of his progeny
(i.e. will be worried about them), will incur fever, will
wander aimlessly, will incur phlegmatic disorders,
will hate food and will obtain comforts galore.

486. Saturn transiting in the 10th house (read
“Karmarkshe” instead of “Janmarkshe”) will grant
curd, sauce or vessels (i.e. eating comforts), quadru-
peds, agriculture (or professional gains), courage and
ornaments. In Adhana ascendant, it will bring royal
wrath apart from causing mental infirmity and de-
struction of conveyances, wealth and food. Inthe 8th,
there will be fear from enemies and troubles relating
to progeny, friends, spouse and king. In the 7th there
will be troubles from king, enemies and odd or
unsuitable placements, apart from troubles from
servants. When such forecasts are made by the
astrologer in the presence of a king, the king will be
surprised, and all that is told by such astrologer will
never go against truth.

488 - 493. Dispositors & Dasa Effects: During
the sub period of an adverse planet, in the dasa of
Rahu’s dispositor, the subject willincurdiseases, and
fear from king and enemies. According to other
authorities one will lose household articles in a theft
and will incur destruction and difficulties. Further he
will be in debt and troubled by ulcers. In the sub
periods (of adverse planets) in the dasa of Saturn’s
dispositor, he will be troubled by debts, theft and
ulcer. The dasa of the dispositor of a benefic will give
auspicious effects. Similarly the dasa of the disposi-
tor of a malefic planet will give inauspicious effects.
The sub period of the dispositor of the 12th lord will,
in the dasa of the dispositor of the 8th lord, cause fear
of untimely death, and also grief on account of loss
of one’s kinsfolk. Among the dasas of the Rasi/
Navamsa dispositors of Saturn, Mandi and 8th lord,
the weakest will cause death. Saturn in transit in the
8th....(text incomplete).

Notes: The word “dasa” is understood in the
original sloka 488 with reference to Rahu’s dispositor
as could be seen in sloka 490 infra.

494. 496, The wise should deduce the following
fromthe 12 houses of a horoscope and declare effects
accordingly.

The ascendant - Fame, physique, figure and
disposition.

2nd house - Gold (i.e.wealth), eyes, family, face
and food.

3rd house - Ability in war, prowess, cheek and
ears.

4th house - chest, comforts, residence, convey-
ances and pleasures. (“Mukha” should be read as
“Sukha” to mean comforts. “Mukha” means mouth
which is ruled by the 2nd house and not by the 4th
house.)

Sth house: Stomachial region, mind, sons, hand
(?) and disciples.

6th house: Step-mother, enemies, ulcers, dis-
ease, poison, navel.

7th house: Wife, the lower belly or pelvis, urine,
sexual desire, amorous passion, sexual enjoyment.

8th house: Hole (Randhra itself means the 8th
house), calumny, death, lack of cleanliness, secretive
diseases.

9th house: Fortunes, righteousness, gods, auspi-
cious acts, prosperity, preceptors, and penance.

10th house: Honour, foreign residence, Yagnas
(Vedic rituals), profession, fame, se}f-conceit, au-
thority and success.

1] thhouse: Attainment without obstacles, wealth
(or exalted position) and well-being.

12th house: Obstacles, loss of wealth, destruc-
tion and bed-comforts.

Notes: As for the8th house, which is called
Randhrasthaana, hole means the cavity through which
the life force leaves the body at the time of death.
There are nine holes in the body. Some recognise 10,
including the cavity at skull. That is why the 8th is
related to end of life, The ancients believed thatwhen
the life force left the body through the hole of the skull
- called Brahma Randhra - one attained Sathya Loka,
the world of Brahma and got rid of further births.
Should the life force leave the body through the hole
of rectal or urinary passage, the dead would go to hell
and would have rebirths.

Chandra Kala Nadi

497. The good effects of a Bhava depend on the
strength of the lord of that bhava; a weak planet will
give converse results. In analysing the effects of a
Bhava, the yogas (association, aspects etc.) involved
thereof should be given due consideration.

522. Yamala Yoga: Saturn being in the 7th and
getting the company of an exalted planet produces a
yoga called Yamala Yoga.

Notes: The effects of this yoga are not directly
giveninthe sloka. Yamala means twins. Apparently
the christening of the yoga itself implies that the
subject with this yoga will beget twins.

Since this yoga is discussed in the context of an
immovable ascendant, it applics only to Scorpio
ascendant from where the 7th, Taurus, can have an
exalted planet - the Moon. The other three immov-
able signs do not exalt any planet.

§30 - 531. General: The Sun in transit in 6th, 3rd
and 10th, the Moon in 10th, 11th, 1st and 7th,

532 . 536. Saturn’s Transit Effects: (a) Danger,
damage, wealth, abdominal disease, great fear, de-
struction of enemies, great courage, death, physical
decay, suffering, gains and losses are the effects of
Saturn moving in 12 places in order.

(b) Saturn in the 1st (i.e. on the Moon sign) will
cause dispute and argument.

In the 2nd - loss of money and troubles from
enemies.

In the 3rd - eating comforts, happiness to prog-
eny and kinsfolk, success in war, many kinds of
happiness and fulfilment of desires.

In the 4th - destruction of friends, progeny,
wealth, quadrupeds, lands, undertakings and honour.

In the 5th - mental aberration, various kinds of
worries, and faults.

In the 6th - advent of wealth aplenty and happi-
ness.

In the 7th - destruction of wife, progeny and
servants.

In the 8th - destruction in general, trouble from
enemies, loss of weight on account of grief.

In the 9th - attachment to sinful acts, and sudden
destruction of auspiciousness and prosperity, pitiable
state or miserliness, and troubles onaccount of sexual
unions,

Chandra Kala Nadi

In the 10th - loss of fame (or honour), fear of
strife and blemish.

In the 11th - acquisition of wealth and installa-
tion as a king (i.e. getting superior position).

In the 12th - destruction of figure and limbs,
experiencing abundant grief, irritation, humiliation
inthe hands of servants, victimisation through severe
diseases.

Seeing the transits of Saturn, one can off-handedly
declare effects.

father will be destroyed. (In the process) with the
attainment ofthe Sun’s decanate, Navamsa or Dwada-
samsa by Saturn, coupled with an adverse solar
transit (i.e. the month), destruction of father will
occur.

546 - 553. Jupiter in Pisces with Libra Nav-
amsa: One born in Lakshmi Shashtiamsa and with
Jupiter in Pisces having Libra Navamsa will beget the
following effects. The person will be broad-faced, be
employed, will have affectionate spouse,be happy,
dark in complexion, of praiseworthy qualities, skillful,
and will have abdominal disorders. His paternal
uncle’s family will prosper. The subject will be fond
of his paternal uncle’s son. He will live in a town
surrounded by forests and will have a windy body.
Annual rituals to dead souls will interest him. He will
be a miser, be patient, be fond of and skillful injustice
and meritorious deeds, be learned, tond of fun, will
construct temples and gardens, will honour gods and
Brahmins, will please his relatives, will worship Lord
Vishnu and Lord Siva, will eat limited food, be
secretive, passionate, timid, profoundly intelligent,
will beget much prosperity in the middle age and will
suffer trouble and poverty in childhood. His after-
born will be destroyed. He will be fond of his
maternal relatives. His maternal grand-mother will
be long-lived. He will be liked by his matcmal uncle.
He will be the eldest issue, be sickly, be happy after
marriage, will have self-earned wealth, and will have
a position in royal palace.

Notes: There is no Lakshmi Shashtiamsa as
such. Apparently there is some compositional error.

559. Immovable Ascendant: The 7th lord inthe
Shashtiamsa entitled Lakshmi will, for a native of
Mudgara Nadiamsa, give marriage in the birth coun-
try. His bride will prove ominous for her father (i.e.
she will have lost her father before marrying the
subject).

Note: A careful study will reveal that from sloka
559 to 664, the Nadiamsa dealt with is Mudgara and
the ascendant is Leo. Of course there is no clear
mention that the ascendant discussed is Leo. Simply
the preceding slokas discuss an immovable ascend-
ant. Unless one applies his heart and soul, required
clues will not emerge from certain areas in the text.
That Leo is discussed can be somewhat understood
from the following sloka, No.560.

Chandra Kala Nadi

However in between this space, slokas belong-
ing to other ascendants also interrupt. These are
clearly separated by me by necessary paragraph
captions.

560. The number of Bindus in Venus’ Ashtaka
Varga or in that of the 7th lord from the Moon (will
denote the number of coborn the native will have).
Should the 7th lord (from the ascendant) be exalted,
only two or three (coborn) will be long-lived.

Notes: To geta proper meaning of this sloka, we
have to supply certain information ourselves. In-
volvement of 3rd lord Venus, 7th lord Saturn exalted
in the 3rd, and reference to long life - all these point
out to two things:

1. The ascendant discussed is Leo.

2. The issue in this verse is coborn.

580 - 5801/2. When Saturn comes to Libra in
transit, there will be all-round drought. In the end of

581 - 5871/2. The lord of the ascendant in the 6th
while the 6th Jord is in Ripu Rasi (i.e. in the 6th) in
the company of the 8th lord will cause disorders ofthe
spleen. Venus in the 7th house in aspect to or in
conjunction with Satam will lead to blood disorders
and windy diseases. To overcome this blemish,
observation of religious vows on Sundays should be
resorted to. The names of the twelve Suns should be
recited on Sundays. Donation of red coloured clothes
Should be done. As a result health will prevail.
Golden image of the Sun God should be got made
according to one’s capacity. This should be wor-

the Sun God, health will be recovered. Fora year one

fruits only.

588 - 594. Leo Ascendant - Mudgara Nadiamsa:
Jupiter dasa, Sun bhukti will cause some fear in royal
circles and later on relief from ill-health. In the sub
period of the Moon, there will be a mix of good and
bad effects apart from indigestion and dysentery. In
his relative’s circle also, mental distress, grief and ill-
health will prevail. The same effects will prevail in
the sub period of Venus. One will beget ownership
of relatives’ wealth inthe sub period ruled by the Sun,
apart from distress in king’s family (?) and destruc-
tion of friends. ‘In the sub period of Mars troubles to
son, and marriage to daughter will come to pass.
Rahu’s sub period will endanger the person’s spouse
and will cause a death in father’s circle. In the sub
period of the Moon, maternal uncle will be endan-
gered, coinciding with adverse solar movements.
Further this sub period will cause cold fever to the
native, and agitation to mother. Due to birth in
Mudgara Nadiamsa and Jupiter in the 10th prevailing
together (“Jivamsa Nadiyogena"), the subject will
enjoy happiness (i.e. ultimate freedom from all these
dangers). He will obtain a son; there will be a
marriage in his family. Later on mental agitation will
occurand he will derive a mix of good and bad effects
in royal circles.

602. Disease: When Saturn comes to the sign
denoted by the Navamsa occupied by Ketu, diseases
will strike the person including impure excretion,
physical pain etc. Health will however be recovered
early.

Notes: This is one of the most important clues to
detect period of disease. Note the Navamsa position
of Ketu. With Saturn in transit in the sign identical
with the said Navamsa, one will suffer from diseases.
If the dasa of a disease-causing planet be in simulta-
## Page 158

142 Chandra Kala Nadi

neous operation, the person will have perpetual ill-
health condition.

“Recovering early” mentioned in the text may
have to be applied after a complete study of all the
planets.

603 - 6051/2, Dasa of 9th Lord: For the native of
Mudgara Nadiamsa, Leo ascendant, the first sub
period of the 9th lord’s dasa (i.e. Mars dasa, Mars sub
period) will cause much distress. In the 19th year
trouble from royal sources be foretold. After 24,
prosperity will dawn apart from a marriage in the
family. In the sub period of the lord of the ascendant
(i.e. in Sun’s sub period) during the dasa of the 9th
lord, a son will be born to him through his second
wife; there will also be advent of wealth through
royal sources. Ketu’s sub period will cause distress.
Abundantly auspicious results will follow the sub
period of Venus. The sub period of the Sun will
involve him in royal assignments, but will harm his
spouse and progeny.

abdomen and mental aberration which can be cured
by worshipping the Sun God, repeat Sun God.

627 - 6361/2. The abdominal sickness caused by
Saturn-Sun conjunction in the Sth can be warded off
by donating gingilee cakes ("Tilapishtarkadanena"
should read as “Tilapsihta pradanena"). An idol
made of gingilee cakes, with three eyes and two
diamond-studded hands, with red robes and sur-
rounded by horses be obtained. Homa (fire sacrifice)
as prescribed be done and charities given, which will
serve as the most excellent remedy according to
Rudra Yamala. The (worship of the) image of the Sun
God made of gingilee cakes will increase life span.
“Grant me health, prosperity and progeny.” (This is
the meaning of the mantra given inthe text.) The Sun
god should be placed in the middle of the image of the
zodiac. At the end of the Pooja, charity be given
away. This will increase health, prosperity and will
stall untimely death. To donate the image of the
zodiac to the astrology is among the most meritorious

Chandra Kala Nadi

deeds. Due to the mercy of the Nava grahas, he will
be endowed with longevity and health. His desires
will be fulfilled. The pot decorated as per Vedic
injunctions should be placed in the midst of Nava
Dhanyas (nine kinds of grains) along with the image
of the zodiac and be worshipped. At the end of the
Homa, charities be givenaway whereupon longevity,
health and fulfillment of desires will come to pass,
according to (Rudra) Yamala.

Notes: These slokas are also a mix up and are in
the wrong part of the text. The reader may take only
useful clues hereof and ignore the rest.

Apparently the remedy suggested for Sun-Sat-
urn conjunction in the Sth is donation of gingilee
cakes and worship of Sun God. Asa result, abdomi-
nal diseases will not trouble the native.

684 - 686. Sun - Venus aspecting Rahu: Rahu
placed in Ico ascendant with Virgo Navamsa will

concerned will be (often) in difficulties. He will be
capable of managing difficult lasks, be enthusiastic,

truthful, will incur difficulties in the middie of his
life, be happy in childhood, modest, righteous, will
use tricky expedients, will have a thin body, be
wealthy and devoted to Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva.
All these results will come to pass only if the planet
Rahu as above 1s aspected by the Sun and Venus
jointly.

Nadiamsa: One born in the former half of this
Nadiamsa will have three long-living maternal un-

be in (perpetual) grief. Another sister will have long

So also yet another sister.

702 - 7041/2. Leo Ascendant - Sivakari
Nadiamsa: (a) The subject of first half of this
Nadiamsa (as against Mohana Nadiamsa, above) will
have one long-lived maternal uncle. Although he
willhave eight maternal uncles, only two or three will
be long-lived.

(b) Take the Moon’s Ashtaka Varga and note the
net bindus got by the sign occupied by the Moon
which will denote the number of brothers the sub-
ject’s mother will have.

(c) Similarly the number of brothers, father will
have to be deduced from the net bindus in the sign
occupied by the Sun, with reference to the Sun’s
Ashtaka varga.

Notes: The instructions given at “b” and “c” can
be used for other ascendants as well. The Ashtaka
Varga referred to is the finally rectified one.

Sivakari Nadiamsa is explained in notes under
sloka 3241 supra.

705 - 7061/2. Leo Ascendant - Mercury: (a) The
11th lord Mercury being in Leo, which ascends at
birth, should be in Scorpio Navamsa. Further, the
ascendant lord should be in the company of a malefic.
As a result of these, two of the native’s paternal
uncles will have two wives each.

(b) Mercury in Sivada Nadiamsa (in the ascend-
ant Leo) denotes that the father will be a wise person
(or will have spiritual knowledge), will destroy his
elder brothers (i.e. will lose them prematurely), and
will have three long-living younger brothers.

Notes: (a) Mercury should be in Leo 23° 20' - 26°
40' so that he obtains Scorpio Navamsa.

The 11th and its lord denote one’s paternal
relatives.

Sivada Nadiamsa - see notes under sloka 3211
supra.

(b) Father’s wisdom, intelligence, memory etc.
are to be analysed from the native's natal ascendant,
which is the Sth (the bhava concerned) from the 9th
(father). Thus Mercury in the specified Nadiamsa in
the 5th from the 9th will not allow any older coborn
of father to survive.

711-7141/2. Effects stated about paternal uncles
will bear truth. So also about maternal uncles. The
Moon in the ascendant (Leo) while Mars is in the 4th
house will cause evil effects for maternal relatives,
will trouble maternal uncles and maternal grand-
father. In the absence of these, evils to maternal
uncles (if not to other maternal relatives) will come
to pass. To overcome these evils, suitable remedies
be resorted to. As prescribed by Sastras, Homa (fire
sacrifice) for Mars and Rahu should be performed.
Donation of Nagapasa (a sort of magical noose)
should also be done. After these, auspiciousness in
maternal relatives’ familics will prevail.

Notes: “Janma Pake Nisa Nathe” in sloka 711
means Moon in Janma Dasa which does not convey
a proper meaning. Itshould be Moon inJanma Lagna,
ic. natal ascendant, i.e. Leo. The translation is
accordingly rectified.

In the yoga for evils to maternal relatives, the
Moon in the ascendant and Mars in the 4th only
feature. But in remedy, Rabu is included and Moon
excluded. Rahu is Sarpa (or snake); hence donation
of Nagapasa is prescribed.

Donation of Nagapasa is notclearly understand-

15]

able. Nagapasa is a divine noose used in the remote
past in large-scale battles which would bind the
inflicted by venomand deprive him of consciousness.
This weaponis attributed to Varuna by ourscriptures.
For example, Naga Pasa (or Nagaasthra) was used on
Lakshmana in Ramayana era whereupon Lord
Hanuman had to bring the Sanjivani plant.

After performing the prescribed Fire Sacrifice
(or Homa) for Mars and Rabu, one may donate an
image of Cobra, preferably golden, ifnota Nagapasa
precisely.

715 - 7161/2, Ifthe Moon is in Mohana Nadiamsa
(being in Leo, as Mars is in the 4th, as above), there
will be no such blemishes in paternal relatives’
families. However, maternal families will to some
extent suffer apart from father incurring distress in
the native’s first dasa, in the months denoted by
adverse solar transits, or in the sub period of the Sun,
the lord of the ascendant. The native’s mother will
(also) undergo great distress.

Notes; From these relevant discussions, we can
foresee troubles for mother if the Moon is in the
ascendant while the 4th lord is in the 4th house itself,
ona general basis. Ifthe Moonis not inthe ascendant,
the 4th lord in the 4th should not be treated as evil.
The Moon is significator for mother.

Mohana Nadiamsa - refer to sloka 445, Book I.

721 - 724, Sivada Nadiamsa - Father: The
native’s father will be devoted to Lord Siva when the
Sun’s dispositor is in exaltation as the 10th lord is in
aspect to Venus. In addition, the person’s father will
perform activities related to Lord Siva’s worship, be
righteous, endowed with brothers and sisters, be
learned in the philosophy related to Lord Siva, and
will honour gods and Brahmins. The native’s second
dasa will endanger his father, in the 16th year when
transit Saturn is in Scorpio. During the person’s
twelfth year of age, father will be in the grip of
untimely death which will be remediable by propitia-
tions. 12th, 16th or 19th year will prove fatal for
father in case of the subject belonging to first half of
Sivada Nadiamsa.

Notes: These events do not relate to Leo ascend-

Chandra Kala Nadi

ant as the 10th lord is required to be associated with
Venus. The other three immovable ascendants, viz.
Taurus, Scorpio and Aquarius will come under the
purview of this principle and the results will be as
described above.

ora trine thereof, when in transit by Saturn will cause

very time, maternal relatives will (also) be in danger.
Astrologers declare distress of a great order to mother,
with this transit.

732 -735.(a) The sub periods of lords of 8th/1 1th
in the dasa of the 6th lord will destroy the person’s
elder brother.

(b) During the operation of the Sth lord’s dasa,
Saturn in transit in the sign identical with the Nav-
amsa occupied by the Sth lord at birth or a trine,
thereof will cause diseases to elder brother.

(c) In this dasa of Sth lord, the sub periods of
Saturn, Mercury and Mars will cause sickness to
elder brother or paternal uncle. (d) The sub period of
Venus in any dasa will cause distress to father who
will also have fear of royal wrath in the sub periods
ruled by Saturn in general.

Notes: (a) The sub period of Jupiter or of Mer-
cury in the major period of Saturn will harm older
brothers of a Leo native. Jupiter is the natural
significator for older co-born while Mercury is the
11th lord, having a sway over older co-born.

(b) Sth lord’s dasa is Jupiter’s dasa.

(c) The sub periods of Saturn, Mercury and Mars
in the major period of Jupiter are said to be adverse
forelder brother or paternal uncle. Mercury involved
is understandable. But Saturn and Mars playinga role
needs a special note.

(d) The sub period Venus and of Saturn in any
dasa is said to be generally adverse in certain re-
spects, because they are evil lords for this ascendant.

736. General: When the dasa and (or) sub

period ruled by Saturn be in operation, the transit of
Saturn ina sign will destroy the good effects of that
Bhava with reference to which the transited sign is the
8th one. So say the learned in astrology.

Notes: Take the case of Leo ascendant for
example, having Satur in transit in Taurus at a time
when Saturn dasa, or Saturn’s sub period in another
dasa is in operation. Taurus is the 8th from Libra.
Libra denotes brothers, sisters, journeys, writing
activities, arms, legs, lungs etc. for Leo ascendant.
Thus the transit of Saturn as above will play
havoc in these spheres.

737 - 740. Sivada Nadiamsa - Leo ascendant:
Saturn in the 3rd in exaltation, in full strength, and
being with the Moon will give three brothers and one
sister, all with long life spans. After some time, the
person’s landed properties will be destroyed. So also
his children being born. To overcome the blemish of
progeny, donation of (the image made out of) a
specified plant (named Sisumara, cited in Varaha
Mihira’s Brihat Samhita, wherein it is referred to as
Sisumari) should be given away. This remedy will
increase the life span of progeny. Because of Saturn
and Moon as above, the subject following his mar-
riage will incur destruction of wealth in his in-laws’
family.

751 - 760. Sivada Nadiamsa - Leo Ascendant:
The Sun in the 3rd house in debility will cause
following effects. When Saturn comes to that degree
(occupied by the Sun), there will be drought(?)
Further, the person’s income will be obstructed to
enmity in royal circles. (Without referring to Saturn),
this native will be happy after 30 years of age, in
Mercury’s sub period (of 2nd dasa). He will be
famous, but will incur some enmity with coborn.
Blemishes will be destroyed in the 3rd dasa during the
sub period of second lord (Mercury). In the sub
period cited earlier, the head of the country will be
endangered(?) The idols kept in worship will be
destroyed. There will be fear of obstructed rains (?)
The 4th dasa will cause mental agony. The first half
of this dasa will produce much distress while the later
half will bestow happiness and a prosperous calling.
The 5th dasa will be somewhat auspicious while the
6th dasa will (indeed) be auspicious. His death will
occur in 56th year, failing which 71st year will be
fatal. In his second dasa he will visit Sethu along with
his father. His coborn will be longlived. The native’s
third dasa will bring prosperity for the brother. After
30, prosperity will be on the rise and auspicious
effects of Raja Yoga will be experienced. He will
visit shrines and become famous in royal service.
Fortieth or forty-second year will cause fear of
untimely death and abundant difficulties.

772 - 773. Umbilical Cord: In case of former
half of Kalika Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascendant, the
Moon in Scorpio Navamsa will entangle the child
with umbilical cord at the time of birth, apart from
causing evils to maternal kinsfolk. But she will be a
source of great happiness to paternal side of the
relatives; the person’s paternal uncles will receive
greatly auspicious effects. Birth in this Nadiamsa
will usher happiness to father.

775 - 777. Infantile Mortality & Remedies:
Should the 8th lord Sun be in the ascendant, with a
benefic’s aspect, and a benefic’s Navamsa, the child
will incur Balarishta or infantile mortality, to some
extent, for two or three weeks in the first year, or in
the first sub period of the 2nd dasa. For this, remedies
be done in the form of worship of the image of the
Moon god made ofsilver installed ona copper vessel.
Suitable charities be also given away (at the end ofthe
worship).

778 - 782. For birth in the former half of Kalika
Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascendant, with the Sun in
Capricorn, the blemish of infantile mortality could be
overcome by propitiating the Sun God thus: An
image of the Sun God made of gold, decorated with
red apparels be worshipped at home with Japa (reci-
tation of sacred spells) and Homa (fire sacrifice) as
prescribed by the Sastras. Pacifying the Sun God
thus, the blemish can be warded off. The Moon god”s
image decorated with robes should be worshipped as
prescribed by “Chandra Kalpa" which will bring
happiness to maternal relatives, and will remove the
balarishta effects of the child as well.

Deva Keralam

783. One born in the second half of Kalika
Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascendant will be wanting in
energy. He will lead a life marked by troubles and be
endowed with brothers and sisters.

Notes: Inthe first line “Alasyaadisusaukhyavan”
appears. Alasya means want of energy. The effect of
being happy denoted by saukhya does not go well
witb “want of energy and troubled life”. Hence such
an effect is not included in the rendering.

784. Life Span: The dispositor of the 8th lord
being in exaltation and with strength will cause
longevity to the native of Capricorn, Kalika Nadiamsa.
Jupiter in the 8th, with a benefic’s Navamsa will also
bless one with longevity.

Notes: Some may like to club both the above
conditions into one to obtain longevity. However, a
purposeful interpretation does not deter splitting this
into two principles, each giving longevity. Because
each on its own merit can confer a long life.

785. Short Life: Astrologers predict short life if
Jupiter in the 8th is aspected by a malefic, and
occupies debilitation Navamsa, or a Navamsa ruled
by a malefic planet.

Notes: This does not apply to Capricom ascend-
ant as Jupiter in Leo in the 8th will not obtain
debilitation Navamsa. This should be applied to such
ascendants only where Jupiter in the 8th obtains
debilitation Navamsa.

786-7 Capricorn Ascendant - Infantile Mortal-
ity: For a native of Capricorn ascendant, Kalika
Nadiamsa, the Moon in extremis, with Scorpio Nav-
amsa, and in aspect to a malefic planet, without that

157

of a benefic, will cause infantile mortality. Should
the Moon be in association with Jupiter or another
benefic, and be InJeevitavastha, there will be nosuch
effect.

Notes: The Moon will be in Mritavastha or in
extremis in the last six degrees of an odd sign and the
first six degrees of an even sing.

“Jeevithavastha” is not a standard astrological
term, and hence defies proper identification. At best
it can be interpreted that the Moon should not be in
Mritavastha or in extremis. Opposite of Mrita (dead)
is Jeevitha (not dead, alive).

788'- 790. Capricorn Ascendant - Kalika
Nadiamsa: One born in the first half of this degree
with Jupiter in Capricorn, and Saturn in aspect to
Jupiter as the Sun is in Halaahala Shashtiamsa will
beget the following effects. He will have an even
physique which will be blood-red in complexion. His
eyes will be broad, and nose beautiful (i.e. sharp and
prominent). During childhocd, he will have an
emaciated body and be troubled by paralysis. After
3rd or Sth year he will be happy and will enjoy
physical felicity. In the 3rd year he will be greatly
endangered.

Notes; 3rd year giving happiness, mentioned in
the first place, is to be treated as faulty. Only fromthe
Sth year, the subject should be said to be happy. His
third year will endanger him in a big way, as per the
text.

791-794, Kalika Nadiamsa - Saturn in Aspect
to Mars: Saturn being in aspect to Mars and placed
in Libra, with his own Navamsa will give following
results for a Capricorn native. He will be happy after
eighth year of age. During childhood (i.e. upto 8 in
this case), there will be a mix of happiness and lack
of happiness. He will eat limited food, will enjoy
pleasures, be liberal, famous, fond of learning, mod-
est, skillful in writing and learning, fond of
Panchakshari Mantra ("Om Namassivayah"), be hon-
ourable, inclined to perform Japa (recitation of sa-
cred spells), be an expert in poetry, devoted to Lord
Siva and righteous. Further, he will be ever ready to
help others, and be more intelligent than his father.
He will have two maternal uncles, be passionate, will
have three paternal uncles, and be pious.

795 - 799. Jupiter in the 7th: For a Capricom
birth in Kalika Nadiamsa, Jupiter in the 7th gives
following results. The native’s paternal aunt will
have a long married life, will have many sons and be
auspicious. Three of his paternal uncles will be long-
lived. One of them will have two wives. Anotherwill
have a barren wife, but will acquire progeny after
remarriage. With the help of paternal uncles, the
subject will gain honour in royal service. He will be
inwardly cunning, be passionate, miserly, virtuous,

Chandra Kala Nadi

helpful to others, will honour gods and Brahmins,
will have two wives, will obtain good children and
will become wealthy and prosperous in old age. His
father will (initially) be honoured by his three
brothers, but will after some time develop enmity
with them, will undergo a family division and be
mentally distressed.

810 - 8101/2. Destruction of Spouses: Jupiter in
Virgo or Sagittarius, or in the 2nd/7th, with associa-
tion or aspect of Saturn will destroy (i.e. will kill
early) the native’s two wives. The persons’s (first)
marriage will be during his twelfth year.

Notes: Apparently it is harmful for the life-span
of spouse in case of the native of Capricorn ascendant
who has Jupiter in Cancer, Aquarius, Virgo or Sagit-
tarius in relation to Saturn.

of her progeny. During the native’s second dasa, she
will fall sick. His paternal grand-father will be
destroyed. So also his maternai uncle. Due to the
death of her brother, mother will be distressed.

$37 - 838. Fifth Dasa: During the Sth dasa, he

will be endangered by fear of untimely death. The
first sub period in this dasa will give auspicious

countries. Later on he will return to his native land.
In the sub period of Rahu........... His death will occur

cause danger.

863 - 865. Bhava Lagna: Venus should become
the lord of Bhava Lagna, and, being in aspect to the
9th lord Saturn, should beget his own Navamsa. Then
the native will reap abundant fortunes in the 3rd dasa.
The 2nd dasa will (generally) give great distress. But
its first half will cause much auspicious effects and
the 2nd half of 2nd dasa will gain entry for the subject
in royal circles. He will attain happiness with the
good offices of his maternal aunt’s husband. The said
relative’s son will also earn fortunes ofa great order,
and much happiness, and will enjoy pleasures like a
king.

Notes: Bhava Lagna is one of the special ascend-
ants. From Sun rise to the time of birth, every five
ghatis (or 120 minutes of clock time) constitute one
Bhava Lagna. In other words, the ghatis and vighatis
elapsed from sun rise to birth should be divided by
five and the quotient in terms of signs and degrees
should be added to the Sun’s longitude prevailing at
the commencement of the day.

Example: Sun’s longitude on the starting of the
## Page 180

164

day concerned = Virgo 15°.

Time of birth = 20 ghatis. Divided by 5 this
yields four signs or 120°. When 120° are added to the
Sun (i.e. 165°), we get Bhava Lagna as 285° or
Capricorn 15°.

This is as per Brihat Parasara Hora.

For further details the reader may referto Jaimini
literature.

the person in politics who will follow the king’s
orders (i.e. be close the king). He will beget a lot of
honour and be always engaged in pleasing the popu-
lace. He will himself be (equal to) a king, will have
knowledge of tastes (a branch of medical science) (or
be analchemist, a poet, a writer) and will have a soft
tongue.

876 -879. The Moon in Vargottama in Libra, «nd
inthe company of Saturn and Mars, willin the middle

undertake royal assignments and beskillful in sword-
fighting. He will be famous, virtuous, good at heart,
ever fond of learned men, valorous and highly learned.
These are applicable to the native having the Moon

881 - 8821/2. Fatal Death for Father: The Moon
in Vargottama in Libra along with the aspect, on her,
of two malefics will cause fatal death of father who
will have great fear from Nishaadas. To overcome
this blemish suitable propitiations be done. Donation
of the image of Lord Bhairava made ofsilver, holding
Kala Danda (divine staff) along with a pair of robes
will cause relief from the said blemish.

Notes: "Nishaada" in sloka 881 means a non-
Aryan tribe regarded as hunters, robbers, fishermen
etc.

“Madhyame Kale” vide sloka 881 denotes the
middle portion of Chitra Nakshatra, i.e. ending por-
tion of second quarter and beginning portion of third
quarter. It practically means the 3rd quarter of Chitra
Nakshatra where the Moon is required to be. This
gives her Vargottama position in Libra.

896 - 905. To get rid of the said blemish, the
discerning should gift away an image of Iswara (i.e.
Siva, one of the Rudras) robed in a rough garment as
laid down in Rudra Yamala. A learned astrologer
belonging to an excellent race and learned in Veads
and its divisions should be appointed as preceptor for
the purpose which will beget the mercy of Mother
Durga who is seated on a golden lotus, adoring the
Moon on Her head, destructive of enemies, fulfilling
one's desires, displaying Her hands of fearlessness,
robed in yellow garments, endowed with a smiling
face, and living in the midst of forests. With Her is
personified and identified the illusory nature of the
worldly objects. She is Bhagavathi, the giver of
fortunes. Such Durga should be meditated and
worshipped which will eliminate fear from enemies
and weapons. A golden image of Varuna, the lord of

167

waters, whose vehicle is crocodile, and who holds
Naga Pasa (Nagasthra, described elsewhere in the

notes in the present volume), should be obtained (and-
worshipped) following which one will be relieved of
bondage. On the left side of Varuna, the image of
Devi should be installed. Lord Siva, holding a skull

in His hand, adoring the crescent Moon on His head,

along with Uma, His consort, should be installed and

worshipped. Worship, Japa, and Homa for Durga

will increase the effects three-fold. At the end of the

ritual, charities should be given away. Goddess

Durga's both sides should be occupied by Varuna and

Rudra. The image of Durga should be provided with

red robes. Prayerto Uma (i.e. Parvathi) willelminate

enemies and will bless the aspirant with health,

fortunes and wealth.

Notes: The remedies given in the above slokas
are connected with the planetary blemishes in the
preceding verse (i.e. sloka 895). As such we should
take it to be general involving the worship of Varuna,
Rudra and Durga. For further details, see Rudra
Yamala.
