925 - 937. Ona day of Ashtami, Chaturdasi,
Dwadasi, or Parva (the days of four changes of the
Moon; also Ashtami and Chaturdasi of either fort-
night) coinciding with the native's birth star or its
trines, and the week day ruled bya "malefic", the wise
should choose a temple located ina shrine on the bank
of a river. There should be erected a pavilion on the
ground in the midst of which a wooden vessel be
placed containing de-husked rice grains. This should
be covered with a new cloth. An axe with a silver
handle and a sum of 100 or 50 or25 gold coins should
be given away in donation in order that the enemies
are destroyed. The donor should take his seat facing
the east and recite "Mama satru kshayarthaya thava
poojam karomyaham / Sarva satru kshayakaraayethi
madhyamam partpujayeth" (I worship you inorderto
have my enemies destroyed.) Parasu Rama, who was
fierce, who saw the blood of his enemies, who offered
## Page 186

170

their flesh, who destroyed members of royal clan,
who was chief among Brahmins and dearto Lord Siva
and who weore red robes, who adored elephant's skin
and who used the axe to destroy enemies. This ritual
will destroy enemies and save the subject from fear
of untimely death.

940 - 9401/2. Gemini Ascendant - Chirajivi
Nadiamsa: One born inthis degree with the Moonin
the Nakshatra quarters of Revathi (i.e. the Moon in
any quarter of Revathi), while Jupiter is in a friendly
Navamsa, will be a leading killer of enemies, as
stated in Sathya Nadi.

Notes: In sloka 940, the terms “C/urajivamsage
Chandre” and “Revathyamse Nisanathe” contradict
eachother. The Nadiamsa relates to birth and the first
term is corrupt. I have taken only the Nakshatra
position of the Moon for purpose of translation.

Chirajiva Nadiamsa extends thus: from 12° 24'
to 12° 36' in movable signs; from 17° 24' to 17° 36'
of immovable signs; andd from 27° 24’ to 27° 36' in
common signs. This Nadiamsa is actually known as
"Chiranjivini".

941-943, Chirajiva Nadiamsa - Former Half:
The native of Gemini ascendant, of this degree, will
be blood-red in complexion, and be valorous. His
fortunes will be through his in-laws (or he will have
fortunate in-laws). He will have three sisters, plenty
of wealth and grains. He will be a student of the
Vedas and be learned (in general). He will be a
presiding person in the reign of a great Saiva teacher.
A person enjoying freedom, he will love his family,
be honourable and respected in royal circles.

Notes: “Mahakaala Gurudvare Sarva-
dhyakshah” needs some clarification. Mahakaala is
a form of Lord Siva in his character of "great de-
stroyer". Thus, the native will hold a position witha
preceptor who propagates Saivism. In essence the
subject will be engaged in spreading Lord Siva’s
school of thought, distinctly opposed to Vaishnavism.

For those who want freedom to interpret this
complicated expression, the other meanings of
Mahakaala are supplied below.

Mahakaala = A place sacred to the destroyer-
Siva; a mythical mountain; a teacher so named;
Durga in Her terrific form; one of Her attendants; one
of the sixteen Vidya-devis; the Linga in Ujjayini; a
Goddess who executed the commands of fifth Arhat
of the present Avasarpini.

we anfet wt yeqesa aiferd
datas, art wer waarafra: ewe Il

concerned will be splendorous, will enjoy pleasures
and will be ever fond of all people.

Gemini ascendant having the Moon in Vargottama in

untimely death. Suitable remedies be resorted to.

after his 16th year. 64th year will cause near-death

Vedas and be beautiful.

36' of fixed signs; and from 10° 24' to 10° 36' of
common signs.

1035 - 1037. Gemini Ascendant: Venus ruling
‘the 5th, denoting paternal grand-father, should be in

respective Bhavas (i.e. 3rd from the Sth denotes first
brother of paternal grand-father, Sth from 5th the
second one, 7th from the Sth the third one, and so on
and so forth.)

will have huge testicles. Or else, he will be prone to
suffer from ulcers, leprosy or defects in palm orsoul.
His paternal grand-father will also suffer from dis-
eases.

1051 - 1053. Mars in 10th: For a Gemini native,

1054 - 10571/2. (a) Kaalaagni Shashtiamsa -
Father: The father of the native of Gemini ascendant
with Isaana Nadiamsa, as Mercury is in Kaalaagni
Shashtiamsa would be poorin the native’s childhood,
and would have illicit connections with females
belonging to good families. He would be lustful and
fickle-minded.

(b) Should Mercury and Venus be together in
Saptamsa, in case of birth in Isaana Nadiamsa, Gemini,
father would befriend the ruler, be passionate, and
patronized by the ruler.

(c) Mercury in Isaana Nadiamsa denotes that the
## Page 196

180

person’s father would be a devotee of Lord Siva,
would regularly worship Him and will be close to the
king’s minister and army chief. Due to the blemish
of having joined virtuous women, he (i.e. the father)
would grieve losing his progeny. He would also lose
his brothers, and would incur difficulties in his old
age.

Notes: (a) Kaalaagni Shashtiamsa = Daavaagni
Shashtiamsa. This extends from 16° 0' to 16° 30' of
an odd sign, and from 13° 30'to 14° 0' ofanevensign.

1058 - 1060. Birth should be in Isaana Nadiamsa
in Gemini while Mercury is in Vishnukalamsa. Then
the father will follow Vaidic path, be righteous,
devoted to Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva. Due to the
merits obtained by him worshipping Lord Siva, he
will beget prosperity in his middle age. All his sins
will be destroyed due to his observing vows and fasts
in devotion to Lord Siva. Quitting his mortal coil, he
will attain the Heavens and inthe present birth he wil!
be happy.

Note: Vishnukalamsa is not a standard term.
Obviously the text refers to Vishnu Shashtiamsa
which extends from 11° 0' to 11° 30' of an odd sign,
and from 18° 30' to 19° 0".

1085 - 10941/2. (a) Prior to this the marriage of
the ruler will have occurred. These are the effects for
beginning and concluding portions of sub periods of
Ketu and Venus. There will be drought conditions in
the country. One of the friends of father, a Soodra,
will obtain a son. The king, served by the person’s
father will beget married. (b) In the sub period of
Venus, his father will visita king and will gain wealth
through the good offices of the army chief. (c)
Mercury in Isaana Nadiamsa will cause prosperity of
coborns. (d) The person’s father will be happy in
Pandya kingdom and will receive royal honours. (e)
These are effects for sub periods of Ketu and Venus.
(f) In the sub period of Venus during Jupiter’s dasa
people will be troubled by revolt. Stability will result
later on. (g) Father and others will receive auspicious
effects in the said dasa periods. (h) The time of
Jupiter - Rahu conjunction will cause distress to king
and his ministers, and fear to Brahmins. Later on the
king will be destroyed with Saturn moving in Leo
through Libra. (i) Saturn’s movements in Revathi,
Sravana, Hastha, Arudra, Bharani and Svathi will
cause drought. (j) While Satumnis in Libra, retrograde

Deva Keralam

1106 - 1107. Rahu’s Sub Period: During the

main period of Jupiter, the sub period of Rahu will

## Page 200

uncles be foretold when Saturn transits the sign

Notes: The words “Kheda Modam” in the first

Bhedam” meaning grief and enmity (or division etc.)
which are part of the last sub period, of Rahu, in the
dasa of Jupiter. Because happiness is something rare
in this phase of Vimsottari which can be verified in
practical horoscopes.

1120-1121, Destruction of Mother & Coborn:

When Saturn comes to the sign identical with the

Navamsa position of the lord of the 4th counted from

the natal ascendant or the Moon sign, or toa trine to

one of the said Navamsa positions, the person’s

mother will face her end. Similarly brothers will be

destroyed when Saturn’s transit involves as above the
Navamsa position of the lord of the 10th (Jupiter).

1122 - 1123. (a) Special Rule of Transit: In
respect of a Bhava, note the Navamsa, Drekkana and
Dwadasamsa positions of the lord of the eighth
therefrom. When Saturn transits in a sign identical
with any of these divisional positions, the Bhava in
question shall be destroyed.

(b) Jupiter (instead of Saturn) in transit in an
above place will cause great happiness in respect of
the Bhava, and the Bkava effects will progress.

Notes: (a) For example, take the 2nd house in
case of Capricorn ascendant. The 8th therefrom (i.e.
Virgo) is ruled by Mercury. The Navamsa, Drekkana
and Dwadasamsa positions of Mercury be noted.
And when Saturn comes to the Rasi identical withone
of these divisional positions of Mercury, the indica-
tions of the 2nd house (viz. family, finance, eyes etc.)
will be destroyed.

(b) Conversely when Jupiter transits such a
position relating to Mercury, the 2nd house will
reveal its effects favourably and ina great measure.

1135 - 11371/2. Kamala Nadiamsa - Gemini
Ascendant: Satu ina sign of Mercury, in aspect to
Mars, and beingin Aries/Scorpio Navamsa will make
the native childless. According to sage Garga, Sat-
urn’s position in the 5th house in Kamala Nadiamsa
or his aspect to the 5th house will cause abortions to
the person’s wife. This involvement of Saturn can
however give progeny due to other Yogas (favour-
able for progeny) or can lead to adoption of a son (in
the absence of suitable yogas for obtaining a son).

Notes: “Vandhyavastha” is a peculiar term.
“Vandhya” denotes barrenness. Apparently the text

refers to state of barrenness caused by Saturn as
above.

1150. Kamala Nadiamsa - Aquarius Rasi Dasa:
The first dasa happening to be that of Aquarius -
Satum, will cause danger through water in the month
denoted by the moments of the Sun in the Rasi natally
occupied by him. His mother will incur sickness and
will survive early death.

Notes: “Kumbha Chakre” is not the specifically
used by various exponents to denote exactly the dasa
of Aquarius in Kala Chakra Dasa scheme. However,
the text used terms like Jeeva, Deha etc. which are
applicable only to KCD. Hence I interpreted the
present term and such other terms elsewhere in this
work as belonging to KCD although the ruling plan-
et’s name is as a rule added to the name of the Rasi
indicating the Dasa.

For obvious reasons, “Janma Maase” does not
indicate the first month of birth.

1152 - 1154. Malefic Rasi Dasa: During the
dasa of a malefic sign (ruled by Mars, the Sun or

mother will to some extent suffer from physical
ailments during the Sun’s adverse transition. In the
same dasa (without referring to Jupiter), his close
relatives willbe destroyed. In the second half of such
dasa, the native’s marriage will occur.

1162 - 11691/2. (a) Mars - Moon in Scorpio:
The native of Gemini ascendant’s Kamala Nadiamsa
having the Moon and Mars in Scorpio (in the 6th) will
reap abundant prosperity and will have happiness
through spouse. His step-brother will acquire prog-
eny while his full older brother will get auspicious
effects (in general). The subject will gain much
wealth and grains. He will be happy through his
father etc.

(b) Saturn’s Transit - Irrelevant: The planet
Saturn moving in Scorpio, Aries, Leo or Cancer will
cause stress of hunger to the populace. There will be
dearth of rains and occurrence of difficulties through
hunger and rectal disorders (to the public) in spite of
which people will survive (i.e. there will be no

189

casualty).

(c) Irrelevant: Saturn’s first round of transit in
fixed signs will cause distress to people. They will
mourn the death of their ruler.

(d) Irrelevant: Evils to king will come to pass
when Saturn is in the 9th, in case of a Gemini native,
during the dasa of Libra.

(e) Scorpio Rasi Dasa: The 7th lord (Jupiter) in
Pisces Navamsa will during the dasa of Scorpio will
cause sadness in the families of in-laws and will
destroy the father-in-law.

(f) Libra Rasi Dasa: During the dasa of Libra,
very important relatives will die in the in-laws’
family. His brother-in-law will be in the grip of great
danger through weapons.

(g) Obstruction by Tenth Lord: The lord of the
{0th in the 9th will cause great difficulties and will
obstruct prosperity in the Rasi dasas ruled by the th
lord (i.e.Aquarius or Capricorn, more specifically
Aquarius Rasi dasa, as per KCD). Results which are
a mix of auspiciousness and inauspiciousness will
also follow.

1170 -11711/2. (a) Mars in the 8th From Moon:
The native of Gemini ascendant will in Aquarius
Dasa suffer obstacles to his prosperity fora period of

1172 - 11731/2. The Kala Chakra Dasa periods of
the Rasis denoted by the sign, decanate and Navamsa
occupied by the 8th lord (Saturn) will give grief and
obstruct prosperity of a Gemini native. The periods
denoted by evil Rasis will cause ill-health and
financial upheavals. Else, there will be quarrels and
loss of place (or position).

Notes: Here we get one of the most precious
clues in the direction of using KCD effectively.

The dasa periods denoted by decanate or Nav-
amsa occupied by a certain planet - good or bad - will
give good or bad effects. For example 10th lord ina
given case is in his exaltation decanate or exaltation
Navamsa. The dasa indicated by the Rasi concerned
as per KCD will give excellent effects concerning the
10th house.

Similarly for other Bhavas. This clue can be
applied for the various ascendants.

ant having Jupiter in the 9th from the Moon sign will

1183 - 1187. (a) Saturn should be placed in
Kamala Nadiamsa in Libra so that death of father
occurs inthe firstsub period of the dasa of the 2nd lord
(Moon). Failing which grief to (full) sister, and step-
brother will show up. Urinary disorders (to self) and
marriage of the native’s son will follow.

(b) The first sub period of the Sth dasa will cause
prosperity to the native in his birth country.

(c) Saturn moving in Virgo, during the first sub
period or that of Mercury in the fifth dasa will
endanger the father. If not, the period will destroy a
step-brother.

(d) The sub period of Saturn in the fifth dasa will
cause the death of a brother-in-law during Saturn’s
movements in Virgo.

Notes: "Kanya Chakre" should read as "Kanya
Sanau", meseems, to have a meaningful instruction
as noted in “c” and “d” above.

1188 - 1189. General: Even a single powerful
yoga for prosperity will be capable of giving wealth,

191

will incessantly cause the progress of coborns and
will give an excess of money and red robes. The
wealth will be acquired by the powers invested by the
ruler. The person will beget a powerful position of
rendering justice. He will give happiness to men. His
entire household will spill with wealth and grains.
With the advent of Jupiter’s dasa these effects will be
specific.

Notes: Since the author has taken the verses for
Gemini ascendant, Kamala Nadiamsa, from Guru
Nadi, specific importance is laid on Jupiter’s dasa. It
is commonly to be understood that any relevant dasa
will give the good effects cited, the sum total of which
is wealth, position, happiness et cetera.

1191 - 11941/2, Death: The native of Kamala
Nadiamsa, Gemini ascendant, will die with Saturn
moving in Cancer. But Saturn moving in the end of
Capricorn, or in Aquarius, with the Sun in Leo, will
usher fear of untimely death. In Scorpio, Satur in
transit, will cause pains of the body, and destruction
of men equal to the subject (in age). In a trine to
Scorpio (i.e. in Pisces/Cancer) Saturn’s movement,
obtaining at the same time the Navamsa of Cancer,
## Page 208

192

canalso cause timely (insurmountable) death. Saturn
in Cancer in transit will cause death. Probability of
death will also exist with his movement in the end of
Virgo, orin the end of Libra, in the month denoted by
Sun in Virgo. The subject of Kamala Nadiamsa wil]
pass away in one of the three months commencing
Leo (i.e. the transit Sun in Leo through Libra), in a
dark fortnight, on a Wednesday, due to dysentery.

Notes: In these slokas, Kulira Chakre, Kanya
Chakre should actually read as Kulira Sanau, Kanya
Sanauetc. and the translation is for suggested correc-
tions. This is done in order to keep a flow with the
sequence. In some places these of course refer to
respective Kala Chakra Dasa periods.

1195 - 11981/2, (a) Aquarius Ascendant -
Champaka Nadiamsa: The lord of the ascendant
(Saturn) with Ketu in the 6th house, with Sagittarius
becoming the Aroodha ascendant (as per Jaimini
school), will make the native wealthy right from birth
and happy.

(b) Jupiter in Aroodha Ascendant: In this yoga
if Jupiter also happens fo be in the Aroodha ascend-
ant, Sagittarius, the person will be wicked, honour-
able, will be the leader of bad men, be interested in
achieving difficult things, fair-complexioned, beau-
tiful-eyed, be a king, minister, leader of an army, be
highly honoured, soft-bodied and very intelligent.
He will be endowed with all kinds of wealth, be of
peaceful disposition, will indulge in various kinds of
charities and be a lord.

Notes: (a) For Aquarius ascendant, its lord Sat-
urn in the 6th therefrom in Cancer causes Sagittarius
to become the Aroodha ascendant. Saturn and Ketu

Chandra Kala Nadi

inthe 6th (Upachaya house) will thus give riches right
from birth, and the subject will enjoy happiness in
general.

(b) With the combination cited at “a” being fully
present, the Aroodha ascendant’s lord Jupiter in
Sagittarius itself will produce the additional effects
listed. The only adversity is wicked disposition.

Also see slokas 1203-1205 infra for a modified
version.

For Champaka Nadiamsa details, refer to notes
under sloka 1412. Book I.

1199 - 12001/2. Saturn in 6th - Champaka
Nadiamsa Birth: In case of Aquarius rising, with its
lord in the 6th, making the Aroodha ascendant fall in
Sagittarius predict the following. The subject will be
irascible, honourable, fond of wicked men, be in-
wardly crooked, sickly, will cheat others of their
wealth and undertakings, and will possess a thin body
that is prone to windy diseases. During childhood, bis
body will be lean. This native will be learned and will
enjoy eating comforts.

Notes: In this yoga, Ketu and Jupiter are elimi-
nated. The lord of the ascendant Saturn alone in the
6thin Cancer, with Sagittarius becoming the Aroodha
ascendant, will give many bad effects like sickness,
and cheating disposition.

read as "Kinchid Rooksha Sariravan" denoting a thin
or emaciated physique.

Honour, learning and eating comforts are only
positive effects.

1201 - 1202. Champaka Nadiamsa - First
Half: Birth in this space in Aquarius (without refer-
ence to Saturn etc.) will make the native famous in
royal assembly. He will be an expert in giving
advices related to use of Mantras (sacred spells), and
be dear to the ruler. He will be able to understand
others’ thoughts by their mere gestures, be intelli-
gent, will enjoy powers bestowed upon him by the
king and will receive great respect and reverence. He
will be endowed with longevity, will serve the ruler
and be famous among the men of his race.

Note: “Sripankajamse” meaning birth in
Sripankaja Nadiamsa in sloka 1202 is an unwanted
addition here oritshould read as “SriChampakamse”.
It was a custom for ancient writers to add the prefix
“Sri” to auspicious Nadiamsas and such other terms.
Any way the results mentioned in the sec” .J half of
sloka 1202 shouldalso belong to Champaka Nadiamsa
when carefully compared with the rest.

1203 - 1205. Aquarius ascendant, Saturn in
Cancer, Jupiter in Sagittarius in aspect to Venus and
simultaneously getting Leo Navamsa - togetherthese
will cause a Raja Yoga, giving three conveyances.
The person will have some fear from mean people.
During his childhood he will incur disorders caused
by indigestion. Although irascible, he could be
instantly pleased and be charming in appearance.
(Breaking the flow, Saturn in 6th should not be
isolated to cause charming appearance. This position
is part of the Aroodha ascendant condition.) He will
be ever valorous, wil] have a bilious and windy body
(prone to disorders like abdominal illness, premature
gray hair, yellow sweating, jaundice, rheumatism,
and arthritis), and will enjoy pleasures of the world.

Notes: The Navamsa position in Leo is. for

193

Jupiter in the sign Sagittarius. That is Jupiter should
be between 13 deg 20' and 16 deg 40' of Sagittarius.

Ketu’s position is excluded and Venus is intro-
duced in this yoga - a different version of what is
given in “b”, 1195 - 11981/2 supra.

“Enjoying pleasures of the world” shows a high
degree of material enjoyments accruing to the sub-.
ject.

1220 - 1224. Results Concerning Father: The
Moon in Swaaha Nadiamsa will give following ef-
fects to the father of the native belonging to former
half of Champaka Nadiamsa, Aquarius. The father
will be a righteous person, wealthy and will be
affectionate to living beings. (Jeevapreetikarah need
not be interpreted as: pleasing the planet Brihaspathi.)
He will religiously recite the Rudra Japa (prayer to
Rudra, Lord Siva), be an expert in righteous and
meritorious acts, and be learned in Puranas (Hindu
mythology), and will construct temples, villages,
Brahmins’ colonies and tanks. In the middle part of
his life, fortunes will abound. He will beget a position
of authority under the king, will become an army
head, minister and will involve in political adminis-
tration of the country. He will gain happiness in his
country and be enthusiastic in destroying the wicked
(or unlawful). His wealth will be acquired through
various means. He will accomplish an us ,ertaking
with suitable expedients, and will be a skillful
gatherer of wealth. His fame will extend to many
countries during the early days of the native.

1227 - 12311/2. (a) Champaka Nadiamsa -
Aquarius Ascendant: Saturn in transit in the sign
represented by his natal Navamsa position, or a trine
thereof will cause troubles to father on account loss
of relatives, royal wrath, difficult assignments and
danger from weapons.

(b) Moon’s Dasa; For the said native, the Moon
in exaltation will in herdasa give wealth. Butthe dasa
will destroy the person’s coborn. There will be
acquisition of quadrupeds and wealth in his family.
Much troubles will occur in paternal grand-mother’s
family. Due to efforts of father, undertakings
(responsibilities) will be fulfilled.

(c) The Moon in Naga Nadiamsa in the company
of Mercury will destroy brothers. Due to the good
offices of his father, the person will prosper.

("Naagamsa Jathaka" should not mean birth in
Naga Nadiamsa. The text refers to the Moon insuch
a position in case of Aquarius ascendant, Champaka
Nadiamsa. Such briefings in many parts of the text
should suitably be understood, and the rendering is
accordingly made keeping the spirit of the original in
tact.)

(d) Irrelevant: The 2nd year will cause evils
and great danger to the king’s people.

(e) Continuation of “C” above: The person will
obtain a new job and will flourish under the king.

1254 - 1258. Aquarius Ascendant - Champaka
Nadiamsa: (a) The Moon sign of the spouse will
correspond to the sign represented by the Navamsa
occupied by the 7th lord (Sun) or a trine thereof.

(b) The native will be happy and will prosper
after marriage.

(c) He will incur danger to spouse during his
fourth dasa and he will immediate get remarried.

(d) Father’s Death: During the concluding
phase of the third dasa, his mother will be emaciated
(i.e. grieved) due to loss of her husband. (Thatis, the
subject will lose his father.) Alternatively, the 2nd
dasa during the sub period of 8th lord will endanger
his father. If he survives the sub period that is the 6th
in order (in the second dasa) will cause father’s exit.
(“Saadhanesanthe” should read as
“Saadhanesanthare”’ .)

(e) Paternal Grand-father: During the 11th
year of age (or) in the junction period of the 2nd dasa,
(with the end of first dasa) danger to the said relative
will come to pass, with Saturn moving in the end of
Libra, or in Scorpio.

() Dasa of 10th Lord: This dasa will give
equally auspicious and inauspicious effects.

1263 - 1264, Karma Samrajya Yoga for Im-
movable Ascendant: The lord of the 10th, posi-
tioned in an angle to the Moon, and aspected by the
lords of the 2nd and 11th (both counted from natal
ascendant) will cause Karma Samrajya Yoga. Asa
result, the person will be rich, valorous, widely
famous and will be wealthy with a lot of possessions.
He will adopt a virtuous path and will serve the king
and his minister. He will be lustful, be ever righteous
and will enjoy much pleasures.

Notes; The yoga given above applies to an
immovable ascendant, viz. one of Taurus, Leo, Scor-
pio and Aquarius.

Example: Take Taurus as the ascendant. The’
lord of the tenth from ascendant is Saturn. Lords of

‘2ndand 11th in orderare Mercury and Jupiter. Hence

the yoga is formed thus for this ascendant - Saturn in
the 10th from the Moon sign, and in joint aspect to
Mercury and Jupiter.

This yoga may not exactly apply to Leo whose
2nd and 11th lord is Mercury. Here instead of his
aspecting Venus, the 10th lord, it should be relaxed
to be a conjunction.

1267. Aquarius Ascendant: Satumin Champaka
Nadiamsa, while there exists Samrajya Yoga in the

sloka, the involvement of the lord of the ascendant,

sign, will take the person’s father to dizzy heights in
terms of fortunes and progress.

1270 - 1278. Aquarius Ascendant - Champaka
Nadiamsa: (a) The 2nd dasa will give sadness ina
limited way while the 4th dasa will cause much grief
(in terms of family deaths).

(b) Sakata Yoga: Due to Sakata Yoga the dasa
of 10th lord will give some distress.

(c) Fourth Dasa: The 4th dasa will cause in-
crease of prosperity, but the first sub period will
indicate much distress. The said sub period will
promote enmity with the king and Vaishnavites
(those belonging to the school of Lord Vishnu).
Gradually prosperity will be on the increase from the
middle of the 4th dasa. In this dasa, there will be a
family marriage, but children born (to the subject)
will be destroyed. His wife will incur evils.

(d) Jupiter’s Dasa: In the sub period of the lord
of the ascendant, during the dasa of the 2nd lord
(Jupiter) the person will acquire wealth, grains and”
## Page 216

* 200

ornaments. He will visit pilgrimage centers and
beget auspicious effects. In the sub period ruled by
the lord of the 8th (Mercury), he will incur physical
ailments. His spouse and progeny will face distress.
After a while happiness will revive. The sub period
of Ketu will destroy the wealth gathered. In the
months denoted by adverse solar transits, in the said
Ketu bhukti, he will incur fear from king, thieves and
fire. The sub period of the 9th lord (Venus) will
increase prosperity apart from happy events relating
to progeny; but there will be evils in the family of in-
laws. In the Sun’s sub period due to royal assign-
ments (rather wrath), he will have to leave the
country. More specially in the sub period of the
Moon. Further in the Moon’s phase, he will have
illnesses of the body.

1288 - 12931/2. Damini Yoga: (a) There should
be Damini yoga in the horoscope while the ascendant
lord Satu is in extremis (Mritavastha). Such a
person will beget much fortunes in his early child-
hood. He will be somewhat dusky in complexion, be
crafty, an expert in use of weapons, a poet, be
honourable and will have many brothers and many
sisters. Out of the many sisters, all will die (prema-
turely) but one. He will have only one daughter
whom he will get married in 25th year. During 20th
year, his trial for her marriage will face obstacles due
to his (earlier) sins. His father will die en route during
his (native’s) 22nd year. During his 16th year he will
have abundance (of everything). During his 20th
year he will lose his mother in a foreign land.

(b) With Damini Yoga, Saturn placed in the 6th
with debility in Amsa (not Navamsa but other appli-
cable Aries divisions) will cause a long-lasting fever
for the mother of the native. He will lose his father
during his boyhood and will incur much grief.

(c) Kedara-Damini Yoga will give wealth in the
16th year. After 30 prosperity will be on the rise. His

201

happiness follow the destruction of his relatives.

Notes: (a) Damini yoga as per standard prescrip-
tion occurs whenall the 7 planets are insix signs. This
is a Sankhya Yoga. Saturn also being a part of the
yoga, Should be in Mritavastha, that is in the last six
degrees of an odd sign, or in the initial six degrees of
an even sign.

(b) In this Damini Yoga, Saturn instead of being
in Mritavastha, should be in Cancer with Aries
divisions.

(c) Kedara-Daminiis not one yoga. Kedara yoga
occurs when all the 7 planets are in four signs.
Apparently the author had some thing else in mind or
there is some compositional error.

faces fafrter aaTeey FAT RE Il

aasatd aetfra strat oIeTAT eee I

1294 - 1297. Saturn in extremis (Mrithavastha)
in the divisions belonging to the 6th (Cancer) will
give Raja Yoga effects buta limited length of life. It
will cause the end of father or mother in the first dasa
of the subject. He will be troubled by penury, grief,
danger and urinary diseases. Due to a revolt (in the
country) he will be displaced and will wander in
many places. He will serve a Mlechcha king, be a
great sinner and will lose many of his brothers.
Throughout his life he will be grieved, and will live
through sinful means.

Notes: "Shashiamsake" means the divisions of
Cancer. That is Saturn in Shodasa Varga scheme
should obtain many of Cancer positions.
Shashtamsaka here does not refer to the one sixth
division, which is not recognised in the Shodasa
Varga.

will make the whole life miserable. (That is miseries
willbe endless.) Untimely death will occur in the sub
period of a malefic or of 8th lord during the dasa of
Satur placed in extrentis.

Note: The condition of Ghora Nadiamsa be
ignored with the introduction of “Mrithavastha”.

1300 - 1304 1/2. Aquarius Ascendant
Champaka Nadiamsa: The Sun in debility as the
Moon is in the 6th (Cancer) will give effects as

“i

mentioned in “a” to “c” below.

(a) This yoga will cause much prosperity. Fur-
ther results for this yoga are - One will have many
brothers and sisters, including one older brother. He
will be wealthier than his father and will enjoy
powers granted by the king.

(b) Second Dasa: Due to enmity with
Vaishnavites, he will have checkered prosperity in
the 2nd dasa. During the 8th yearhe will pass through
a very difficult phase. His fortunes will take a

favourable tum following change of ruler. His.

brother will beget married. The person will derive
much happiness in his marital life. His father will live
a happy life. This dasa will destroy his general
fortunes and paternal grand-father as well. His 5th

Chandra Kala Nadi

year will give much distress to his father.

(c) Third Dasa: This dasa will give abundant
happiness in the sub period ruled by the 7th lord (the
Sun). There will be generally obstacles with scope
for some happiness. (That is, the other sub periods in
this dasa will not be of great help.)

1305 - 13071/2. Father’s Ill-health & Rem-
edies: In case of Aquarius ascendant, Champaka
Nadiamsa, Ketu in the Sth in aspect to Saturn will
cause enlargement of the spleen or glands and cough
(like tuberculosis of the lungs) to the native’s father.
Necessary remedies be sought to overcome these
diseases. On Sundays the names of the twelve Suryas
should be recited (i.e. reciting Dwadasaditya Stotra)
and donation of red silken clothes to an astrologer be
given. Following these, recovery of father’s health,

great happiness, firm wealth and lasting auspicious-
ness will accrue.

1314 - 1317. Mudrika Nadiamsa: Birth in the
former half of this Nadiamsa ina fixed sign (specially
Aquarius) will obtain following results, if Jupiter is
placed in Mohana Nadiamsa. The subject will be a
staunch Saivite. Yet he will be of bad conduct. He
will live through various sources of business activi-
ties, will have two brothers and three sisters, be
honourable, endowed with a step-brother, and be
emaciated due to loss of a brother during his child-
hood. His father will be miserable during his old age,
will grieve the loss ofa son, will sufferfrom disorders
of lungs and eyes and will lose the wealth accumu-
lated by him.

Notes: Mudrika Nadiamsa rules from 18° 24' to
18° 36' of movable signs; from 11° 24' to 11° 36' of
immovable signs; andd from 3° 24' to 3° 36' of
common signs.

1318 - 1321. (a) Two Marriages to Father &
Grand-father: One born in Mudrika Nadiamsa of a
fixed sign and having Venus in Mohana Nadiamsa
will beget the following effects. His father, so also
paternal grand-father, will be twice-married.

(b) Step-mother: The native of former half of
Mudrika, fixed sign, will have a step-mother (without
involvement of Venus as in “a” above).

(c) Father & Grand-father: Other authorities
state that the father and paternal grand-father of the
native described in “b” would in early childhood
undergo difficulties and be prosperous in the middle
part of life. The paternal grand-tather would obtain
a son through another wife and would have secret
pleasures with his maid-servant. The native’s father
would live in a town surrounded by forests in the
middle of his life, would become very wealthy,
prosperous and endowed with money, grains and
robes.

1336 - 1340. Mudrika Nadiamsa - Former
Half: (a) One born ina fixed sign in this space of the
zodiac, with the Moon in Sumathi Nadiamsa, and
Jupiter in Mohana Nadiamsa will lose (one of) his
older brother(s). His elder brother will be quite a
righteous person while father will never be relieved
of debts. The subject will be endowed with two sons,
be honourable, will worship Lord Siva, will honour
the words of his father and will commitsome sins due
to ignorance. Due to the curse of a Brahmin in an
earlier birth, he will be troubled by tuberculosis.

(b) Many Deaths in 3rd Dasa: He will die in his
third dasa following the death of his father. He will
incur grief on account of the destruction of his elder
brother. His step mother, wife and two paternal
uncles will also pass away (during this dasa).

1356 - 13591/2. Fixed Sign - Mohana Nadiamsa:
A younger brother of this native will obtain a son after
a long spell of time. According to the school of sage
Vyasa, the said brother will have two sons, and many
daughters. One of them will be long-lived. As per
Garga, the brother in question will beget only dead
children and _ by his efforts, he will be fortunate
enough to have one child with long life. During the
native’s youth, his step brother will incur diseases of
blood vessels, and will lose weight. If he survives he
will be endowed with sons and daughters.

Notes: Reference to former half of Mudrika
Nadiamsa in sloka the first line of sloka 1356 is an
erroneous addition in the original and hence not
added to the translation.

1364 - 1369. Mohana Nadiamsa - Fixed Sign:
(a) Ketu in Aries with the Sun will restrict the number
of issues. The subject will obtain a son in his fourth
dasa.

(b) The Sun in the 5th in aspect to or company
of Mars will prove an obstacle in respect of acquisi-
tion of progeny. Anyway, after a long interval, a son
will be obtained. As per Garga, this yoga will kill the
issues as and when they are born. To overcome this
evil, a Linga (idol of Lord Siva, or of Naga Raja, the
king of Cobras) made of gold be given away in
charity.

(c) Progeny’s life-span will be increased by
aonation of a golden (Naga) Linga if Saturn is in the
5th house from the natal ascendant in the company of
the Sun, and begets a Navamsa ruled by Jupiter. The
suggested donation of Naga Linga should be givenon
a Monday evening (Pradosha). In the absence of this
remedy, the person will beget many daughters while
sons born to him will only find their instant exit from
this mortal world.

Notes: (c) Pradosha = the first part of the night;
evening personified as a son of Dosha, Blemish, and
associated with Nisitha and Vyushta. Vyushta is day-
break personified and is the son of Pushparna and
Dosha, or the son of Vubhavasu and Ushas.

1371 - 1372. (a) One will obtain progeny in the
4th dasa, through his third wife. (This relates to
Mohana Nadiamsa, vide sloka 1341 supra, and is
independent of sloka 1370.)

(b) Saturn in the 5th (for a fixed sign, with
Mohana Nadiamsa ascending) will give only one
spouse (i.e. no other marriages) but no progeny.

(c) The subject of Mohana Nadiamsa (without
reference to Saturn) of a fixed sign ascending will
have three wives and be endowed with progeny. In
his second dasa, he will beget ornaments and paternal
wealth. (To wit, Saturn in the Sth in case of birth in
Mohana Nadiamsa will stall additional marriages.)

With the Moon in Libra with Pisces Navamsa while

results will come to pass. The first two dasas will give

texts, he will live ina river-bound region, suffer from
physical ailments, have limited gains and will incur
both happiness and unhappiness in life.

causes Soola Yoga. In the second half of the dasa of
the said Saturn, one will be greatly in grief. His wife
as well as his brothers will incur danger. Following
death of his father (in Saturn’s Dasa), he will earn
grief and penury. Particularly the sub »° fod of Rahu
and of Mercury, or in the concluding portion (in the
dasa of Saturn) will cause these untoward events
coinciding with adverse Jupiterian and solar transits.
Severe difficulties and dangerous fever will result.
Donating a pot of honey, this phase of ill-health can
be overcome.

1394 - 1395. (a) Irrelevant: The ruler will be
destroyed when Saturn comes to the sign indicated by
the sign occupied by the 10th lord’s dispositor, or a
trine thereof, or the sign thatis at birth aspected by the
lord of the 10th.

(b) In the context of the said transit, the person’s
coborns will be in grief, due to illness of a child in
their families.

(c) The 2nd line of sloka 1395 is ungrammatical
and incomplete, dealing irrelevantly with the death
of the king.

t“b” conveys a proper instruction. Saturn’s transit as

due to progeny’s illness.

One will beget paternal wealth. There will be a
marriage at home. There will be famine in 30th, 8th,
38th, or 40th year. Many difficulties and strife to
populace will come to pass. The gravity of the famine
will be revealed according to the planet Saturn
moving in Taurus, Libra, Aquarius, Scorpio, Pisces
or Leo, or Jupiter Rabu conjunction in transit; the
tuler will quite the world; the people will be in the
grip of hunger; devils will wander in the villages,
forests and burial grounds flaunting human heads.
Saturn moving in trines will destroy the ruler of the
kingdom Chola.

1404 - 1410. Fixed Sign Ascending: (a) Birthin
Kesari Yoga with the Moon in Sumathi Nadiamsa in
Libra will cause influx of wealth in the 4th dasa, and
happiness after the age of forty.

(b) Should Saturn be in Libra, the second half of
his sub period in the 4th dasa wil] cause destruction
of enemies. The person will gradually progress.
After 38, his progress will commence and some
happiness will prevail. He will obtaina son inthe end
of the said sub period. In the end of the 3rd dasa, or
in the first sub period of the 4th dasa, family quarrels
will prevail followed by worries onaccountofcoborn.
The person will gain horses (“Ashta” should be
“Aswa”), cows and housing properties in the region
of a great hill. He will commence a new business
undertaking and will get wealth and auspicious*ef-
fects.

(c) Due to blemish of 8th lordship (apparently

Jupiter ill-placed), he will see his friends in distress.

1413 - 1415. Aquarius Ascendant: (a) In the
beginning of the dasa of Mercury occupying Pisces,
the native’s son will beget married. In the middle of
the sub period (of Mercury), auspiciousness will
increase in the family circles. End of the said sub

in the family. The person will incur positional
displacement and his health will recover later on.

(b) The sub period of Venus in the 4th dasa will
cause a division amongst brothers, apart from mutual
quarrels between thesons of the person’s step-brother.

1432 - 1434. Aquarius Ascendant - Sumathi
Nadiamsa: (a) The fifth dasa will cause marriage to
the person’s daughter. It will grant him financial
gains. During his 54th year (or) in the end of Ketu
dasa in 61st year of age, death will strike him. The
sub period concerned will be that of the planet ruling
the dasa which is sixth in sequence.

(b) Should the lord of the ascendant (Saturn) be
witha malefic, the period following 56th year will be
a source of distress (i.e. fear of death). In that dasa
(i.e. in the 5th dasa, as Saturn is with a malefic at
birth) mental distress, loss of money and a mix of
happiness and unhappiness will result.

Although “Sumathi” Nadiamsa is prescribed in
the text, the sequence ofslokas suggests that itshould
be Mohana Nadiamsa, in Aquarius ascendant.

physical troubles, mental distress, loss of money and
destruction of son.

1436 - 1437. Aquarius Ascendant - Mohana
Nadiamsa: Should the planet Ketu, being the rulerof
the 5th Nakshatra (read fifth dasa), be with a benefic,
and be ina benefic’s Navamsa, only good results will
follow (in place of above-mentioned evils). How-
ever, the sub periods of malefic planets, in the said
dasa, will counter happiness. The sub periods of
benefic planets will cause beneficial results; auspi-
ciousness will follow the Sun’s favourable move-
ments inthe form of acquisition of wealth and grains
and a male offspring.

1441 - 1442 1/2. Mohana Nadiamsa - First
Half: His next birth will be ina family of traders. In
this birth (under discussion) he will obtain worthy
son(s). Fortieth year will usher great prosperity.
Following his 52nd year, a great danger will appear.
From birth he will be wealthy. In between he will be
emaciated due to grief. Afterwards his prosperity
willbe on the rise. His fourth dasa will give him much
happiness. Following destruction of enemies he will
be happy and endowed with financial gains and
wealth.

1443 - 1445. Aquarius Ascendant - Maalini
Nadiamsa: (a) One born in the former half of this
Nadiamsa as Jupiter is in Kalakoota Nadiamsa will
be blood-red in complexion and will have an auspi-
cious appearance. (b) If Jupiter is in Capricorn
Navamsa, (instead of being in Kalakoota Nadiamsa
as per“a”) the subject will be famousand will prosper
greatly.

Notes: From sloka 1443 to 1508, there is confu-
sion in the original as to which ascendant these
discussions belong to. Moreover, along witha giver
Nadiamsa of birth, yogas like Matanga and Koorma
are also tagged as an additional condition. I feel these
additions are corrupt and hence excluded from trans-
lation as and when necessary. As far as possible, I
tried to sort out these contradictions and explain ina
suitable manner.

Generally these slokas belong to Aquarius as-
cendant, according to my understanding. The reader
will find clear reference to Maalini Nadiamsa,
Aquarius ascendant, in slokas 1505 - 6 infra.

mother will be long-lived and will have three sisters.

a long married life (i.e. her husband, the native’s
father, will be long-lived) but be distressed due to
destruction of her brother. (The second line of sloka

1449 is a mix up and apparently it conveys that the
present native will be a loner, without any co-born.)

1455 - 1457 1/2. Aquarius Ascendant - Maalini
Nadiamsa (continued): (a) For birth in this degree,
one’s mother and (half) sister will be long-lived.

(b) The Moon: The Moon in Durbhagavastha
(read Durbhaga Nadiamsa) will make the sister un-
fortunate and destroy his coborns.

(c) Father: With birth in the subject degree, the
native’s father will have two wives. According to
another authority he will have three wives (vide sloka
1447) and be very fortunate. He will visit many
countries and will involve in buying and selling (i.e.
trading). He will acquire precious stones, grains and
classic robes and will have many business activities.
He will subsist through intelligence ("Vriddhi
jivanavaan" should be "Buddhi jivanavaan"”), He
will have brothers and sisters.

1474, Business Partnership: The subject of
Maalini Nadiamsa, first half, belonging to Aquarius
ascendant, will have friends (or partners, as the
expression is replaced by “Sahavanijya jeevanam” in
another version) if the 10th lord joins Rahu and
begets Cancer Navamsa.

Notes: This sloka is rendered after some recon-
struction (“Malinyamse poorvabhage prajathasya
karmese rahusamyuthe kuliramse...) to get the re-
quired instructions in a practical spirit. Apparently
this hints at possibility of partnership in business
activities, aS against proprictorship, as in modern
times.

1483 - 1487. (a) Mars Dasa: During the time of
his undergoing the 10th lord’s dasa, his friends will
be destroyed; his sister will be troubled and his
mother subjected to danger.

(b) The mother of the native of Maalini Nadiamsa,
Aquarius, will be mentally deranged in her old age
(independent of “a” above). She will dic ina forest,
struck by wild animals like a tiger.

(c) There are others who state that violent death
of mother (in the event of the condition at “b”) will
occur if the 11th lord is with Rahu in a malefic
Shashtiamsa. Further during his childhood his father
will die a pitiable death due to a woman (or) due to
delirium in a foreign land.

(d) The subject of former half of Maalini
Nadiamsa, Aquarius ascendant, will become rich in
the middle portion of his life. In his old age,
difficulties and penury will exist. Childhood will be

somewhat marked by happiness. After the age of 43;
perhaps for “three years”, he will be troubled.

1498. In the case of the native of Maalini
Nadiamsa, Aquarius, the sub periods of the Moon,

Notes: These three planets are not favourable for

these three sub periods will give restricted results.
This axiom can generally be applied to Aquarius
ascendant notwithstanding the Nadiamsa of birth.

cited will occur in the dasa of Mars, the dispositor of
the Moon.

1510 - 1511. Achala Nadiamsa - Fixed Sign
(upto sloka 1549); The native of former half of this
Nadiamsa will be a Brahmin. He will be dark in
complexion and will look emaciated. He will be dear
to his elder brother. During his childhood he will be
gentle, but will incur difficulties.

Notes: Achala (or Achalaprabha) Nadiamsa is
from 23° to 23° 12 'of movable signs; from 6° 48' to
7° of immovable signs; and from 8° to 8° 12' of
common signs.

1512. No Younger Co-born: Mars in the as-
cendant and Jupiter in the Sth will deprive the person
of younger brothers and youngersisters. Evenifthere
be such births, they will only die.

Notes: The word “Sithe” meaning Venus, should
be “Suthe” meaning the Sth house. The text does not
imply three planets, viz. Mars, Jupiter and Venus in
the ascendant.

“Ambaramse” should read as “Achalamse”
meaning Achala Nadiamsa, not Ambara Nadiamsa.

1515 - 15181/2. (a) The native of first half will
live in a small village during his second dasa. In
childhood he will wander in the hilly region of the
West or in the region of Gokarna. He will be troubled
by poverty.

(b) One belonging to the second half will make
his fortunes in the birth region.

(c) The subject of first half will be displaced due
to a revolt and will later return to his birth region.

(d) One born in Aquarius with Aries Navamsa
will beget prosperity in a shrine. He will gradually
eam fortunes being close to the king of Andhra
region.

(e) The native of former half will lose his father
in the midst of his boyhood. His mother will be long-
lived. (The effect concerning mother is contradictory
to earlier statement.)

Notes: The rule at “d” is for birth in Aquarius
ascendant, Aries Navamsa. That is the ascendant
should be between 20° 0' to 23° 20' of Aquarius. No
Nadiamsa comes in the picture.

The instructions contain in “a” to “c” and “e”
apply to the given Nadiamsa, ina fixed sign including
Aquarius.

1526 - 15291/2. Hurdles in Getting Progeny &
Remedy: (a) Jupiter in the Sth house in aspect to two
malefics denotes that the native of Achala Nadiamsa
obtained a curse from Brahmins due to his previous
life’s sins. (That is the reason which will pose prob-
lems in respect of progeny in the present birth.) To get
rid of this sin, he should take bath in the Sethu and
worship Lord Siva and donate the image of a golden
Nagalinga on a Monday evening. Following these,
birth of children will come to pass.

(b) Should the Sun be placed in the 11th, the
native of former half of Achala Nadiamsa (will face
obstacles in begetting progeny and finally) will be
blessed with a son due to merits acquired by observ-
ing religious vows for the Sun God.

1530 - 15311/2. (a) Danger Through Water:
The lord of the 3rd aspected by Mars and begetting
debilitation Navamsa will cause death of a son of
elder brother through water.

(b) The person belonging to former half of
Achala Nadiamsa will bring up the progeny of his
sister. He will enjoy happiness through maternal
uncles right from his childhood.

Notes: (a) Lord of the 3rd, which is 5th (progeny)
from the 11th (older co-born) indicates progeny of
older brother or sister.

Mars in the sign Cancer or in Cancer Navamsa
will pose danger through water to the specified
relative. If Mars happens to be the lord of the
ascendant, the victim will be the native himself.

(b) Mars is notin the picture. Itis merely because
of the birth in this particular Nadiamsa.

1556 - 1560. Libra Ascendant: (a) Ifthe birth be
in the “Kaala of Pisces” Jupiter while Jupiter is in the
sign Leo with Leo Navamsa the subject will be
devoted to Lord Vishnu and he will honour Brahmins
and Gods. He will follow the codes prescribed by the
Vedas.

(b) If in this yoga Saturn joins Jupiter (in the sign
Leo), he will disregard such prescriptions.

(c) As per Naradeeyam the subject of Agada
Nadiamsa of Leo ascendant will be devoted to Lord
Vishnu and be highly prosperous. This applies to
birth in Jupiter’s Hora.

(d) Venus and Jupiter should be in mutual as-
pects being the rulers in order of “Moon’s Kaala” and
“Sun’s Kaala” the result of which is fortunes.

(e) Venus ruling the “Kaala of the Moon” and
placed in the 11th will give knowledge in rules and
philosophy of one’s ownreligion. Further the person
will be adept in creating difference of opinion by
mean expedients.

Notes: Three peculiar terms like Meena Kaala
are used which are not widely used astrological
terms. None of these could be found instandard texts.
They certainly do not refer to planetary hours.

1563 - 1564. (a) The Navamsa occupied by the
lord of the ascendant should be owned by Venus who
in turn should be in association with Saturn by aspect
or conjunction (in Rasi chart). Then the subject will
be intent upon find others’ faults and be very intelli-
gent. The ascendant should be in Jagathi Nadiamsa.

(b) Jupiter should be in Vargottama in Leo while
Anes is the Aroodha ascendant. The result is the
native will have limited number of offspring.

Notes: These two slokas, in my view belong to
Jagathi Nadiamsa in Leo. These do not belong to
Libra, if we scrutinize the expression - “Lagnesamsa
pathau Sukre”. In the first instance, if the ascendant
is Libra, Venus himself is the lord of the ascendant
and he will not be referred to in such indirect term.

From an understanding of related passages on
earlier occasions, I feel these two slokas deal with
Leo ascendant. Hence in “b”, the Sun as lord of natal
ascendant should be in Sagittarius as Jupiter is in
Vargottama in Leo.

1576 - 15801/2. Agada Nadiamsa - Libra As-
cendant: (a) Jupiter in the 1 1th house with Venus will
give wealth.

(b) If Saturn joins Jupiter in the 11th, one will
obtain many dead children. By suitable efforts, the
life-spans of children can be increased.

(c) Jupiter in Agada Nadiamsa will deprive one
of paternal happiness. His mother will live with him
(i.e. not with the father) and he will enjoy fraternal
happiness. He will have two honourable brothers and
one auspicious sister. Another sister will be in
troubles. The person will be grieved on account of
loss ofa son. He will be excellent among his co-born
and his progeny will prosper. To overcome the
blemish in respect of progeny the native should
donate a specified plant called "Sisumaara", (whose
scientific name is Delphinus Gangeticus) fcl! swing
which his children will be blessed with longevity.

Note: Sisumaara also means a collection of stars
resembling a dolphin and held to be dear to Lord
Vishnu. The north-east point in the Heavens is also
called Sisumaara.

The plant in question seems to be in wide use in
traditional medicine and seems to grow abundantly in
Gangetic plains.

aspected by Mars and occupying a Navamsa of
Saturn will usher danger to progeny through poison,
fire or water. To ward off the blemish, the Moon God
Should be propitiated. The image of Lord Siva
adoring the lunar crescent should be obtained and
worshipped as prescribed. Astrologers should be
pleased with gifts. Following these measures chil-

1584 - 1587 1/2. (a) Incase of the subject native,
Saturn, Venus and Jupiter in the 8th from the Moon
will bring evils to progeny due to curse of Brahmins
in the previous birth of the native. To overcome this
blemish, he should have dips in the Sethu, donate a
golden image of Cobra and perform Japa (recitation
of divine names). Asa result he will get progeny with
long life-spans - two sons and one daughter.

(b) According to the school of Parasara, Jupiter
in Agada Nadiamsa will give two long-living sons
and will destroy other children.

1588 - 1592. (a) Dead Children: Saturn in the
8th from the Moon sign, or in the 11th from the

ascendant will give dead children. To overcome this
blemish, remedies as prescribed be done. Or else,
## Page 242

226

sage Garga declares, children will only be dead as
they are being born. Remedies will ensure their
longevity.

(b) Saturn’s Transit: Counted from a given
Bhava if Saturn moves in the 8th, orina trine (Sth/9th
from the Bhava in question), he will destroy the
Bhava in the respective time periods. According to
experts in astrology, this has reference to the as-
cendant andthe Moon sign as the case may be. The
effects due to transits should be enumerated with the
help of directional influences.

(c) The Dasa periods related to the 7th lord or the
ascendant lord will cause progress of fortunes and
acquisition of wealth and a life-partner.

Notes: The effects given in these slokas apply in
general to the various ascendants and not confined
only to the current Nadiamsa.

(or) in the 2nd dasa. Later, in the junction periods of

Chandra Kala Nadi

first and second dasa, the person will be in fear of

1609 - 16141/2. (a) Evils in the in-law’s family
will strike six years (after the native’s marriage).
When Saturn transits the sign which is at birth
aspected by Mars, the 2nd lord, or the sign repre-
sented by the Navamsa occupied by Mars, ora trine
thereof, these evils will occur. Or else, his wife will
incur physical ailments; his progeny will cause grief
and his father-in-law will be troubled.

(b) Dasa of Rahu: Rabu in the 9th will in his
Dasa, during the sub period of 2nd lord Mars or 10th
lord Moon will cause financial gains. In the sub
period of 8th lord (Venus), the dasa of the said Rabu,
will produce mental anguish, leaving the country,
checkered prosperity and a mix of auspicious and
inauspicious effects. After these, the person will
restart living in his birth region during the sub period
of the Moon (in Rahu dasa). The sub period of Mars
will obstruct prosperity, and griefdue to displacement.
After 26th year of age, Lakshmi Yoga will occur to
him giving wealth; he will beget abundant money,
ornaments and birth of sons.

1615 - 1618 1/2. (a) Vargottama Rahu: Rahu
in Vargottama Navamsa in the 9th (Gemini) will give
much gains in the end of his dasa. In the middle of
the dasa, mental anguish will prevail, while the
commencement of the dasa will be on an auspicious
note.

(b) In any dasa, the sub period of Venus (being
that of the 8th lord) will cause evils to the kinsfolk of
the native of Agada Nadiamsa, Libra ascendant.
(“Sarvabhuktau” is excluded in translation, as it
means al] the sub periods.)

(c) Venus inownsign, own Navamsa, Vargottama
Navamsa or in another benefic’s Navamsa will cause
much grief in the end of the dasa (of Rahu). In the
junction of dasa (of Rabuand Jupiter) there will be no
blemish. (In my opinion, there is some confusion in
these assertions.)

(d) Gaining Wealth: The native of Agada
Nadiamsa will beget good effects in the junction
period of third dasa (i.e. concluding portion of third
dasa). He will move in villages and gain wealth.

1619 - 16211/2. Birth of Co-born: Jupiter’s
transit in the sign identical with the Navamsa occu-
~pied by the lord of the ascendant (Venus), or a trine
thereof, or the one that is in aspect to the lord of the
ascendant will cause birth of co-born. So also from
the lord of the 9th (Mercury).

(b) Birth of Off-spring: Note the Navamsa
occupied by the 9th lord Mercury at birth. Also see
in which Navamsa the dispositor of the 7th lord
(Mars) is placed. When Jupiter moves in one of the
signs identical with these positions, ora trine thereto,
the subject will beget an off-spring.

Notes: (a) Two planets feature here - Venus as
lord of the ascendant, and Mercury lord of the 9th.
Jupiter’s above transits involving the positions with

Chandra Kala Nadi

reference to these planets will give rise to acquisition
of co-born. These transits should be applied to the
native according to the age. Mercury is discussed in
“b” above in respect of obtainment of progeny as
well.

(b) Mercury as the 9th lord, and dispositor of
Mars as the 7th lord being discussed in respect of
progeny should be profitably noted. Mars comes in
the picture, perhaps because, he owns a trine from
each of the two signs of Jupiter. Aries is trine to
Sagittarius while Scorpio is trine to Pisces.

1622 - 16251/2. (a) Obstruction: In the case of
Libra native, the Moon in Melapa (read Melapavarga)
Nadiamsa will cause obstacles to one’s progress in
the 29th year. Further, mental distress and loss of
place will result. 28th year will be one of good
progress giving the mercy of Goddess Lakshmi (i.e.
wealth). After the 28th year, it will be a phase of
difficulties.

(b) Saturn’s Transit: When Saturn is in transit
in the sign represented by the Navamsa of the 6th
lord, or the sign that is at birth aspected by the 6th
lord, or ina trine to either of these, the person’s elder
brother will undergo mental anguish. Further his
older sister-in-law will incur some evils. The na-
tive’s marriage will also take place in this phase. He
will spend away the wealth gathered.

1644 - 1651. (a) Libra Ascendant - Agada
Nadiamsa:; Saturn transiting the sign represented by
the Navamsa occupied by Mars, ora trine thereto will
cause difficulties.

(b) Irrelevant: This transit will also cause strife
to people in “Martian countries”. The ruler will die
With Saturn’s transit in the end of Libra or in Scorpio.

Chandra Kala Nadi

Loss of army chief and minister will come to pass
with Saturn’s transit in end of Aries, or in Taurus,
Cancer, Leo or in trines of Pisces. The kings of
Pandya and Chola kingdoms will be destroyed. The
5th house and the 9th houses are called Rajya Sthaana.
In the sub period of the 8th lord strife and quarrels in
kingdom will exist. Royal ministers will face de-
struction when Saturn transits the resulting sign
represented by the sum of 12th and 4th lords’ posi-
tions or the sign represented by 8th lord’s Navamsa,
in evil years and evil months.

(c) Physical illness will come to pass in the sub
periods of malefics. To overcome this blemish
Saturn should be suitably propitiated.

Notes: In the above eight slokas, most clues are
irrelevant to natal horoscopy. In some places ill-
conceived versions also exist. The reader can how-
ever get benefit from “a” and “c” above.

1652 - 1654 1/2. (a) 8th Lord’s Navamsa: When
malefics in transit come to occupy a sign which is in
trine from the 8th lord’s natal Navamsa, one will
incur sickness to self, apart from troubles to spouse,
progeny. and kinsmen.

(b) Deha & Jeeva Rasis (as per KCD): A
malefic planet in the Deha Rasi will cause physical
ailments and mental anguish. In Jeeva Rasi, it will
promote distress to life force. Both the Rasis in
occupation will only destroy the physique (i.e. will
terminate the mundane journey). (These apply to
transit.)

(c) For Capricorn Navamsa or Cancer Navamsa,
Scorpio is Deha Rasi while Pisces is Jeeva Rasi. (This
is an uncontextual and incomplete clue.)

will not die) and will get auspicious effects.

1657 - 1658. Sickness: He will fall sick in the
month when Venus or Saturn sets in the heavens.
Sickness will also be possible in malefic sub periods.
The effects described by the astrologers for the
various planetary transits will bear truth.

Notes: Setting in the heavens means remaining
in combustion. As planets almost regularly set, this
instruction should be used in association with suit-
able directional influences and transits.

However, combustion of Saturn, Venus etc. is
just not restricted to a month alone.

1679. One born in the said Nadiamsa, having
Venus in Mohana Nadiamsa will ever be devoted to
Lord Vishnu. He will follow the school of
Madhvacharya.

Notes: Madhvacharya was the founder of a sect
of Vaishnavites in the south of India. He was a
Kanarese Brahmin called Ananda Tirtha
Bhagavthpada, or Madhu, said to have been born
about 1200 A.D. His doctrine is commonly called
Dvaita - i. e. “Duality” - (in opposition to the
“Advaita”, i.e. Non-duality of the great Vedanthist
Sankaracharya) and his sectarians are called Madhvas.

1683. Lordly Father: Venus should be in Mohana

born of a person equal to a lord.

Notes: “Kshiteeswaramsasthe” means the Nav-
amsa or Nadiamsa entitled “Kshiteeswara” which
makes no sense. Another version has the expression
“Khiteeswara Samyukthe” requiring Venus to be
with “king” which again makes no sense. Mars has
asynonym, “Kshitija” - born of the earth. Perhaps the
text means that Venus should be with Mars and be in
specified Nadiamsa - Mohana. The rendering is for
the supposed version.

1686 - 1688. (a) Venus in Aslesha: The native
of Mohana Nadiamsa, Libra ascendant, having Ve-
nus in the 10th in Aslesha Nakshatra along with the
11th lord. (the Sun) will have two older brothers.

1689 - 16911/2. (a) Scorpio Navamsa: The

native of Libra ascendant with Mohana Nadiamsa,

having Ketu and Venus in the 10th will be associated
with a girl living in royal palace. In this case Venus
should simultaneously beget Scorpio Navamsa.
According to another authority this combination will
give fondness for pleasures through the queen. And
the subject will be very intelligent. He will befriend
a king who will be interested in performing vile acts.
The person will be happy gaining precious jewels.
(b) Venusian Shashtiamsa: Ifin the above yoga
of Venus-Ketu in the 10th house, Ketu begets a
Shashtiamsa ruled by Venus, the native will earn the
liking ofa king, will gain conveyances from the king
in return for gems (i.e. underground treasures handed
over to the Administration will fetch him rewards)
will have four to six brothers who will be long-lived.
Notes: (b) Shashtiamsa rulership is very simple
to be calculated. The first Shashtiamsa of a sign is
ruled by its very lord, the 2nd thereof by the lord of
the 2nd sign therefrom, the 3rd by the lord of the 3rd
therefromand so onandso forth. The 13th, 25th, 37th
and 49th ofa sign will again be ruled by the lord of
that sign itself.
Example: The 1st Shastiamsa of Aries is ruled by
Mars, the 2nd one by Venus, the 3rd one by Mercury,
the 4th one by the Moon and so on and so forth.

of arc.

1692 - 1698. Co-born: (a) The ascendant lord
Venus in Mohana Nadiamsa while the 11th lord (Sun)
is in Sura Nadiamsa, the person’s older brother will
be famous, be the head of an army and many steeds,
be miserly, passionate, and will be prone to danger
through weapons ina war. The eldest of all brothers
will be more famous than his father, be highly
prosperous and will have two wives.

(b) With Venus in Mohana Nadiamsa (not in-
volving the Sunas at “a”), there will be two wives for
a brother who is the 2nd in series in the family.

(c) One born in Mohana Nadiamsa, Libra as-
cendant with Venus joining Ketu denotes that one of
the sisters-in-law of the native will desire another
man (i.e. will have illicit relations outside wedlock).
Further, his eldest brother’s wife will have pregnancy
problems, will however give birth to progeny and will
pass away after some interval. One of his paternal
uncles will be long-lived, will have three wives and
many of his children will die to trouble from snakes.

1705 - 1707 1/2. (a) Spouse: The ascendant lord
Venus in Mohana Nadiamsa as Mars the 7th lord is in
Sobhana Nadiamsa will give a spouse who will be
virtuous, chaste and be endowed with one brother.
She will give birth to offspring after some delay, will
please her husband (i.e. the native) and will be
auspicious.

(b) Progeny: Saturn in aspect to Mars and Rahu
and occupying a Navamsa of Venus will cause a
spouse who is somewhat sickly; she will be troubled
by abortions. To overcome these blemishes, (the
couple) should bathe in the Sethu. Following this,
progeny who can live long will be bornand the spouse
will be immune to abortions.

1708 - 1714. (a) Devout Wife: Jupiter should be
the ruler of the 7th Aroodhapada in case of Libra
ascendant. Mars should be in Sobhana Nadiamsa,
without a malefic’s aspect. As a result the person’s
spouse will be chaste and devoted to him.

(b) Seventh Aroodhapada: If Jupiter becomes
the lord of the 7th Aroodhapada while Venus is in
Mohana Nadiamsa, the subject will have two wives
and will obtain good sons. His father will have one
marriage. The native will have two brothers both of
whom will have two wives each. One sister will be
childless and will have an adopted son. There is also
a possibility thata brother could have three wives. So
also his paternal uncle will have three wives and will
obtain progeny in old age. His grand-father will be
famous, will be honoured in royal assembly, will be
surrounded with children and grand-children, and
wil grieve in his old age on account of loss of a son.
The effects stated concerning grand-father shall bear
truth. The subject will lose his father in the ninth year
of his age, either in the sub period of the 10th lord or
2nd lord (in the first dasa). His mother will also
simultaneously offer herself to the pyre of her hus-
band. Children of grand-father’s younger brother
will incur sickness and troubles. His grand-father
will also lose a son and be in much grief, during the
commencing phase of the native’s second dasa.

Notes: (a) For Libra ascendant, the 7th lord Mars
should be in Aquarius so that Sagittarius becomes the
7th Aroodha (or Dararoodha Pada). Jupiter will be
the lord of the said Pada. That is, Mars in Aquarius
in the 5th with Sobhana Nadiamsa, without malefic
aspect, will give the relevant effects.

(b) Again Mars in Aquarius, with Jupiterbecom-
ing the lord of the 7th Aroodha, while Venus is in
Mohana Nadiamsa will cause the effects mentioned.
Inthis case, the Nadiamsa position of Mars in Aquarius
is not restricted to Sobhana.

1715-1717. (a) WhenJupiter rules the 2nd dasa
he should intransit occupy the 8th. Then in that Dasa,
distress apart froma mix of good and bad effects will
come to pass for the Libra native. Many of his
relatives will be destroyed and the person will as a
result be in much grief.

(b) In the dasa of the 6th lord (Jupiter) one will
earn royal wrath. His older brother will be in distress,
but will make much progress when the native is inthe
first phase of the said dasa. Afterwards he will be in
trouble and his progress checked.

1718 - 17281/2. Effects of Transits during
Jupiter’s Dasa:

(a) Saturn: Distress to brothers willaccrue with
Saturn’s transi in the sign that is at birth aspected by
6th lord Jupiter, or the one that is identical with the
Navamsa occupied by Jupiter, ora trine thereof. The
subject will also acquire prosperity as well as obsta-
cles to prosperity, i.e. ups and downs.

(b) Transit of Venus: During the operation of
the 6th lord Jupiter’s dasa, when Venus comes to the
sign occupied by the 6th lord at birth, one will be
displaced. He will further be troubled by fever and
ill-health, misunderstandings with co-born, and some
evils to his spouse.

(c) Transit Saturn: Saturn in transit in the Sth
(from the Moonsign) during the rulership of Jupiter’s
dasa will also give identical results (as at“b”). Inthe
4th he will cause great agitation. Ina trine to the 4th,
the same effect will materialise to some extent. But
when Saturn attains Cancer Navamsa, more auspi-
cious effects will be felt; due to mercy of the emperor,
the person will obtain wealth.

(d) Venus Sub-period: In the dasa of Jupiter, in
Venus’ sub period one will obtain wealth but will be
displaced in the end (of the sub period).

(e) Jupiter in 12th: 20th yearorend of 21st year
will be one of great difficulties when Jupiter comes
to the 12th in transit.

(f) Transit Saturn - Irrelevant: During the dasa
of Jupiter, Saturn moving in the 4th will cause change
of king, and death of the queen.

(g) During the rulership of third (lord’s) dasa,
Saturn’s transit in the 7th or in the 11th, will cause
grief to the person’s co-born. Or else the king will
die(?)

(h) Saturn in Libra in transit will promote the
prosperity of the subject. He will also visit the king
of his country. Due to association with his older

237

brother he will acquire ever-lasting wealth.

(j) Saturn moving in Virgo will cause debts and
mental distress. The native will live in a different
village (or place). Later on, he will return to his birth
place.

1729 - 17311/2. Jupiter Dasa - Rahu Bhukti: In
the dasa of Jupiter and in the sub period Rahu, when
Venus moves in the Sth one will acquire money. But
the gains will be limited. If Rahu moves in the 8th
from the natal Jupiter, the dasa lord, or in the 12th
fromthe ascendant, the person and his paternal uncle
will acquire physical ailments. Yet, bis kinsfolk will
in general beget auspicious effects and celebrate
birth of children. In the months denoted by adverse

solar transits, in the said sub period, the subject will
be troubled by fever.

1732 - 17351/2. (a) 2nd Dasa - Rahu Bhukti:
Jupiter becoming the lord of the 2nd dasa will give a
mix of good and bad results in the sub period of Rahu,
in case of the native of Mohana Nadiamsa, Libra
ascendant.

(b) Saturn’s Navamsa: The sub period of a

planet occupying Saturn’s Navamsa will give ex-
tremely inauspicious results when the dasa of Jupiter
## Page 254

comes to rule the native. Additionally his sister-in-
law will also be in trouble.

(c) Rahu’s Bhukti: In case of Libra ascendant,
see if Jupiter is placed in the 9th (in Gemini). Then
the sub period of Rahu in the dasa of the said Jupiter,
will in its concluding phase, destroy the progeny of
the native’s brother being then born. So also in
respect of the progeny of his paternal uncle. This
phase could also destroy the prospects of their nup-
tials. - The persons’ relatives will be on visits to
shrines and acquire merits.

1736 - 1739. (a) Libra Navamsa: In case of
Libra ascendant, Saturn in aspect to Mars and obtain-
ing Libra Navamsa will make the person given
inwardly to anger. He will be a pleased soul and will
have enmity with his kinsfolk.

(b) Scorpio Navamsa: The natal ascendant be-
ing Libra with Scorpio Navamsa will give following
effects if Saturn occupies Scorpio Rasi. He will be
attached to vile people, be passionate, will serve a
king who takes to bad ways, will incur the wrath of
the king, bea sinnerand will take to bad ways. He will
suffer from urinary disorders, be emaciated and will
torture living beings. He will sing the praise of his
king.

1740 - 17411/2. Kulaghna Shashtiamsa: The
blemish of Saturn being in Kulaghna Shashtiamsa
will cause sickness to the native’s sister-in-law and
her son. Saturn in this Shashtiamsa in aspect to two
malefics will cause evils to the progeny of his brother
and paternal uncle. In the dasa of such Satur,
children of kinsfolk will be destroyed. The native
will remarry and obtain auspicious effects.

Notes: Kulaghna Shashtiamsa extends from 3°
30' to 4° 0' of an odd sign, and from 26° 0' to 26° 30'
of anevensign. Kulaghna means ruining the family.
Generally a relevant planet in this Shashtiamsa will
be a stumbling block in obtaining progeny.

1742 - 17461/2, (a) Sun - Mercury: The Sun in
Sura Nadiamsa and Mercury in Melaapa (or Melaa,
also Melapavarga) Nadiamsa will cause happiness to
the Libra native after the age of 25.

(b) Venus’s Navamsa Dispositor: Due to the
blemish of the Navamsa dispositor of ascendant lord
Venus, the native of Mohana Nadiamsa will be
grieved on account of displacement for eight years.

(c) Saturn in the 2nd and Mars in the 8th will give
effects of what is called “Keka Yoga” and will
destroy (even) great wealth.

(d) Mercury’s Navamsa Dispositor: Saturn
joining the Navamsa dispositor of 9th lord Mercury
will cause wealth through royal favours in the 25th
year or in the 19th year. With the help of his older
brother, he will resume living in his native place.

(This effect should be linked to “b” above.) Further
he will visit the king and will be ever happy.

1747 - 17511/2. (a) Acquisition of Son: The
person belonging to Libra ascendant when Saturn
transits the sign indicated by his own natal Navamsa
position, or a trine thereof, will obtain birth of a son.

(b) In the beginning or ending of Saturn’s dasa,
when Saturn joins (in transit) the (natal sign position
of) 6th lord (i.e. Jupiter) or the (natal sign position of)
Navamsa dispositor of 9th lord, there will be visit to
a shrine and (consequent) acquisition of a son.
(“Punyatheerthe Suthotsavam” means birth of a son
in a shrine. There is another version which apads
“Punyatheertham Suthotsavam”. The rendering
above is made keeping in view the following hints.)

(c) Bathing in Sethu: In the sub period of Rahu
during the dasa of Jupiter, or in the first sub period of
Saturn’s dasa, the native of Libra ascendant will have
dips in the Sethu and will acquire a son.

(d) One born in Mohana Nadiamsa, Libra as-
cendant, will have his first impregnation ceremony
with Saturn moving in Libra, during the Sun’s south-
erly course. His paternal uncle will also obtain
progeny. In the end of the dasa, his brother will beget

progeny. Children thus born will be somewhat
inflicted with Balarishta effects (infantile mortality).

1752 - 17551/2. (a) The native of Libra ascendant
having Mercury in Melaa Nadiamsa with the Sun in
the 10th will obtain a daughter through first wife.

(b) Jupiter in the 9th while the Moon is in the Sth
will cause birth of a male issue. The first wife will
give birth to three children. One of them will die.

(c)Saturn placed atbirth in Kulaghna Shashtiamsa
will in his dasa, during the sub period of Venus, will
kill the first wife of the native of Libra ascendant.
There will however be fear of untimely death in the
sub period of Mercury and troubles from windy
disorders to the first wife. She will also incur
problems of indigestion. Suitable remedies (for
Mercury’s sub period) should be sought.

1756 - 17571/2. Blemish to the Seventh House:
Incase of Libra native, Saturn inthe 2nd while Venus
is in the Sth (Aquarius) with Capricorn Navamsa
causes blemish to the 7th house indication. As a
result, the person’s first wife will be destroyed.
Remedy lies in worshipping the image of the zodiac;
giving donations to the astrologer will ward off the
possible evils to the said spouse.

1758 - 17601/2. Spouses & Progeny: Fora Libra
native, Mars in Sobhana Nadiamsa will give two
## Page 256

240

long-living wives. The person will be happy after
second marriage. Both the wives will yield offspring.
He will have a total of seven children. Five of them
will be endowed with long life-spans. Five daughters
and (two) sons will be had by the native. These
effects will come to pass in the dasa of the lord of the
Sth (Saturn). Further he will enjoy effects of Raja
Yoga (due to the said position of Mars) and will enjoy
happiness on account of co-born.

Notes: “Aayushmathi Kalatre Dwe” is replaced
in another version by “Kalatradwayamaayushyam”
denoting two long-living wives. Similarly, the ex-
pression “Chiraayushaastheshu...” is replaced by
“Panchasamkhyaa chiraayushyam” hinting at five
long-living children.

1761 - 1763. (a) Navamsa of 10th Lord: If
Satum occupies the Navamsa occupied by the 10th
lord Moon (i.e. Satur and the Moon should be
together in navamsa), the dasa and sub period of
Satur will produce Raja Yoga (prosperity). The
person will make his fortunes in his native region.

(b) The sub period of the lord of the Navamsa
occupied by the 11th lord (Sun) will give great
happiness (in the dasa of Saturn). Further, he will
procure many precious jewels, valuable convey-
ances, offspring and highly auspicious effects.

(c) One will attain merits due to numerous
charitable activities and will involve in repairing
dilapidated public places in the dasa of 10th lord’s
Navamsa dispositor (apparently Saturn dasa, vide
notes under “a”) provided Mercury, the 9th lord, is in
(the subject) Nadiamsa (that is Sobhana, vide sloka
1758).

Notes: (a) “Karmesasthamsage” as appearingin
the text only means that Saturn should be in the same
Navamsa as the 10th lord Moon is. However if the

Chandra Kala Nadi

expressionis “Karmesasyaamsage”, itmeans Satum
should be in the Navamsa owned by the 10th lord,
Moon, that is Cancer. The former as appearing in the
original seems to be more logical.

(b) “Yannavamsasthe Bhuktikaale” is replaced
by “Yannavamsesa Bhuktikaale” in another version.
The rendering - the sub period of the Navamsa
dispositor of the Sun - is for the second suggestion.
The first one is somewhat inconclusive.

(c) The conditions laid in sloka 1763 are not
Straight but crooked. These are brought out in the
translation after some experience with the mind of
the author. One may or may not agree with me.

1764 - 1769. (a) Mercury in Melaapa Nadiamsa
causing Vishnu Yoga will in the Sth lord’s dasa cause
the Libra native perform many charitable activities.

(b) TheSun inthe 10th (Cancer) inSura Nadiamsa
While Mercury is in Melaapa Nadiamsa will produce
excellent charitable activities through the native’s
hands. He will be lustful and will construct a colony
for Brahmins (i.e. will donate houses to deserving
people). After the age of 25, in the Sth lord’s dasa, the
said native will be happy. Following the 27th year,
one with Vishnu Yoga will be famous. He will make
his fortunes from a new king, and favours from the
queen and be close to the princess.

(c) One born in Mohana Nadiamsa, Libra as-
## Page 257

Deva Keralam

cendant will obtain a powerful position under the
king in the dasa of the 4th lord, Saturn. (Vishnu Yoga
seems to be a redundant condition.)

(d) In the sub period of Venus, the ascendant
lord, that of Mercury, the 9th lord, and thatof the 10th
lord Moon, the person will enjoy great prosperity (in
Saturn’s dasa).

Notes: (a) Vishnu Yoga is a redundant term
which appears in many places in this part. In my
opinion this has no relevance.

be in aspect to Mars, and should be in the sign Scorpio
with Capricorn/Aquarius Navamsa. Lastly heshould
be the ruler of the third dasa (the first being that of
Rahu). The result of all these is gaining lordship over
treasury, wealth and precious jewels in the sub period
of the planet that is placed in a favourable Navamsa.
Notes: “Yogamsa graha bhuktishu” being a
round-about term is provided witha feasible meaning
as above.
