1771 -17771/2. (a) Adversities relating toa given
Bhava will occur when transit Saturn reaches or
aspects the 8th thereof.

(b) Evils to one’s kinsmea will result the transit
of Saturn in the sign identical with the Navamsa
occupied by the 8th lord at birth, ora trine thereof, or
in the sign that is aspected by the said 8th lord.
Diseases, royal wrath and intense difficulties are also
predicted by the astrologers in this context with
(Saturn’s movement in the) sign occupied oraspected
by the lord of the 8th (Venus), ora trine thereof (will
be revealing) correlated with adverse months and
years (i.e. adverse transits of the Sun and Jupiter in
order).

(c) Agiven Bhava’s effects will be destroyed by
transit Saturn in the sign or Navamsa occupied by the
lord of the 8th from that Bhava, or a trine to either of
these. These effects declared by astrologers in Sarva
Nadi will become true in the dasa periods denoted by
the dispositors of the lord of 2nd, 8th or the 7th. The
sub periods will be of obstructive planets.

1778 - 17791/2. Diseased Spouse: The Libra
native of Mohana Nadiamsa having Saturn inthe 7th
in joint aspect to Rahu and Mars will have a sickly
wife who will also be troubled by evil devils (er
spirits) etc. In the absence of these, she will have
obstacles (for obtaining progeny). The person will
anyway be happy and will beget offspring in remar-
riage.

1780 - 17821/2. Jupitershould be in the 9th in full
## Page 258

242

strength and be the lord of “Kalaamsa” (part of a
part). Then the native with Vishnu Yoga will in the
3rd dasa will become wealthy. Due to the good
offices of his father, he will enjoy prosperity from
birth to death. He will ever gain through the fortunes
of his co-born. In the dasa denoted by the lord of
“Kalaamsa” his gains will be restricted and a mix of
good and bad effects will prevail. He will be happy
in the first dasa, more especially in the 3rd dasa.

Notes: Strange terms like “Kalaamsa” and
“Kalaamsesa” appear in this part, defying scope of
translation. We can make some partial gains out of
these instructions as under:

The native of Libra ascendant having a powerful
Jupiter in the 9th house will reap wealth in the 3rd
dasa, and will obtain uninterrupted prosperity with
the help of father. His brothers will be responsible for
his progress.

As for the dasa of restriction, the secret is
unsolvable.

The next clue about Ist and 3rd dasa is clear.

1783 - 1788. (a) Satur with full strength in an
angle to the Moon will in his dasa and sub period
Cause great prosperity.

(b) One born in Mohana Nadiamsa, Libra as-
cendant, will obtain the mercy of the queen. Due to
change of the king, he will obtain wealth in the third

Chandra Kala Nadi

“a ”

dasa. In Saturn’s sub period (“a” above) during
adverse solar transits, he will be somewhat distressed
due to troubles to his spouse. There will be grief in
his in-laws’ family, but his brother-in-law will cel-
ebrate the birth of a son. The native will beget
auspicious effects in the months coinciding with
auspicious solar transits. In adverse months he will
be banished, will visit shrines and will beget limited
happiness. (Susobhanam is a contradictory term.)

(c) In the 3rd dasa’s first bhukti there will be fear
out of famine.

(d) Jn the dasa of Saturn placed in the 2nd, the
wives of the natives relatives will be subjected to
evils and be destroyed. His brothers will undergo a
family division. The native will however obtain
happiness and jewels (i.e. wealth) through a change
of king.

Notes: (a) Here Saturn is required to be in
“Cheshta Kendra” of the Moon, as per the original
whereas it should just be “Kendra” or angle from the
Moon. For the term “Cheshta Kendra” atts not
apply to the Moon and the Sun.

1789 - 1800 1/2. Dasa of Saturn: Saturn in the
2nd in Scorpio, with Aquarius Navamsa will in his
dasa, and the sub period ofa malefic, coinciding with
adverse solar transits, cause fever, distress and royal
wrath. The native will visit shrines along with his
king (?) and there will be fear from poison, thieves
and fire for his kinsfolk. The sub period of Ketu will
give these effects (or will be specially revealing as
against other malefic sub periods in the dasa of
Saturn). The sub period of Venus (in the dasa of
Saturn placed as defined) will give a mix of good and
bad effects. The adverse effects will include enmity
with people in the king’s employ. The concluding
part of the sub period of Venus will cause much
distress. The sub period of the Sun will also cause
much distress apart from expenditure beyond re-
sources. The sub periods of the Sun and Venus will
cause diseases of the rectum and sight. In the sub
period of Venus in Saturn dasa, an auspicious func-
tion in the family will occur following which great
distress will prevail in adverse months. In the sub
period of the Sun, he will be engaged in royal duties,
and his king will be a victim of great danger. The sub
period of the Moon will give extensive diseases.
Mars sub period will promote marriage of his son,
much auspiciousness, professional advancements and
destruction of enemies. Although the sub period of
the Moon will give some happiness, there will be
perpetual mental strain. The sub period of Mars will
prove auspicious but its end will be distressful. The
sub period of the Moon will endanger the king greatly
apart from troubling.the minister and relatives. Ra-
hu’s sub period will destroy the native’s relatives.
The sub period of Mars will destroy the good effects,

243

will give happiness after a spate of events like fear
from king and thieves. When Saturn moves in transit
in adverse degrees (or Navamsa) during Rahu’s sub
period, one will incur evils to his kinsfolk in evil
months apart from distress to paternal uncle, and
destruction of close relatives. Jupiter’s sub period
will give a mix of good and bad effects.

Notes: We can rearrange the whole thing ina
nutshell as under to have a better picture:

In case of Libra ascendant, Saturn being in the
sign Scorpio, between 23° 20' and 26° 40' of arc, with
Aquarius Navamsa, will give the undermentioned
effects in the relevant sub periods.

1. Malefic’s Sub Period - Fever, distress and
professional troubles to self; Danger from poison,
thieves, fire and government to his relatives.

2. Venus’s Sub Period - Good and bad effects in
general, enmity in high circles, diseases of eyes and
anus, auspicious function in the family. The sub
period concludes with distress.

3. Sun’s Sub Period: Distress, expenditure,
diseases of eyes and anus, engagement in govern-
ment duties.

4. Moon’s Sub Period: Extensive diseases,
happiness in general, but mental stressful.

5. Mars’s Sub Period: Initially troubles through
king, fire and thieves, later on marriage to son,
professional progress, destruction of enemies.

6. Rahu’s Sub Period - Destruction of relatives.

7. Jupiter’s Sub Period - Mix of good and bad
effects.

1801 - 1806 1/2. (a) Dasa of 5th Lord Saturn:
In this dasa, the native of Libra ascendant will obtain
auspicious effects in the family during the sub peri-
ods of the lords of 10th (Moon), 11th (Sun), 7th
(Mars) and 9th (Mercury). In the sub period of the
Moon, or in the end of the (Saturn’s) dasa (i.e. last
phase of sub period of Jupiter), orin the sub period of
8th lord Venus, evils to wife, mental distress to self
and to co-born will come to pass. The sub periods of
benefic planets will yield inauspicious effects while
contrary will prevail in the ones ruled by malefics (in
the dasa of the 5th lord Saturn). Jupiter’s sub period
will (also) be inauspicious.

(b) The Moon: Incase of Libra ascendant, see if
the Moon is in Aquarius (in the 5th) with a Navamsa
of Saturn, while Saturnis ina Navamsa of Jupiter. As
a result, the dasa of Saturn will give inauspicious
effects, with intermittent good effects.

(c) If the Moon is found to be in Vargottama
Navamsa in Aquarius, the sub period of Jupiter (in the
dasa of 5th lord) will give sound health and will not
be an obstacle to one’s prosperity.

(d) The Moon ina trine of Aquarius (i.e. Gemini/
Libra) will cause Saturn dasa to be even in respect of
effects. (This relevantclue is made best use of though
it is not as clear as it should be.)

Notes: General guidelines are formulated for
Saturn’s dasa with reference to Libra on the horizon.

The sub periods of Mercury, Sun and Mars will
be favourable. Venus and Moon in their sub periods
will give inauspicious effects. So also Jupiter.

It is significant that the sub periods of benefic
planets, particularly Venus and Jupiter, will be inaus-
picious in Saturn dasa, while the ones ruled by
malefics, viz. Sun and Mars (also by Rahu and Ketu)
will give good results for a Libra native in Saturn’s
dasa.

However, the text specially makes Mercury
auspicious, by an exception, though he is a benefic.

ora trine thereof, the person will lose his mother. The

1812 - 1813. (a) Financial gains, Raja Yoga
(prosperity), acquisition of ornaments, progeny and
auspicious effects will result in the dasa of the
Navamsa dispositor of the 11th lord, Sun. Further, in
his old age, he will gain wealth and fortunes.

(b) The dasa of the 9th lord (Mercury) will prove
auspicious and will give marriage to daughter, apart
from grand-children to the native.

amy ste yareer weafeafaerat |
## Page 261

Deva Keralam

Tae Tent fates igeey

1814. Jupiter in 9th: The dasa of the 9th lord
(Mercury) will cause financial gains through royal
ministers’ mercy provided Jupiter is in the 9th
(Gemini).

Notes: In “b” at sloka 1812-1813, Mercury dasa
is said to be auspicious in case of Libra ascendant as
for marriage of the native’s son. Further grand-
children will be born to the subject according to his
age.

But in the current sloka, an essential condition is
laid down for Mercury dasa to be favourable to the
subject in terms of financial gains - that Jupiter should
be in the 9th at birth. This means with Jupiter in the
9th, the Libra native’s Mercury dasa will not be so
helpful for progress.

Jupiter is one of the most adverse planets for
Libra ascendant. Mercury is also the lord of the 12ib
though simultaneously of 9th, and can cause some
mischief in his dasa at some stage or the other. To
counter his partial evil propensities, an equally tough
evil lord is needed. And that is none other than
Jupiter.

This kind of hidden clues in the Nadi texts stand
apart and prove quite helpful in analysis ofa practical
horoscope.

Insloka 1816-1817, forexample, Mercury as the
12th lord is said to be dangerous forthe progeny of the
native in his own dasa and own sub period. The text
does not call Mercury the 9th Jord in that context.
This shows how a “favourable planet” can also be
unfavourable.

1816 - 1817. (a) Inthe dasa of the lord of the 12th
(Mercury), the sub period ruled by the dispositor of
the Moon, or that of Mercury itself will destroy the

1818. General: Note the lord of a given Bhava
and see when his dasa operates. The sub periods ruled
by the lords of the 6th/8th from that Bhava will
destroy the effects thereof.

Notes: This is a very important clue. As an
example, take Libra ascendant. The Moon rules
Cancer, the 10th, indicating one’s profession. From
Cancer, the 6th and 8th in order are Sagittarius and
Aquarius. Hence the sub periods of Jupiter and
Saturn, in the dasa of the Moon, will generally give
adverse effects about profession for a Libra native.

1825. Melaapa Nadiamsa: The native of Libra
ascendant with (Mercury) in Melaapa Nadiamsa will
incurunavoidable death in Saturn’s sub period during
the dasa of the lord of the 8th counted from the Moon
sign.

Note: The Nadiamsa position is for Mercury and

Chandra Kala Nadi

not for the ascendant. The word “Mercury” is

deficient in the original and is to be understood as
existent, when read in sequence with other parts.

1826. Sobhana Nadiamsa: Mars in this space
will cause untimely death in the 45th year for which
suitable remedies be resorted to.

Notes: Sobhana Nadiamsa extends from 16° 0'to
16° 12' of movable signs; from 13° 48' to 14° 00' of
immovable signs; and from 01° 00' to 01° 12' of
common signs.

1827 - 1820. Mohana Nadiamsa: Venus in
Mohana Nadiamsa will endanger the subject un-
timely in the 51st year or 56th year. Further relatives
of his age group will die (in these years). In the 28th
yearorin the 32nd year, he will losea co-born. Noting
Venus in the above specified degree, one should
declare mental distress when Saturn moves in the end
of Scorpio or in Sagittarius. Further, his death will be
unavoidable in the 61st year. The month concerned
will be coincidental with the Sun’s transit in Aquarius
through Aries. These are the effects for the said three
planets (viz. Mercury, Mars and Venus) in the speci-
fied Nadiamsas (in case of birth in Libra ascendant).
Moreover Venus in Trailokya (i.e. Mohana) Nadiamsa
will in the junction period of Saturn (with that of
Mercury) endanger father by physical ailments fol-
lowing which the mother will also die.

1831 - 18361/2. (a) The dasa of the lord! che Sth
(Saturn) will cause birth of children and also destruc-
tion of (some) child or children. The native will
acquire enmity with relatives.

(b) When Saturn attains the sign Leo during his
zodiacal movements, destruction in the family (i.e.
possibly a family division) and a mix of good and bad
effects will materialise. His brother will beget mar-
ried, and he will be on inimical terms with - his
paternal uncle. (“Graha” should read as “Griha”.)

(c) The dasa of Ketu being the third in series will
cause fortunes. He will however have a separate
business due to enmity with his kinsfolk.

(d) His relatives will be a source of much trouble
when Saturn and Rahu in order transit the 12th and
9th. He will as a result be grieved.

(e) In the dasa and sub period of Ketu, death of
a relative will come to pass.

(f) The first sub period of the 4th dasa will usher
much distress. The middle portion of this dasa will
bring grief, apart from:some illness to one’s co-born.

(g) The above effects from “a” to “f” are for the
position of Venus in Trailokya (i.e. Mohana)
Nadiamsa as declared by the learned in astrology (in
addition to the earlier stated ones).

1837 - 18381/2. Capricorn Ascendant- Gopriya
Nadiamsa: The subject belonging to this space of the
zodiac, as Saturn is in Vargottama in Pisces will have
a blood-red physique, be learned, will enjoy pleas-
ures, will have (only) one brother and many sisters,
and be wealthy.

Notes: The first two lines of the Sanskrit text
need some reconstruction which has been done with
the help of the clues in the next two lines. Otherwise,
the first two lines do not tell us as to who should be
in Vargottama and where. Further “Jhashamse”
meaning Pisces Navamsa cannot also be properly
allied.

1839 - 18411/2, (a) Rahu - Mars: The native of
Capricorn having Saturn in Pisces, while Rabu in
Gemini in aspect to Mars is in Aries Navamsa, will be
fortunate and will have one brother. In the 2nd dasa
(or) in the 12th year (not “Dwadasamse”) he will
obtain a (surviving) brother. Prior to this, brothers
born will die.

(b) Saturn: The lord of the ascendant, Saturn, in
Vargottama Navamsa in the 3rd, without being in
connection with a malefic, will give one brother,
much wealth and robes.

Notes: (b) “Ekabhratrupriyo” should read as
“Ekabhratruyutho”.

Saturn in Pisces from 26° 40' to 30° will be in
Vargottama Navamsa. He should be free from
malefic connection. If however he is related to a
malefic, his ability to give wealth and acquisition will
be paralysed, and he will prove quite ordinary.

1842 - 1844, (a) Extensive Trading: Saturn in
Vargottama in Pisces will in the case of the native
belonging to the subject Nadiamsa in Capricorn,
while Jupiter is in the Nadiamsa called Ganesa, will
cause livelihood through extensive trading activities.

(b) Co-born: During the second dasa’s Rahu
bhukti, the native will obtain co-born. To overcome
the blemish in respect of co-born (passing away till
his age of 12), remedy suggested earlier (read
suitable remedy) should be undertaken.

(b) “Poorvoktha” reads as “Poorvokthe” refer-
ring to the blemish cited earlier, not to the remedy.

1845 - 1849. Effects about his co-born are now
narrated. The person will be dear to his older brother.
He will have three or foursisters, be passionate, more

to his mother and be honoured in royal circles, will

enjoy prosperity in his youth. He will be endowed
with many sons (or children) and much wealth, will

brother’s son, be famous among his kinstolk, long

1851 - 18521/2. (a) Grand-father: Saturn in
Gopriya Nadiamsa as the Sthlord Venusis in Pramoda
Nadiamsa will produce the following effects. His
grand-father will be a famous person.

(b) The Native: Further, as a result of the above
yoga, the native’s fortunes will be abundant in the
middle part of his life. He will have many a co-born,
be sacrificing in disposition, be fond of Brahmins
who follow the Vedic codes, be an expert in the
conduct prescribed for the family of his birth, will
patronise his kinsfolk, be honourable among his
relatives and will enjoy favourable effects duc to the
good deeds of his grand-father.

1853 - 1856. Mercury - Venus - Saturn: Incase

of birth in Capricorn ascendant, the 9th Jord in a
Navamsa of Jupiter while Venus and Saturn are in
## Page 265

order in the Nadiamsas entitled Pramoda and Go-

issue of the family. His grand-father will attain good
worlds after death and will have an excellent rebirth.
The native’s father will be equal to a king and will
later on be reborn as a righteous person. Due to
mental distraction at the time of worship in the
present birth, the father will attain Heavens as a
martyr and be reborn as a king.

and rebirth as a king in consequence thereof are quite
inconsistent.

1858 - 18601/2, Capricorn Ascendant - Mar-
riage: (a) Saturn in Gopriya Nadiamsa as the Moon
is in“Paapaamsa Nadi” (should be Paasa Nadiamsa)
will cause marriage in Rahu bhukti of 2nd dasa.

(b) Saturn in Vargottama in Pisces will cause
marriage to the native of Libra ascendant (should be
Capricorn ascendant) in the 2nd dasa when Saturn
transits in Leo. The concerned month will be Pisces
(i.e.Sun moving in Pisces). Alternatively, itcould be
when Jupiter moves in the end of Pisces or in Aries,
as Saturn is retrograde. In this case, the months
concerned will coincide with Sun’s transit in Pisces
through Taurus.

249

Notes: (a) “Paapaamsa Nadige” refers to the
Nadiamsa so named, which is not enlisted. It should
be “Paasa” Nadiamsa. The Moon should be in this
Nadiamsa.

(b) “Makare LagnaJathake” is another version,
in place of “Thula Lagna Samudhbhavah’, referring
to Capricorn ascendant, which is only correct.

1861 - 1865. (a) Marriages: Two malefics inthe
6th will cause two marriages for the native of Capri-
corn ascendant, Gopriya Nadiamsa; Saturn in the
12th will cause three marriages.

(b) Fortunes & Progeny: Saturn in the 3rd in
Gopriya Nadiamsa will cause fortunes. The person
will have limited number of children to bis grief (i.e.
contrary to his desire of having many children) orwill
obtain dead children. According to other authorities,
with this position of Saturn, the subject will beget
sons and daughters due to the good deeds of his father.
Further he will have co-born equal to the number of
letters in the word “Gopriya” (i.e. three co-born) all
of whom. will be long-lived. So also he will have three
children and the rest will be destroyed.

1866 - 18691/2, Saturn’s Transit: (a) The native
of Gopriya Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascendant, will
incur evils inhis country when Saturn transits the sign
identical with the Navamsa occupied by the Moon or
a trine thereof. However, his father will gain wealth
through extensive business activities.

(b) Destruction of Grand-father: Saturnshould
at birth be placed in Gopriya Nadiamsa in case of
birth in Libra ascendant (“Capricorn” as per another
version, which is correct). Then when he transits Leo
during the second dasa, the person’s paternal grand-
father will be destroyed.

(c) Troubles to Father: During Satum’s transit
in Virgo, his father will face evils from his enemies
or from the king. ,

(d) Great danger to paternal uncle will come to
pass coificiding with adverse solar transit as Saturn
moves in Libra. In a trine thereof (i.e. in Aquarius/
Gemini) this transit of Saturn will cause the end of the
paternal uncle, and difficulties to the nearand dear of
the said relative. -

1870 - 1874. (a) Death of Relative: When
Satur moves in the sign occupied by Rahu at birth,
(or) in the sign which is the 6th in Navamsa, ora trine
thereof, a close relative of the subject will pass away. *

(b) Difficulties to Progeny: Note the sign which
is identical with the Navamsa occupied by the 12th

Chandra Kala Nadi

lord (Jupiter) at birth. Also the one that is aspected
by the 12th lord. When Saturn comics in transit to one
of these signs, ora trine thereto, his offspring will be
in for much trouble.

(c) Death of Father: Should Satu be in Gopriya
Nadiamsa, the person’s father will incurtimely death
during the fourth dasa. (The sub period seems to be
the first one as the term is unclear.)

(d) ness to Father: In the sub period of an
adverse planet during the dasa of the 8th lord (the
Sun), his father will incur fear from disease, for which
remedies should be resorted to. The person will lose
offspring then born, and will also acquire ailments.

1875 - 1878. (a) The person belonging to Gopriya
Nadiamsa, Capricorn ascendant, will in the first sub
period of the third dasa be prosperous.

(b) The 4th dasa will grant wide fame, and
enjoyment in royal service; one’s acquisition of
wealth will exceed ten thousand (gold coins) and he
will be endowed with uninterrupted wealth and hap-
piness.

(c) In the sub period of a malefic, in the dasa
which is the 4th in sequence, Saturn’s journey in
Cancer and Leo will destroy his wealth.

(d) In his first round of transit in Scorpio, Saturn
will to some extent contribute to the person’s fame,
but will trouble bis father with physical ailments.

(e) In Sagittarius, this planet will prove a source
of great trouble.

1879 - 1881. Irrelevant: Saturn coming to the
Rasi will cause troubles to the king, and due to a
revolt, to the people. Mars in the company of Rahu
in transit in the 4th or 10th from the Rasi of the
country will cause troubles to the people of the
respective country. If the said transit is in the Rasi of

These effects are from Sarva Nadi.

1882 - 1883. In the beginning and ending part of
the dasa of the 4th lord, in the sub period that will be
ruled by the lord of the 4th dasa, or in the 5th Jord’s
dasa, maternal family will be in great danger, and
maternal grand-father wil] face death. The native’s
father will attain increased prosperity and wealth.

Notes: The dasa periods denoted need some
clarifications. The dasa of Mars in its beginning and
concluding portions will cause danger in maternal
family. Second alternative is to note the planet that
will rule the 6th dasa and locate his sub period in the
dasa of Mars. Third alternative is the dasa of 5th lord
Venus.

Remember the gap between the dasa of Venus
and Mars. This warrants a judicious use of this
principle.

1884 - 1886. Capricorn ascendant - Gopriya
Nadiamsa: (a) Saturn should be in Vargottama as
Venus occupies the Aroodha ascendant. In this case
Saturn’s second round of transit (i.e. after he crosses
his natal position, or Moon’s natal positionas the case
may be) will give auspicious effects relating to
Lakshmi Yoga (i.e. acquisition of wealth). After the
age of 23, the person’s prosperity will increase by the
day.

(b) In case of Capricorn ascendant (“Mandabhe”
is to be treated as Capricorn ascendant, seeing the
flow of the text), Venus in the Sth (Taurus) and Saturn
in the 3rd (Pisces) will make one wealthy right from
birth till the end. He will be further famous, and
happy.

(c) Venus becoming the lord of the Aroodha
ascendant, will give plenty of quadmupeds, corns,
ornaments, and pleasures. The subject will construct
tanks and gardens.

Notes: (b) This yoga is on account of two
planets. One, Saturn in the 3rd in Pisces, and second,
Venus is in the 5th in Taurus. The yoga at “c” is
without reference to the position of Venus, but with
exclusive reference to Saturn in Pisces.

(c) The 2nd line of sloka 1886 - “Madhu Maase
Jhashe Mande Gopriyamsa Samudbhavah” - is in-
dicative of two things. First the birth should be in
Gopriya Nadiamsa, which meaning has already been
adopted. Another clue that is expelled from the
translation is Saturn in Pisces and the month of
Chaitra to disallow incoherent and incomplete in-
structions.

‘Venus will become the lord of Aroodha ascend-
ant, fora Capricorn native, if Saturn is in the 3rd in
Pisces. Thatis, the effects cited at“c” are for Saturn’s
placement in Pisces in case of Capricorn ascendant.
The importance is of course givento Venus ruling the
Aroodha ascendant.

1887 - 18921/2. (a) The results mentioned above
will occur in the sixth dasa.

(b) In the beginning and concluding portion of
the 2nd dasa, the person will enjoy fame and wealth.

(c) In the 4th dasa he will reap abundant business
gains.

(d) The subject belonging to Libra ascendant
(Capricorn as per another reading, which only is
correct) having Saturn in Pisces will undergo much
difficulties in old age. He will somewhat be grieved
on account of death of a son.

(e) (Without reference to planetary positions)
the death of the native of Gopriya Nadiamsa, Capri-
corn ascendant, will occur in the 62nd year with
transit Sun in Taurus, in a bright fortnight; on the
morning of a week day ruled bya malefic planet. He
will after death attain an excellent world. During the
47th year, in the last one third part of his full life span
(said to be 62 as above) he will incur fear of untimely
death for which remedies be done. His destiny in the
next world has been explained in the chapter relating
to “Para Loka” (inthe work consulted by the author).

(f) Saturn in Gopriya Nadiamsa (in Pisces) as
Ketu is in the 12th will send one to hell after death.
However in the present mundane journey he will be
somewhat happy. (“Bhooloka” is replaced by
“Bhooloke” in another version which means on the
earth, or in the present mundane journey).

1893 - 1894. Leo Ascendant - Bahu Dhanya
Nadiamsa: Birth in Leo ascendant with the Sun
therein in the Vaisya Kala of the subject Nadiamsa
(which is also known as Dhanya Nadiamsa) denotes
that the person belongs to traders’ community. His
mother will have a second name (will be known by
another name).

Notes: The Nadiamsa can be treated to be hous-
ing the Sun elsewhere. But seeing the expression
“Vaisyakala” it should be interpreted as above only.

Leo (“Bahudhanyaamsaka prajaatasya” is another
reading) with the Sun in the 11th (Gemini) with three
planets will make one wealthy right from birth.

(b) The Sun inthe 1 1th with Pisces Navamsa will
grant abundant wealth. He will be the Jonely child,
devoid ofany co-born. He will have much grains (i.e.
eating comforts) and paternal wealth.

(c) The Moon in Aries (in the 9th) with Taurms
Navamsa, (or) in the Nadiamsa entitled Paasa with
Martian aspect denotes that the subject is born due to
the mother’s worship of Lord Rama and Lord
Subrahmanya, the six-faced God (progeny of Lord
Siva).

1900 - 1906. Leo Ascendant: (a) The Moon in
aspect to Mars and being in the first half of Paasa
Nadiamsa denotes birth in traders’ community. The
native will be the eldest issue of the family.

(b) The Sun in Dhaanya Nadiamsa while the
Moon is in Paasa Nadiamsa will deprive the Leo
native of an after-born. He will be the lonely child,
be intelligent, will enjoy pleasures and will have a
body with black complexion. He will join many
women, be lustful and will suffer disorders caused by
heat as well as those of blood vessels.

(c) The 7th lord (Saturn) in aspect to Rahu while
Venus is in his exaltation Navamsa causes the follow-
ing. The subject will in his childhood take to bad
ways. He will join many women.

(d) The Moon in Aries (in the 9th) with Taurus
Navamsa will make him addicted to women and
wine.

(e) The Moon in aspect fo or in association with
Mars will cause diseases of blood vessels (through
infectious) sexual acts.

(f) The native of Dhaanya Nadiamsa will earn
over ten thousand (gold coins) with the 11th lord in
the 2nd inthe company of the lord ofthe 10th. Further

253

his paternal grand-father’s wealth will be available to
his father.

Notes: Paasa Nadiamsa - from 4° 48' to 5° 0' of
movable signs; from 25° 0' to 25° 12' of immovable
signs; and from 19° 48' to 20° 00' of common signs.

1907 - 19121/2. Father: (a) Incase of birth inLeo
ascendant, with the Nadiamsa entitled Dhaanya,
one’s father is described as under. He will be en-
dowed with gold, diamonds, quality jewels, wealth
and grains. He will be famous, be prone to urinary
disorders, devoid of co-born, big-bodied, big-bel-
lied, very righteous, fond of his wife (i.e. the native’s
mother), devoted to Lord Vishnu and Lord Siva,
timid, and irritable but be instantly pacifiable. He
will be engaged in the trade of clothes, be passionate
and be an intellectual.

(b) The Moon in exaltation as the 4th lord (Mars)
is in the 11th house (Gemini) in the company of three
benefics will cause wealth exceeding ten thousand
(gold coins) to the native’s father.

(c) Ketu in the 12th (Cancer) while his dispositor
(Moon) is with Mars and in aspect to or association
with Rahu denotes that the native’s father will de-
ceive his relatives, will have wealth earned by unfair
means, apart from having some wealth gathered
through somewhat fair means.

Nadiamsa, Leo ascendant, will be a person with good

1913 - 19171/2. (a) Jupiter in 11th: Jupiter
signifying paternal grand-father (ruler of 9th from
Oth, i.e. Sth, .vbich is Sagittarius) being in the 11th
(Gemini) with Aquarius Navamsa will cause pros-
perity to paternal grand-uncle. Also the native’s
father will be endowed with co-born.

(b) Paternal Grand-uncle Described: The Sun
in the 11th (Gemini) in Dhaanya Nadiamsa while
Venus is also in Dhaanya Nadiamsa will lead to the
following effects concerning the person’s paternal
grand-uncle. He would have two brothers and two
sisters, be passionate and skillful in acquisition of
money. During his childhood days, his happiness
would be limited. He would be lustful. Due to
absence ofa male child, he would turn righteous. He
would have daughters, be famous and honoured in
reyal circles. He would befriend those who steal
gold, would earn money through deals in precious
stones, would construct tanks and parks, be fond of
Vaishnava Brahmins, be somewhat faithful to Vedic
injunctions and would bring up his co-borns. He
would suffer from urinary diseases, be a pleased soul,
be passionately fond of (receiving) charity, be kind to

Chandra Kala Nadi

others.

Notes: (a) Jupiter in Gemini 13° 20' to 16° 40!
begets Aquarius Navamsa. Apart from causing wealth
to a paternal relative, Jupiter here is said to give no
coborn to the native’s father. The 1 1this 3rd from 9th
and hence is involved in this regard.

(b) This portion describes the various events in
the life of the native’s paternal grand-father’s brother.
In sloka 1916, the term “Putrabhaavaath” meaning
“from the Putra Bhava, i.e. 5th house” should read as
“Putraabhaavaath” = Putra + Aabhaavaath, mean-
ing due to absence of male issue.

1918 - 1921 1/2. (a) Paternal Grand-father:
The Sun in the 11th in Dhaanya Nadiamsa would
bring fame to the said relative (to the native’s paternal
grand-father) through his brother. He would have
two brothers and be worshipped. His mother-in-law
will somewhat live for a long time. She will incur
grief on account of a son and a brother, be a devout
spouse, would have one son, two according to some
authorities, and would obtain dead children. She
would have a long marital life (long-lived husband).
According to some, the native’s paternal grand-
father will have two sisters who would beget dead
children.

(b) Mother: The Sun in the 11th in Dhaanya
Nadiamsa (ascited above) would give many sisters to
the native’s mother. ‘The native will have two
mothers (i.e. will have a step mother), be passionate,
and be inauspicious for one of his maternal uncles.

1922 - 19241/2. Maternal Aunts: (a) The native
of Leo ascendant having Saturn in the 12th in aspect
to Rahu, and being in Aquarius Navamsa, will con-
tribute to longevity to the native’s mother. She will
grieve on account of loss of her brother. She will have
three sisters, the middle one of whom will have a
long-living husband. Rest will be destroyed. These
are the effects described for the sisters of the native’s
mother.

(b) The Sunin Dhaanya Nadiamsa (inthe 11thin
Gemini) wil] give an adopted son to the sister of the
native’s mother.

Notes: (a) The Navamsa position prescribed is
for Saturnin Cancer. Saturnshould be in Cancer from
23° 20' to 26° 40' and in aspect to Rahu.

1925 - 1936. (a) Father’s Health: Saturn in the
4th (Scorpio) while his dispositor Mars is associated
‘with Rahu by aspect or conjunction will make the
father a synonym of diseases and will give him much
difficulties thereby.

(b) The Moon in Paasa Nadiamsa being in asso-
ciation with Mars would cause (dangerous) fever to
paternal grand-father who would be troubled by
excessive urination. Alternatively, his body would
emit bad smell and in its entirety be inflicted by
ulcers. To overcome this blemish, suitable remedies
be resorted to.

(c) The Sun in the 6th, with a benefic, and being
in 6th in Navamsa will cause obstructed urinationand
other urinary disorders to the native’s father. To
remove these illnesses of the father, one should
donate “Roga Moorthy”. (This obviously hints ata
deity, as described below, who should be pacified.)
The ido] made of sulfur should be of the following
description: Adoring a lotus in the navel (Damodara
does not refer to Vishnu, in this context), having a

‘long physique, bloody face, bloody eyes, six eyes,

three heads, horrible teeth, standing on a corpse,
holding a noose and axe, brandishing destructive fire
(“Kapalagni” reads as “Kalagni”), adoring food
soaked inblood, resemblinga male, and wearing hair
and bones that were cast off. Such an idol should be
worshipped and donated. Itshould be offered gingilee,
scents, (uncooked) yellow rice particles, flowers and
sacred water. Spending about ten gold coins, the
above worship be done. If the idol, three times of the
usual size, is installed in the southern direction
prosperity will result. Whatever diseases are there in
the father’s body will all disappear and instant recov-
ery will come to pass. The idol should be given away
## Page 272

256

with the recitation of “Saanthim Dehi, Sukham Dehi
Twaarogyam Dehi Me Sadaa Aayurbalam Cha
Kaanthim DehiMeSarvaSampadah’ (seeking peace,
happiness, health, life-span, vigour, splendour and
all kinds of wealth in exchange of the whole ritual).

Notes: (a) The adjective “Vyaapya” relating to
diseases of father conveys incurable diseases that
will remain throughout his life in such a manner as
inseparable fire and heat. Thus the father of the
native will perpetually be unhealthy.

For remedy to overcome to this blemish, also
refer to sloka 1940 infra.

1937 - 19401/2. Father’s illness: The Sun in
Dhaanya Nadiamsa while Saturn is in the 4th house
could be propitiated by donating pots of honey and
ghee following which father’s illnesses will be de-
stroyed. A hundred thousand recitations of
Mnityunjaya Mantra followed by Havana (sacred
fire) with another ten thousand, Tarpana (offer of
Pinda to dead ancestors), and feeding of Brahmanas
in the end will bring happiness (i.e. relief to father).
After concluding the Homa, the planets Saturn and
Mars (vide sloka 1925) should be propitiated which
will grant health and longevity to father. Worship of
single-footed zodiac and charities will cause health
to father, warding off the blemish of untimely death.

Taurus Navamsa, will give the following effects in
case of birth in Leo ascendant. The person will spend
on undeserving counts, be lustful, will after some
interval turn righteous and will have multifarious
business activities.

perform sinful acts during the rulership of his second
dasa, if the Moon is in Paasa Nadiamsa. He will

his financial progress will be marked. In the dasa of
the lord of the ascendant, he will have uninterrupted
riches.

1969 - 1970. (a) The Moon’s Dasa: Should the
Moon at birth be in the company of 9th lord (Mars),
then the dasa of the Moon when 4th in sequence will
cause acquisition of fortunes, and a marriage in the
family. However in this dasa children born to the
subject will be destroyed much to his trouble.

(b) The junction phases ofall the dasas will give
much troubles.

Notes: (a) The Moon should be in Aswini or
Makha or Moola, ina trine from the ascendant along
with Mars for the Yoga to give fruits.

1972 - 1977. (a) Troubles from Cats & Rats: The
planet Ketu should be in 12th (Cancer) while his
dispositor joins Mars (elsewhere). As a result, the
native will be troubled by cats, rats and poisonous
fevers. The effects stated forthe 4th dasa will be true;
for overcoming the evils effects concerned, suitable
remedies be done.

or from the Moon sign will endanger the mother of the
native of Dhaanya Nadiamsa. Alternatively his
paternal grand-father will die in the sub period of
Mercury or of Ketu, during the rulership of thc 2nd
dasa. A maternal uncle will lose his son. In the sub
period of Mercury, there will be a family marriage,
and much happiness (on other accounts).

1993 - 1994 1/2. The Moon in the company of the
4th lord (Mars) in Paasa Nadiamsa will cause his next
birth intraders’ community. This yoga indicates that
in the previous birth also the person had belonged to
the same community. These are the effects for the
native and his father. Due to the good deeds, his
father will have three lucky births. The native’s
father after his death, will be reborn to the very loins
of the present native.

Notes: This relates to only Bahudhaanya
Nadiamsa, Leo ascendant. The Nadiamsa referred to
in the text is for the Moon’s positionalthough a literal
translation would mean birth in Paasa Nadiamsa.

1995 - 1997. If the Sun is in Dhaanya Nadiamsa
(elsewhere) while Ketu is in the 12th (Cancer), and
the Moon is with Mars, the native’s father will dwell
fora long time in other worlds including the hell (i.e.
will not take rebirth immediately). Due to the good
deeds father will enjoy prosperity in the whole of his
life (in the current birth). With Ketu inthe 12th, grief
to father on account of loss cf a son in old age will
come to pass. The effects for the Sun’s position (and
birth) in Bahudhaanya Nadiamsa are from the work
entitled “Surya Nadt”.
